Chapter 552: Spacetime Passage

The Epoch Immortal appeared extremely young, looking about Lu Yang’s age. Among the Five Ancient Immortals, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy ranked first in vitality, while the Epoch Immortal came second. His innate foundation far surpassed that of other immortals.

When the Epoch Immortal arrived at the immortal domain and saw the haphazard Five in a Row pieces scattered across the board, his eyelid twitched, and he nearly flipped the chessboard. You three are something else, abandoning me to suffer alone while you run off here to enjoy yourselves.

Then, he sensed an anomaly in the immortal domain, particularly the aura of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy from the future. He inhaled sharply as he shuddered from the lingering fear.

“Fortunately, I didn’t bring ███ over. Never in history has an immortal from the past and future gazed upon each other across time, especially not ███, who wields ████. I’m afraid a great annihilation would occur the moment they meet, overturning both past and future!” Even the Epoch Immortal couldn’t predict what would happen if two Everlasting Immortal Fairies met. He had theorized a highly probable outcome, though it was also possible that nothing would happen and that the two could even chat amiably. freewebnovel.com

But who would dare gamble on such a possibility?

If a great annihilation is triggered, losing the gamble would mean it’s game over for everyone.

The Epoch Immortal bit his finger, revealing the golden blood flowing within. He closed his eyes and painted an immortal eye between his brows with the immortal blood.

The third eye opened, golden and hollow, like a blind man’s gaze. But in truth, it was because this immortal eye’s gaze wasn’t on the present but the future. He could faintly discern a graceful figure standing in this immortal domain in some distant future, but he couldn’t make out her features.

“There’s severe interference!

“Hmm? Who’s this?”

He sensed another presence beside the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. But this person is too weak to be qualified to appear before me across space and time. Yet I can detect a small piece of Jianwu wood–a part of my body—hanging in front of this person’s chest.

Did my future self trust him so much to give him a piece of Jianmu wood as proof? Or was my future self sealed away, and he sent this little cultivator to find the Everlasting Immortal? The Epoch Immortal frowned, keeping his speculations to himself.

“Well? What did ███ say?” the Nine-Layers Immortal pressed urgently.

The Epoch Immortal shook his head. “Not enough. The Spacetime Immortal Eye alone is still not enough.” The Spacetime Immortal Eye was an immortal eye he had refined with his Epoch Dao Fruit. It had never failed him—until now.

“Is it because the distance is too long, or is something in between interfering?”

Without hesitation, the Epoch Immortal summoned his Epoch Dao Fruit, which was woven with boundless laws of spacetime. It swayed up and down gently, as if it was floating on the ocean of time and generating ripples of time.

“Don’t look.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy covered Lu Yang’s eyes just before the Epoch Dao Fruit fully materialized.

The Epoch Dao Fruit was the ultimate form of spacetime rules. Let alone a Golden Core cultivator like Lu Yang, even a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator would lose their insanity at a single glance, their mind clouded from the influence of the Dao Fruit.

The Epoch Dao Fruit encompassed too much; cultivators couldn’t withstand such an influx of information. Their spirit platform would crumble under its torrent.

With the Dao Fruit’s aid, the Epoch Immortal finally glimpsed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s face clearly. The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the other two immortals also saw her through the time passage constructed.

Before the Epoch Immortal could rejoice, cold sweat broke out on his forehead, and he yelled, “Oh no! The spacetime passage can’t last much longer!”

Among everyone present, he sensed it most acutely. It’s as though some entity has severed the temporal channel between me and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. No, more precisely, something has cut off the connection between my era and the future!

What could it be?

“███, what were you trying to say?!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also realized the danger and blurted out, “I was assassinated—”

Boom!

The channel shattered. Under some unfathomable force, the spacetime passage collapsed, breaking off all connection between both parties.

The Epoch Immortal staggered two steps back and was steadied by the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Qilin Immortal.

“Are you alright?”

Shaking his head, the Epoch Immortal stabilized his breathing and activated the Epoch Dao Fruit. In the blink of an eye, he had recovered fully. “It’s not a big problem.” Besides, my condition is the last of our concerns now. He swept his gaze across the group, his voice icy. “You all heard what Everlasting said just now, right?”

“Assassinated...? What kind of joke is that? That’s impossible!” The Qilin Immortal crushed a chess piece in his grip, his eyes filled with disbelief. “Of the five of us, it’s the hardest for Everlasting to die. Anyone can resurrect her just by speaking her name. What method could possibly kill her?”

However, the truth lay bare before them; they had to believe it even if they weren’t willing to. Everlasting loves mischief, but she’d never joke about something like this.

They had considered that the future Everlasting Immortal Fairy had run into some trouble requiring their assistance, but they reckoned the worst scenario was that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was sealed and needed them to remove the seal. Never had they imagined that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would be killed.

If the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could be resurrected easily, she wouldn’t have mentioned this matter. This implied that in the future, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy not only perished, but also could not be revived!

“Didn’t you hear? It was an assassination. Perhaps there is some method beyond our imagination that could prevent her resurrection.” The Heaven Mandate Immortal tapped the table.

“She said she was assassinated but didn’t mention the culprit. Does this mean that even Everlasting doesn’t know who did it?”

The four pondered. Could the Everlasting Immortal Fairy have known the culprit was among us and withheld the information for fear of exposing their identity?

They quickly eliminated this possibility. Given their trust in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, if she had named the culprit, the other three would have attacked without question. How could three not take down one culprit? That was impossible.

Someone had assassinated the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, but she doesn’t know who it is.

“How far away is Everlasting?” the Heaven Mandate Immortal asked. Pinpointing the time will allow us to make preparations.

“I can’t be certain. The passageway collapsed too quickly. But it’s definitely at least ten thousand years in the future.”

“Why did the spacetime passage crumble?” The Nine-Layers Immortal frowned. Had the channel remained, we could have gleaned more information. At the minimum, confirming the exact timeframe would have been good.

The Epoch Immortal’s face turned ashen. “Two reasons. First, space and time have a corrective trait—future information can’t be transmitted to the past, for this will result in temporal and spatial chaos. With my Epoch Dao Fruit, this problem becomes manageable. But the second reason is critical.

“Something has affected the stability of space and time, severing our connection to Everlasting’s future!”

“What could be more powerful than your Epoch Dao Fruit?”

The Epoch Immortal snorted coldly, displeased with the Qilin Immortal’s remark. “It’s not more powerful than my Epoch Dao Fruit! I’ve simply focused on using the Epoch Dao Fruit to deal with the self-correcting nature of spacetime and have no extra energy to pay attention to that thing!”

“What thing could have influenced space and time?”

“Not sure. But anything that could clash with my Epoch Dao Fruit head-on must be another Dao Fruit!”

“And the most important question—why didn’t our future selves resurrect Everlasting?”

Chapter 553: The Four Immortals’ Analysis

“Why didn’t our future selves resurrect Everlasting?”

At the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s question, the four immortals in the immortal domain fell silent.

Indeed, this is the biggest problem. Even if others couldn’t revive the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, couldn’t any one of us do it? It’s just speaking her name—who could possibly stop us?

“It’s not just Everlasting. Something might have happened to all four of us!” the Nine-Layers Immortal stated coldly. This is the only plausible explanation.

Although this answered the previous question, an even greater question now confronted the four immortals. What exactly had happened that even trouble befell the Five Ancient Immortals?

“It can’t be that all four of us were also no more, right?” the Qilin Immortal blurted, the thought sending chills down his own spine. After all, if even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had perished, it was theoretically possible that the four of them were eliminated.

“That’s the worst-case scenario, but it’s unlikely,” the Epoch Immortal analyzed, shaking his head. “Everlasting was assassinated, meaning the killer might be weaker than her or only slightly stronger, but not enough to overwhelm her. Under such circumstances, as long as the four of us were united, that culprit in the dark probably wouldn’t have killed all of us.”

“By the way, Epoch, since you said the culprit had used a Dao Fruit to sever our connection to the future, can you determine how distant this future is?” reewebnovel.com

The Epoch Immortal furrowed his brows. “I can try, but the probability of success is low. Give me a moment.”

Activating his Epoch Dao Fruit again, primal hundun energies surged as his true form transcended spacetime and gazed upon it. However, the future was clear with no signs of obstruction.

“Well, how is it?”

“As I predicted, it doesn’t work. The future appears too clear.”

“What about the severance you mentioned?”

The Epoch Immortal looked at the Qilin Immortal like the latter was an idiot. “This is what happens when you don’t listen to my lectures during our gatherings.”

The Qilin Immortal bristled. As the Epoch Immortal had used his Epoch Dao Fruit to mess with the Qilin Immortal twice, the Qilin Immortal was no longer scared of the Epoch Immortal’s methods. You really think I can’t beat you?

Despite the Epoch Immortal’s sarcasm, he explained, “The future is indeterminate. The future I see is merely the most probable scenario. The closer the future is, the higher the probability; likewise, the further it is, the lower the probability.

“Assuming the future I saw is ‘Future A,’ the most probable future, it’s where Everlasting wasn’t assassinated. However, ‘Future B’ is where Everlasting was assassinated. Earlier, when I was speaking to Everlasting, my Epoch Dao Fruit established a connection with Future B. The so-called ‘severance’ cut off my link to Future B, but not to futures A, C, and D.”

“Does that mean Everlasting wasn’t necessarily assassinated?”

“No, the future is a straight line and has no bifurcations. Everlasting will certainly be assassinated. However, from the Epoch Dao Fruit’s perspective, this probability is so small that it’s unobservable. Only after I’ve refined my Epoch Dao Fruit to perceive all future possibilities can I pinpoint the severed point in time.”

Although this avenue of the Epoch Immortal wasn’t workable, the immortals didn’t lose heart and pressed on undeterred.

“Only an immortal can injure an immortal. Since the culprit could assassinate Everlasting, they must be an immortal. Are there other immortals besides us five?”

The Nine-Layers was the most qualified to speak on such matters. “According to my research, I was the first to become an immortal, followed by you four. Everlasting was last. There’s no sixth immortal.”

“In that case, there are two possibilities regarding the assassin.” The Heaven Mandate Immortal raised two fingers.

“One: someone of extraordinary talent ascends in the future.

“Second: the five of us aren’t the only immortals—there’s a sixth immortal!”

His theory stunned them all.

“That’s impossible! The unusual phenomena during immortal ascension are terrifying. How could a sixth person have concealed it?!” Everyone had endured immortal tribulations themselves. They were cataclysmic, and even blind individuals could perceive their presence. There was no way someone could have hidden it.

“An immortal ascension tribulation indeed can’t be concealed. But what if the other party had formed Dao Fruits like the Karma Dao Fruit or the Destiny Dao Fruit to conceal their existence? That’s totally possible!”

Through self-concealment and self-oblivion, one would forget the terrifying immortal ascension tribulation. An immortal wielding the Karma Dao Fruit couldn’t rise above immortals, but that didn’t signify they couldn’t become immortals.

“This also explains the severance the Epoch Immortal mentioned. Employing the Karma Dao Fruit had cut off the karma between now and the future.

“Alternatively, the Destiny Dao Fruit had blocked off Huang Doudou’s destiny of survival, rewriting it from life to death. If we know too much about the future, Huang Doudou’s destiny of demise would be affected, so the severance emerged to prevent us from learning too much!”

“Even then, there are many other Dao Fruits we don’t understand. The possibilities are countless.”

In truth, their understanding of the Karma Dao Fruit and the Destiny Dao Fruit remained theoretical. Until a complete Dao Fruit was condensed, its true power remained unknown.

For example, when the Everlasting Dao Fruit was in its incipient phase, Huang Doudou had only used it to repair her state or dart around in statues. No one could imagine that after the Everlasting Dao Fruit was fully condensed, Huang Doudou could self-detonate wherever and whenever she wanted, and that she could revive as long as someone uttered her name.

“Perhaps a third possibility regarding the assassin exists. Though I can’t think of it now.” The Heaven Mandate Immortal shrugged. Coming up with two possibilities in such a short time is truly not easy.

The other three immortals also shook their heads, drawing a blank.

“Should we tell Everlasting about this?” the Qilin Immortal asked.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Epoch Immortal pondered the feasibility.

“Absolutely not!” The Nine-Layers Immortal was the first to veto it. “Based on Everlasting’s personality, if she knows she’ll be assassinated in the future, she might say, ‘If I kill myself, I can’t be assassinated,’ and promptly commit suicide on the spot, waiting to resurrect in the future! Who knows what other madness she’d attempt?!”

The Qilin Immortal, “...”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal, “...”

The Epoch Immortal, “...”

That does sound like Huang Doudou’s style.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal stretched lazily. “Let’s prepare slowly. From the looks of it, I think Everlasting will be fine for a while. Epoch, you came out on the pretense of being a referee. It’s about time you return. Otherwise, she’ll grow suspicious, and it’ll be terrible if she comes looking for us.”

At the thought of the meals cooked by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and the Qilin Immortal’s two wives, the Epoch Immortal contemplated mutual destruction. “Fine then, who can I blame for being unlucky?” The Epoch Immortal sighed, resigned to drag himself back to the North Star.

“By the way, it’ll probably take the three of you a century to finish this chess game. That will definitely form a historical projection. Erase this segment where we glimpsed the future Everlasting. If the assassin sees the historical projection, wouldn’t it expose the fact that Everlasting can still be resurrected?”

“You’re still as devious as ever.” The Heaven Mandate Immortal gave him a thumbs-up.

“This is called being meticulous!” The Epoch Immortal fumed.

Chapter 554: Conclusion of the Immortal Sect Exchange

The Epoch Immortal returned to the North Star, only to find the commotion caused by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and the dragon and phoenix prodigies growing increasingly alarming, making his heart race.

“Epoch, you’re back? How are Qilin and Heaven Mandate?”

The Epoch Immortal said solemnly, “It was the Heaven Mandate Immortal, that lousy chess player, who was cheating. I taught him a lesson. After that, they continued playing chess. When I left, both he and Qilin entered a state of enlightenment, as if they had discerned the five elements, bagua, heaven and earth, and yin and yang within the Five in a Row game!

“Since the Nine-Layers Immortal is the creator of Five in a Row, he is guarding them, so I came back first.”

“Eh, those two had such a fortuitous opportunity? Perfect timing, I’ll whip up something nourishing for them!”

Watching the Everlasting Immortal Fairy bustle about, the Epoch Immortal kindly reminded her, “Heaven Mandate especially needs extra replenishment. His enlightenment seemed particularly profound; he’ll need the largest dose!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied loudly, “Say no more! This is my specialty!” She rolled up her sleeves and tightened her headscarf, unleashing her full power.

Soon, the agonized wails of ingredients filled the air.

The Epoch Immortal smirked coldly. Heaven Mandate, who told you to call me ‘devious?’ Let’s see you survive this poisoning!

~~~

“So this is the immortals’ chess game? I feel like I can’t discern anything,” Meng Jingzhou muttered. He examined the chessboard from every angle but failed to pick up on the arcane wonders hidden by the two ancient immortals.

Tao Yaoye and Man Gu reacted similarly, utterly baffled.

Nonsense, Qiu Jin’an thought. Despite a hundred thousand years, our Five-Elements Sect hasn’t produced a second person who can perceive the historical projection. Did you expect to waltz in and see it immediately?

Lu Yang even yawned from boredom. Having just awakened from witnessing the historical projection, his mind was exhausted. For a moment, he couldn’t even distinguish where he currently was.

Before the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s group noticed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Lu Yang had watched twenty years’ worth of chess, though the process was accelerated by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Even so, the mental toll had been tremendous, not to mention that he had confronted the Four Ancient Immortals through the spacetime passage, bridging the past, present, and future.

Qiu Jin’an noticed Lu Yang’s behavior but didn’t dwell on it. Our founding ancestor immersed himself in the historical projection for a century—completely different from Lu Yang.

To outsiders, Lu Yang had merely lowered his head and yawned—a span of two to three breaths. No one would suspect he had viewed the historical projection. Though it was only because he had borrowed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s prestige.

After fifteen minutes, Qiu Jin’an asked cheerfully, “Finished viewing?” As I thought, nothing happened. The youngsters are just here for novelty’s sake.

Everyone sighed collectively. They had hoped to encounter immortal opportunities, or at least get a glimpse of immortals.

In the end, there was nothing.

“Immortal Fairy, wasn’t the message you sent too brief?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had only transmitted five words before the passageway closed due to unknown reasons. Lu Yang was worried their communication hadn’t worked.

“Rest assured. While those four’s intelligence falls short of mine, it still surpasses that of ordinary people. They’ll definitely deduce something and leave behind hidden measures.

“However, I still died. Their hidden measures probably weren’t meant for me but something else.”

“As long as it’s effective.”

Although he was privy to much of the Four Ancient Immortals’ dark history, enough to get himself killed easily, and the Qilin Immortal had even tricked him into eating dirt, Lu Yang still hoped the Four Ancient Immortals survived.

Li Haoran’s expression flickered in a daze. Gazing at the chessboard earlier, he had suddenly dozed off. In his hazy vision, he saw four figures in the immortal domain wielding heaven-defying power and dared not face them directly.

Then he woke up, blinking rapidly. “A dream?”

He struggled to recall the events in his dream and who the four figures were, but the memory grew blurry the more he tried to remember. “What just happened?” Li Haoran’s brows were knitted. He couldn’t help but sense something had transpired, yet upon closer thought, it seemed nothing had happened.

The group departed the immortal domain, unaware that a figure sat motionless atop the mountain summit like a statue. The figure lifted an eyelid, watching the group leave before drifting down and entering the immortal domain.

Finding the immortal domain unchanged, the figure’s eyes contained a trace of bewilderment.

“Strange. Did I see it wrong? Why does it feel like someone saw the historical projection just now?”

The figure shook their head and tossed this matter to the back of their mind.

It should be a figment of my imagination. How could someone access the historical projection without being immersed in it?

~~~

A month passed in the blink of an eye. Lu Yang’s group had gained much from their stay in the Five-Elements Sect—standing in position according to the five elements, cultivating at the grounds of the Five Branches, clearing their meridians, and organizing everything they had learned in this month.

Lu Yang cultivated at the Metal Branch and advanced from the Advanced Golden Core’s first layer to the second layer’s great perfection apex—a significant improvement in cultivation realm.

“Fellow Daoist Bai Ming, until we meet again in the jianghu!” Lu Yang and the others waved vigorously from their flying vessel.

The entire Five-Elements Sect turned up to see them off.

~~~

At the Dao-Seeking Sect’s breeding farm, sonorous Buddhist sounds reverberated through the air as the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed swayed their heads and chanted.

“Within the primordial azure skies in times bygone, the blue firmament echoes vacant hymns, the vast floating land...”

After nearly a month of immersion in Buddhist teachings, they were no longer the same as they were before, especially the Everlasting Immortal, whose comprehension of Buddhist spells progressed by leaps and bounds. Had he not restrained himself, golden light would have radiated from his body.

“Benefactor Bu, your affinity with Buddhism runs deep. In time, you may even be able to join our Hanging Monastery.”

“You flatter me. All credit goes to your teaching, Little Master.”

The Everlasting Immortal and Shi Chan exchanged bows.

“Alas, my time here is up. This little monk must return to the slaughterhouse and comprehend the path of setting down the butcher’s knife and attaining Buddhahood on the spot.” Shi Chan sighed regretfully.

He and the Everlasting Immortal had bonded instantly, wishing they had met each other earlier. The Everlasting Immortal agreed with many of Shi Chan’s views. He’s much more open-minded than Shifu.

This is a benefactor with great wisdom!

Meeting Benefactor Bu alone made this trip to the Dao-Seeking Sect worthwhile! freewebnovel.com

Under the influence of Buddhist teachings, the three Alluring Ghosts had smoothly advanced to the Golden Core Stage.

This was only natural. Although the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups had been refined into tiger-henchman ghosts and denied cultivation resources, casual advice from them could overturn the three female ghosts’ understanding of cultivation; they wouldn’t even need cultivation resources. Combined with Shi Chan’s teachings, their souls underwent metamorphosis, and the progression to the Golden Core Stage automatically followed.

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s disciples felt that the flavor of the barbeque skewers had improved this past month.

Slaughtering livestock would inevitably transfer their lingering resentment into the meat. While true fire could drive it away, its effectiveness still paled to that of Buddhist methods. The creed leader and Vice Creed Leader Jin would chant Buddhist scriptures to dispel the resentful energy.

The Everlasting Immortal was over the moon when he discovered this method. “This is a great idea! I’ll find a chance to suggest it to the second-in-command and see if we can implement this chainwide!” This is proof of our active labor reform.

“Junior Brother Shi Chan, visit again when you get the chance. If there’s anything you need, I will make sure to fulfill it.” Dai Bufan personally saw Shi Chan off.

Learning his shifu was still alive, he firmly believed his virtuous conduct had reached Master Jiesha across space and moved him, thus saving his shifu’s life.

Shi Chan did have something he needed help with. “Senior Brother Dai, could you lend me some travel funds?”

Chapter 555: Clues of the Epoch Immortal

Numerous clouds drifted by. First Elder exhaled in relief as he got closer to the Dao-Seeking Sect. “At last, safely back at the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Although the journey from being captured by the Hanging Monastery to this safe return to the Dao-Seeking Sect had been circuitous, living to return is good enough.

~~~

“Junior Brother Shi Chan, I don’t think you’ll need travel funds.”

“Ah? Why?” Senior Brother Dai looks like a kind person. Would he really bear to make me walk back alone?

“Your sect has come for you,” Dai Bufan said impassively, looking past Shi Chan at the approaching group of monks.

Turning around, Shi Chan saw it was indeed his shifu, senior uncle, and senior brothers. The Buddhist light they radiated was so resplendent it hurt the eyes. His senior uncle, Custodian Monk Jiechen, carried someone by the collar. With their profound cultivation, the Hanging Monastery members crossed a hundred meters per step, arriving at the Dao-Seeking Sect’s mountain gates immediately.

“Senior Uncle Jiechen, why are you here?” Shi Chan was stunned. I didn’t hear anything about them coming to fetch me. Although his shifu Jiesha was present, considering his shifu’s inability to speak for a long while, Shi Chan figured questioning him would be futile—he might as well ask his senior uncle.

“Performing a daily good deed by setting a captive life free.” Master Jiechen shoved his captive toward the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Shifu, are you alright?” Dai Bufan asked First Elder with a peculiar expression.

First Elder waved his hand, gesturing for Dai Bufan not to worry about him. “It’s merely an exchange between sects’ higher-ups. Why wouldn’t I be alright?”

Dai Bufan, “...”

Master Jiechen beckoned Shi Chan over. “Many thanks for your care this past month, Junior Nephew Dai.” Master Jiechen nodded in gratitude.

“You’re too polite, Senior Uncle.” Dai Bufan bowed in return.

~~~

As the Hanging Monastery entourage departed with Shi Chan, the latter kept his head drooped in dejection. It seems I won’t be able to continue working in the slaughterhouse anymore.

“Shi Chan, what did you gain from the Dao-Seeking Sect?” Master Jiechen asked genially. True to his name, which meant “abstaining from anger,” he always wore an affable smile.

“I've gained plenty! The Dao-Seeking Sect abounds with experts. I met many who share my ideologies! But most importantly, I’ve verified that what Shifu said isn’t wrong. The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s eldest disciple is indeed not easy to deal with.”

“That’s a given. Your shifu wouldn’t deceive you. The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s eldest disciple is indeed not easy to deal with... Wait, what did you say?”

“Didn’t Shifu say the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s eldest disciple is extremely formidable and shouldn’t be provoked? I felt that learning it on paper is ultimately shallow and that one must personally take action, so I went to Heaven’s Gate Peak to challenge Senior Yun Zhi. Needless to say, I couldn’t beat her.” Shi Chan’s body ached at the memory, shuddering in lingering fear. Senior Yun Zhi is really powerful.

Hearing what his dear disciple had done, Master Jiesha wobbled mid-flight, nearly plummeting. He wished he could curse out loud, but since he was still cultivating the Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation, he could only confine the outburst to his thoughts.

~~~

“We’re back!” Lu Yang’s group of five returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Nothing compares to the warmth of one’s own sect. Look at Senior Brother Dai and First Elder personally receiving us at the gates.

“It’s been hard on you, First Elder, Senior Brother Dai. I must look for Big Senior Sister, so I’ll take my leave first.” With that, Lu Yang vanished before the bewildered group.

“What’s this kid’s hurry?”

“No idea.”

Lu Yang was naturally in a hurry. Setting aside the plethora of things he had learned from his stay at the Five-Elements Sect, he needed to consult with Yun Zhi regarding the ancient matters he had uncovered.

~~~

At Heaven’s Gate Peak, Yun Zhi sat in a half-lotus position, one foot touching the ground while the other rested on the opposite thigh. She held two golden cores between her fingers in a flower-pinching mudra, her breathing drawn out and synchronized with nature, making her presence nearly imperceptible.

Before Lu Yang could speak, Yun Zhi’s eyes opened slowly. “Little Junior Brother, what brings you here in such haste?” Rising, she flicked the golden cores skyward, where they streaked like meteors before suspending high above.

Lu Yang watched, eyes wide, mouth agape.

Noting his shock, Yun Zhi explained offhandedly, “A month ago, someone came to challenge me, requesting I suppress my cultivation to the Advanced Golden Core Stage. I agreed to his terms and plucked two golden cores from the sky to temporarily suppress my cultivation realm. Afterward, I thought since this is a rare opportunity, I might as well refine them further. Now that I’ve finished, I can return them to their original positions.”

Lu Yang’s eye twitched. Some things are better left unexplained.

“Where did you obtain this wooden tablet?” Yun Zhi hooked her finger, summoning the Jianmu wood fragment around Lu Yang’s neck toward her and dragging him along with it.

Yun Zhi examined the Jianmu wood at close range. This unprecedented proximity to Yun Zhi flustered Lu Yang. He could even feel her breath.

“A fragment of immortal wood?” Yun Zhi’s eyebrow arched as she released Lu Yang. This is extremely precious. How did Lu Yang acquire it?

“That’s what I wanted to report! This is a part of the Jianmu World Tree. Shangguan-jiejie gave this to me!”

“A part of the Jianmu World Tree? The Epoch Immortal?” Yun Zhi was taken aback. So Senior Shangguan possesses clues about the Epoch Immortal? Or perhaps she recognized its value without knowing its origins, so she decided to form friendly ties with Lu Yang for good karma?

“It’s better that I explain,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy interjected. “When Lu Yang and I went to the Five-Elements Sect’s Wood Branch, I discovered it was brimming with astonishing vitality. After noticing the protective charm Lass Shangguan gave Lu Yang, I scanned the entire Wood Branch with my immortal consciousness and found this.” With her consciousness, she recreated the image of the Epoch Immortal’s corpse buried beneath the Wood Branch.

“This is...”

“The Epoch Immortal’s corpse.”

Yun Zhi’s eyes widened slightly at this revelation. Although she had visited the Five-Elements Sect, she hadn’t used her spiritual consciousness to scan the area beneath the Wood Branch out of propriety. Who could have imagined an immortal corpse was actually buried beneath the Five-Elements Sect?!

“The Epoch Immortal perished? No, we can’t make any judgment with just a corpse. Senior, I have something I’d like to check with you. The ancient texts state that the Nian Year Beast[1] is the Epoch Immortal’s familiar. Is this true?”

“It is. The Nian Year Beast is a demon beast that the Epoch Immortal cultivated with the Epoch Dao Fruit.”

“That sounds correct then. Every New Year, the Nian Year Beast is active, but shortly after, it disappears. Once, I tried to intervene to track where it went, but I used too much force and startled the Nian Year Beast. From then on, it flees at the sight of me.”

Mortals, with their brief lifespans, cherished each year. For cultivators with long lifespans, a year passed in a blink. In the cultivation world, the custom was to celebrate the New Year every ten years, and the Nian Year Beast similarly appeared once a decade. Ever since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s revival, she had yet to experience a New Year in the cultivation world.

“What I can determine is that every New Year, the Nian Year Beast comes from the east and returns to the west. Thus, I suspected clues of the Epoch Immortal lay in the East Sea or the Buddhist Kingdom. That was why I sent Second Junior Brother to roam the west more.”

1. It’s said that the firecrackers during the Chinese New Year are meant to scare off the Nian beast. “Nian” is “year” in Chinese. ☜

Chapter 556: Motives and Explanations

“So that’s why Second Senior Brother has been traveling in the Buddhist Kingdom?” Lu Yang was surprised. He had assumed his second senior brother had offended Yun Zhi and was exiled thirty thousand li to the west, forced to beg in the Buddhist Kingdom, wander the streets homeless, and pose as a Buddha statue in temples, living a pitifully impoverished life.

Apparently, I had overthought it.

“Unfortunately, he hasn’t found any useful clues after all these years. Instead, he’s been deported by the Buddhist Kingdom multiple times and had to sneak back in.” Yun Zhi shook her head regretfully.

Tracing clues about an immortal who controlled time is too difficult. Or perhaps I could visit the Five-Elements Sect to examine the Jianmu wood more closely.

“Since the Jianmu wood has regained vitality, if the Epoch Immortal is still alive, could he reenter his Jianmu form?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded. “Quite possible. After all, reforging an immortal body is arduous. If the original body can be used, that would naturally be ideal.

“One more thing. I encountered the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others in the Five-Elements Sect’s immortal domain.”

“What happened? Please elaborate, Senior.” Yun Zhi grew solemn. How had Lu Yang and Senior gained so much from a single visit to the Five-Elements Sect?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recounted their experiences in the immortal domain in detail, emphasizing the Epoch Immortal’s spacetime passage and conversation with her. Naturally, she remained unaware that the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Qilin Immortal had played Five in a Row to avoid eating her meals.

Yun Zhi’s brow furrowed slightly. “When I entered the immortal domain, no historical projections appeared. I didn’t expect such major events to be embedded in the immortals’ chess game.”

Lu Yang was perplexed. According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, those who gleaned insights from the chess game would see the historical projection. Why hadn’t Big Senior Sister seen it?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rolled her eyes. How could Lu Yang ever live without me? He’s too stupid. “The Heaven Mandate Immortal let later generations view the historical projection to show off his prestige. Lass Yun is at the same level as me—what use would it be for her to view the historical projection?”

Lu Yang conceded the point. Even if Big Senior Sister had comprehended something, she wouldn’t marvel at the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s methods.

Lu Yang remarked, “Among the Five Ancient Immortals, the Heaven Mandate Immortal seems to be the brains. His planning is so thorough.”

“What nonsense are you spouting?! I was the brains. How could the Heaven Mandate Immortal surpass my intellect? If the other immortals were as clever as I was, they would have thought of joining hands and killing me secretly, then resurrecting me in the future. Problem solved!”

Lu Yang, “...”

I must admit, this is a solution, though it’s not one normal people can conceive of. “Immortal Fairy, I thought you’d suggest the four immortals convey the message to your past self so that she would kill herself on the spot to prevent being killed by others.”

“That’s Plan B.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was meticulous and always prepared more than one contingency.

Yun Zhi acted like she hadn’t heard the internal discussion of the Everlasting Lineage. “Immortal Fairy, it’s a fact you were assassinated. After the other four immortals learned from you that you would be killed, they must have prepared countermeasures. If they weren’t meant to be used on you, they were likely safeguards for themselves to ensure their survival.

“Therefore, the four ancient immortals may be alive, including the Epoch Immortal. They have hidden themselves behind history, never taking action—is it because they’re in dire conditions, or are there other reasons?

“Based on how you two were unable to hear the information about Senior in the historical projection, and that the spacetime channel was disrupted, it indicates the intervention of another force.” No matter how subpar the Epoch Dao Fruit was, it couldn’t have transmitted only five words. Moreover, the Epoch Immortal himself had mentioned the presence of interference.

“It looks like some power had altered history to prevent later generations from obtaining information about Senior.” The immortal cookbook’s authorship changing from the “Everlasting Immortal Fairy” to the “Heaven Mandate Immortal” and the ancient immortals substituting the “Everlasting Immortal Fairy” with the “Epoch Immortal” were all evidence.

“It appears the contents of ancient texts cannot be fully trusted. Some parts have been edited. To have achieved something like this, the culprit probably used Dao Fruits like Karma, Destiny, Consciousness, and Law Follows Words.” Muttering to herself, Yun Zhi lifted her head and met Lu Yang’s gaze. Upon remembering that Lu Yang was still too young to access such matters, she fell silent.

Lu Yang screamed internally. Big Senior Sister, you can’t just stop like that! Either say everything or nothing! Why leave me hanging? freewebnovel.com

Of the Dao Fruits mentioned, he only knew the Karma Dao Fruit. He had inferred its abilities from the second Imperial Preceptor’s incipient version. The Karma Dao Fruit can pull off a complete subterfuge, making even immortals forget!

Only an immortal can kill another immortal. Is Big Senior Sister implying a sixth immortal existed in ancient times and wielded the Karma Dao Fruit, using it to erase their own presence?

The other three Dao Fruits must have similar effects!

If a sixth immortal really existed, with how strong the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was, the sixth immortal’s Dao Fruit must have perfectly countered the Everlasting Immortal Fairy!

Lu Yang silently pleaded with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. She surely knows the functions of these Dao Fruits.

Unbeknownst to him, when he turned his gaze toward the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Yun Zhi also turned a warning gaze toward the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

Agreeing that Lu Yang shouldn’t learn too much, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy adamantly refused to elaborate on the Dao Fruits.

“Speaking of which, what motive would the mastermind have for killing the Immortal Fairy?” This was a question that had plagued Lu Yang all this time. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was unambitious and stayed aloof from worldly affairs, not to mention that she maintained close ties with the four other ancient immortals. Killing her would inevitably provoke the other four immortals. Assuming the culprit wielded the Karma Dao Fruit, what reason would they have to risk their life by antagonizing such formidable enemies?

“Motive...reason...

“Motive...reason...

“There must be one—a reason related to his personal interests...”

Something suddenly clicked. His eyes lit up with excitement. “Could it be a devouring-type Dao Fruit? The more Dao Fruits consumed, the greater the power?

“Let’s tentatively call this the Devouring Dao Fruit. Suppose there weren’t five but seven immortals in ancient times, and the sixth immortal held the Karma Dao Fruit, while the seventh immortal held the Devouring Dao Fruit. By consuming the sixth immortal, the seventh immortal gained the abilities of the Karma Dao Fruit to conceal their own existence.

“To grow stronger, the seventh immortal targeted the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, striking from the shadows to devour the Everlasting Dao Fruit and become an undying and indestructible existence. However, something went wrong—perhaps the four ancient immortals arrived in time—thwarting the seventh immortal’s attempt!

This would explain the Everlasting Creed’s existence—they established the creed to devour the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit!”

It all adds up!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also enthusiastically patted Lu Yang’s shoulder, feeling he had pieced the truth together. “That makes a lot of sense!”

Yun Zhi cut in. “Enough, Little Junior Brother. Don’t get too involved in this matter; it’s too dangerous. What you should do now is cultivate diligently.”

“Oh.”

Chapter 557: Letter from Third Senior Sister

Three months had passed since Lu Yang returned from the Five-Elements Sect.

On this day, Yun Zhi was taken aback by a long-distance missive she received. After a moment of contemplation in her cave abode, she exhaled softly. “It looks like Little Junior Brother will need to make a trip.”

~~~

Meanwhile, Lu Yang had reached a critical juncture in his cultivation. His mouth was wide open as he devoured spirit energy. Beads of sweat formed on his forehead, evaporating into mist that gathered above him like an auspicious cloud.

“Whew! I’ve finally advanced from the seventh to the eighth layer of the Golden Core Stage!”

When he opened his eyes, he saw Yun Zhi standing right before him, her visage devoid of emotions. “Since when has the Golden Core Stage been divided into seven or eight layers?”

Lu Yang immediately ratted out the mastermind. “The Immortal Fairy said so! She claimed finer divisions of cultivation stages increase motivation, making one feel a sense of achievement with every incremental improvement!”

“Hey hey hey, you betrayed me so easily?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy emerged from Lu Yang’s body indignantly. She was clad in pink sleepwear, having just woken to hear him tattling on her.

“How could you call this betrayal? I was simply answering Big Senior Sister’s question honestly.”

“This is betrayal.”

“This is not betrayal.”

Yun Zhi felt that if she allowed the two to continue the debate, they wouldn’t be able to do anything else for the rest of the day.

She whipped out a letter adorned with graceful and delicate characters that read: To Senior Sister Yun Zhi

“This is...”

“A letter from your Third Senior Sister Gan Tian in the Demon Region. She said she’s encountered some stuff related to the ancient era there. She hopes I can find a scholar knowledgeable about ancient times to assist her research and answer her questions.”

This was no ordinary letter but a magical treasure crafted in paired forms of mother and child. Yun Zhi possessed the mother artifact, while Gan Tian possessed the child artifact. Whatever Gan Tian wrote in her letter would automatically be reflected in Yun Zhi’s.

“After much consideration, you’re the most well-versed in ancient history. If you’re not busy lately, you can make a trip to the Demon Region.”

Lu Yang pondered. I’ve just broken through to the eighth layer, still far away from the ninth layer. Remaining in the sect all the time to cultivate seems unwise. Better to head out and venture.

“I’ll go.”

Seeing Lu Yang agree so readily, Yun Zhi felt she could see their shifu in him. She advised, “You may make new discoveries at the border between the Central Continent and the Demon Region. You can consult Third Junior Sister when you meet her.”

~~~

A cultivator clad in gray silk descended, hands tucked in his sleeves. He wore a faint smile, his eyes narrowed to almost invisible slits.

“Halt! Identify yourself.” The Dao-Seeking Sect disciple guarding the gate stopped the cultivator from entering, eyeing him warily.

The cultivator seemed to have anticipated this and fished out a letter, passing it to the two disciples. “Excuse me, I am Xu You, the chief steward of the Meng Family. I’m here to visit our eldest young master. Please kindly make things convenient for me.”

The disciples opened the envelope and examined the recommendation letter from the Meng Family, which proved Xu You’s identity. No one would dare counterfeit the Meng Family’s letter. The Meng Family had always been the ones deceiving others—who would dare impersonate them? Unless one had no intention of staying in the Central Continent any longer.

“So it’s Senior Xu. May we know what business brings you to Junior Brother Meng?” The entire Dao-Seeking Sect knew that Meng Jingzhou was the Meng Family’s eldest young master; they simply didn’t speak of it openly.

Xu You sighed, his sign fading. “What else? It’s none other than persuading the eldest young master to change his mind and return home. His parents miss him dearly.” He produced two storage rings from his sleeves and pressed them into the two disciples’ palms. “It’s freezing out here. I’m sure it’s no easy task for you to be guarding the mountain gates here. These storage rings contain some trivial items. Please make things convenient for me and grant me passage.”

The Dao-Seeking Sect disciples declined vehemently. “This won’t do! The sect prohibits bribery. Anyone caught will face harsh punishment!”

“Please keep them. Only you and I know. As long as the three of us say nothing, who would know?”

Seeing they couldn’t refuse, the disciples reluctantly accepted. “It’s only natural for parents to want to see their son. Please enter, Senior Xu.” The disciples folded the letter, slipped it back into the envelope, and returned it to Xu You, stepping aside to clear the way.

~~~

Once inside, Xu You’s melancholic expression vanished, replaced by his customary benign smile.

The River Spirit’s head emerged from the water.

Xu You nodded and bowed to the River Spirit, proceeding only after the River Spirit returned to the water.

He had long done his homework. Eldest Young Master is in a cave abode on Body Refinement Peak. The cave abode is easily identifiable by an old horse grazing outside.

The old horse snorted in acknowledgement when it was greeted, confirming that Meng Jingzhou was inside.

Xu You rapped thrice on the stone door, waited thirty seconds, then repeated when he received no response. Just as he was about to knock again, Meng Jingzhou opened the door irritably. “Who is it? I’m not in seclusion. Can’t you just come in if you’re looking for me...” Looking up, he recognized Xu You and grew vigilant. “Steward Xu, what brings you here?”

“Young Master, could we speak inside? It’s inconvenient to speak of certain matters outside.”

Meng Jingzhou could only invite Xu You to enter the cave abode.

Xu You seated himself on a straw mat and explained, “The patriarch hasn’t seen you in two years and hopes you can make a trip back. He says he misses you very much.”

“Impossible.” Meng Jingzhou refused outright. I left home with such steel resolve back then! It’s only been two years. How can I return after merely two years?

“The patriarch said he knows all about your misdeeds and has forgiven you.”

Meng Jingzhou studied Xu You’s smiling countenance skeptically, attempting to discern the veracity of his words. “Really?”

“Really.”

Meng Jingzhou was overjoyed. “I deliberately arranged for my dad and little uncle to throw fortunes to vie over the top courtesan at the brothel and intensified their conflict by having them open their curtains and face each other awkwardly. Dad found out about that and forgave me?

“I beat up Minister Li’s little grandson, Minister Gong’s little son, and the young imperial prince, but I thought I was meticulous enough. Dad found out about that and forgave me?

“When Dad wanted to take in a concubine, I told Mom about it, resulting in Grandfather giving Dad a thrashing in the dark. Dad found out about that and forgave me?

“And also...”

Xu You grew increasingly alarmed. The patriarch only mentioned two to three of these incidents before I came. He said nothing about the rest... Clearing his throat, he braced himself to salvage the situation. “Eldest Young Master, actually, you don’t have to be in such a rush to return home. The patriarch has been busy with political affairs recently and may not have the time to meet you. You can just find another suitable date to head back.

“I’ve come here today mainly for another matter.”

“What is it?”

Still wearing a smile, Xu You’s voice turned low. “I heard you’re very close to Prodigy Lu Yang. The patriarch said this boy is incredibly talented and is destined for greatness. Perhaps he could be of use to our Meng Family...”

Chapter 558: Lu Yang Is My Good Brother—I’d Never Harm Him!

Lu Yang arrived at Meng Jingzhou’s cave abode. Before he could knock on the door, he heard Meng Jingzhou speaking with someone inside.

“Impossible! I’m Meng Jingzhou—what kind of person do you take me for? How could I throw my brother into peril?!” freewebnovel.com

“This is the patriarch’s instruction. It’s the only way to control Lu Yang.”

“Go back and tell my dad that this is impossible! He’d better give up this idea! Don’t talk to me about my dad. If he’s so capable, let him come to the Dao-Seeking Sect. I’ll ask my shifu to pummel him!”

“Eldest Young Master...ai...” Seeing the persuasion yielded no results, Xu You could only give up.

When he headed to the door, he froze, surprised to see Lu Yang standing outside; he had seen Lu Yang’s portrait before.

Lu Yang also felt awkward. Although the two were discussing a matter related to him—one that hardly seemed favorable—bumping into each other like this was still uncomfortable.

The two exchanged a nod as they passed each other, neither speaking a word.

Stepping inside the cave abode, Lu Yang saw the fuming Meng Jingzhou.

“Outrageous! Look at the kind of crooked schemes my father is plotting!” Meng Jinghou vented. Though he often thought of schemes to sabotage Lu Yang, when it truly mattered, he stood firmly by Lu Yang’s side.

Truly, my good brother. Touched by his sense of brotherhood, Lu Yang pretended he hadn’t eavesdropped at the door. “The person just now...”

“Xu You. He used to be my dad’s study companion back in the day. Now he has been promoted to chief steward.”

“He’s here to urge you to go home?”

“That was what he did initially, but he stopped after a few words. He said he was seeking me out for something important this time.”

“Which is?”

“My dad wants to betroth my younger sister to you. I have turned it down on your behalf.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Truly, my good brother.

“I remember your younger sister hasn’t reached the age to cultivate, right?”

“It’s just an engagement, obviously. Don’t aristocratic families love these arrangements? I had a whole crowd of people knocking on the door with marriage proposals when I was a kid. It’s roughly the same routine.

“My dad probably intercepted the letters I wrote to my younger sister and read how I praised you as devious, ruthless, and seemingly possessing the potential to surpass the sect leader. He must have thought you were a talent and wanted you to be his son-in-law. Steward Xu also conveyed his message that since your shifu is the Taciturn Daoist Priest and you’ll never find a wife, you might as well marry into the Meng Family.

“Anyway, why’d you come looking for me?”

“Third Senior Sister sent word, hoping I could visit the Demon Region. I’m planning to make a trip there. Do you want to join me?”

“Which third senior sister?”

“Gan Tian.”

“Who’s that?”

Only then did Lu Yang remember Gan Tian had been away from the sect for years. Moreover, given her low-profile nature, few stories about her circulated within the sect. “My shifu has four disciples. Aside from Big Senior Sister, there’s Second Senior Brother Ye Zijin and Third Senior Sister Gan Tian. One’s in the Golden Buddhist Kingdom, and the other is in the Demon Region in the south.”

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes lit up with recognition. “Oh, I know your second senior brother! He’s the one whose nascent soul ran away and couldn’t even beat his own nascent soul!”

“...I hope you can also say that to his face when you meet him.”

~~~

Xu You hadn’t gone far. He sat beside the old horse and pulled out two gourds of wine—one for himself and the other shoved into the old horse’s mouth.

After pouring himself half a gourd, he asked, “Brother Horse, it’s been two years since I last saw you. How’s life in the Dao-Seeking Sect? Managing the entire Meng Family is exhausting.

The old horse shot him a sidelong glance and tilted its head to gulp down half the gourd of wine before releasing the gourd, letting it hover midair. “Do you really think following the Eldest Young Master is easy?”

You being a steward is nothing. How could it be tougher than my job? When I brought the Eldest Young Master to the Dao-Seeking Sect, before we entered the gates, he called Yun Zhi into the carriage. He even asked whether she was participating in the entrance exams, claiming he had the real exam questions.

I was trembling the whole ride with Yun Zhi inside the carriage.

Then, on the Eldest Young Master’s first mission with Lu Yang, they infiltrated the Everlasting Creed and became branch leaders. Just when I thought we could finally return to the sect after all that ordeal, Lu Yang had to court trouble and utter the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s true name.

I watched an ancient immortal manifest right before my eyes; I nearly died of fright.

Subsequently, I took the Eldest Young Master to participate in the Qingzhou Grand Ceremony. Halfway through, two Great Yu Fusion cultivators and one Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivator popped up. Thankfully, Yun Zhi stepped in.

After that, we headed to Wilderness Province. Oh boy! We encountered three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, one of whom was even a Great Yu emperor. And I was the one who had to cart their souls back.

Which of these events sounds like something a demon king like me can handle?

It’s more like it for the Meng Family’s old ancestor to come here and pull the carriage. This old horse ain’t doing it anymore.

“If you think I’ve got it easy, we can swap.”

Perfect chance for you to witness what high-level cultivators are truly like. Don’t think just being at the Fusion Stage makes us impressive. You’ll be embarrassed to escort the Eldest Young Master if you’re not minimally at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

Noticing the old horse’s sly grin, Xu You sobered up instantly and shook his head vehemently.

The old horse suddenly asked, “Did you do something when you came to the Dao-Seeking Sect? Why is someone looking for you?”

“What did I do?” Xu You took a while to process the question.

Just then, a disciple responsible for guarding the mountain gates gave directions to First Elder. “First Elder, he’s the one who bribed us! These are the storage rings he gave us.”

Xu You, “...”

First Elder wore a smile identical to Xu You’s. “Old Brother Xu, care to explain? Bribing our disciples is no small matter. Do you want me to report you to the authorities, or would you prefer to be detained in our Dao-Seeking Sect for a few days?”

As the eldest brother of the Dao-Seeking Nine and the overseer of the Great Mission Hall, he wielded all intelligence regarding the sect’s affairs. He knew every Fusion cultivator.

The Meng Family Head, demon king old horse, and Xu You were sworn brothers who had traveled the world together in their youth. Later, Xu You became the Meng Family’s steward, while the old horse split his time between the Meng Family and his home in the East Sea.

“I’ll stay in the Dao-Seeking Sect.” Xu You decided quickly.

Without hesitation, First Elder produced a set of shackles he had prepared and clamped them onto Xu You with a loud clang.

“Hey, you don’t have to be so ruthless, right?”

First Elder smirked coldly. “I know what you’re up to. You find being the steward too tiring and plan to take a few days' break at the Dao-Seeking Sect. Had you been upfront about it, I could have played along. But since you insist on scheming...who else should I catch if not you! Come with me!”

Think you can play tricks in front of me? Impossible.

Xu You turned around in despair, only to see the old horse’s expression of schadenfreude.

Just then, Meng Jingzhou pushed the door open. “Old Horse, Lu Yang and I plan to head to the Demon Region.”

The old horse’s face went ashen. I want to trade places with Xu You.

Chapter 559: The United Demon Race

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou immediately decided to head to the Demon Region.

“We shouldn’t rush into this. We need to understand the situation in the Demon Region first.” Lu Yang tried to appear composed, struggling to suppress his grin.

“What about Man Gu and the other two? Should they come along?”

“Man Gu is out of the question. His Ancient Barbarian bloodline is a double-edged sword when it comes to demons. It has suppressive effects on low-level demons but draws enmity from high-level demons.” Lu Yang still vividly remembered their training in the jungle at the Foundation Establishment Stage. Man Gu’s bloodline had awakened and attracted a swarm of Golden Core demon beasts.

If Man Gu were to step into the Demon Region, they would likely draw the attention of a horde of demon beasts at the Divine Transfiguration Stage or even higher. At that point, the only thing they could do was run for their lives.

Oh, we may not outrun the demon beasts—better to use Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist right away.

“Junior Sister Tao is busy cultivating her Metamorphic Immortal Physique and can’t leave.” Before coming to Meng Jingzhou’s place, Lu Yang had visited Tao Yaoye. He saw her enveloped in white-gold feathers as if in incubation, completely cut off from the outside world. She couldn’t be disrupted.

“Junior Brother Li should be free. We can ask him.”

Leaving the old horse behind and ignoring the shackled Xu You, the two made their way to Hundred Refinements Peak to find Li Haoran.

~~~

Li Haoran was shirtless, and his wig was removed, revealing well-defined muscles and a shiny bald head. He swung a massive hammer, forging some magical treasure with rhythmic clangs.

The noise from crafting the magical treasure was deafening, but disciples of Hundred Refinements Peak always set up Soundproofing Arrays beforehand to avoid disturbing others.

“Whew, finally done.” Li Haoran exhaled in relief, picking up a small rectangular object from under his hammer.

“What kind of magical artifact are you refining?”

Hearing Lu Yang’s voice, Li Haoran looked up, only now noticing their arrival. He had been too absorbed in hammering to pay attention to his surroundings earlier. “Ah, you mean this? It’s not a magical artifact—it’s a compressed mantou.

“This is good stuff provided by the Hundred Refinements Peak for our sect’s disciples. It compresses steamed mantou buns, Great Rejuvenation Pills, Essence-Gathering Pills, and more into a single item. Whether you’re exhausted from your travels or drained of spirit energy in battle, one bite will restore your stamina and energy!

“You can even use it as a Heart-Protecting Mirror by placing it in front of your chest. It’s way stronger than the previous shaobing version. Want one? It’s freshly forged.”

The two hastily shook their heads to decline and explained their purpose for visiting.

Li Haoran showed a troubled expression. “Go to the Demon Region? I’m afraid that won’t do. My shifu told me to focus on my cultivation in the sect. I can’t leave the sect until I catch up to your cultivation realm.”

“Aren’t you already at the Advanced Golden Core Stage?”

“But I only reached this stage three months ago. You two succeeded five months ago.”

Lu Yang understood. Li Haoran is at the seventh layer of the Golden Core Stage, while Old Meng and I are already at the eighth layer. This is the disparity.

“If you’re going to the Demon Region, you should make ample preparations beforehand. Qin Haoran once headed there to hide from his debts, so I have a slightly better understanding of the area. There are some things to watch out for—for instance, Senior Brother Meng, you'd better not bring that horse of yours there.”

“Ah? Why not?”

“The old horse is an aberrant demon beast! Making a demon beast pull your carriage—are you afraid you won’t make enough enemies of the demons?”

With the few dragon scales on its forehead, the old horse could easily be mistaken for an aberrant demon beast, in other words, a livestock with demon beast blood but impure lineage.

Li Haoran didn’t know the old horse’s true identity, not that it mattered. Whether the old horse was a demon beast or an aberrant demon beast, having it pull their carriage would be no different from bringing Man Gu along to the Demon Region.

“But if the roles were to be reversed, you probably wouldn’t make enemies.”

“Reverse?”

“You two pull the carriage while the old horse rides in it.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou didn’t know what to say. Then what’s the point of bringing the old horse at all?

“Are all demon beasts that united?” Lu Yang muttered internally. Humans are one race, while demons are made up of many races. Would tigers really get angry just seeing a horse pull a carriage? That’s taking unity too far.

“The demons weren’t this united at the start,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy chimed in, privy to the inside story. “In the beginning, demon beasts ran rampant; there was no place for humans at all. The tiger tribes, dragon tribes, ox tribes, and horse tribes had vast divides between them, constantly fighting to the death.

“Only when humans eventually rose and formed tribes did the demon beasts feel threatened. By our era, three of the Five Ancient Immortals were human, while only the Qilin Immortal was from the demon race. The Epoch Immortal didn’t belong to any race. It was three against one, with the human race securing an overwhelming advantage. That was how humans cemented their dominance.

“Under the pressure from the humans, the demons voluntarily united, calling themselves ‘demons’ or the ‘demon race.’”

Lu Yang quipped inwardly, I thought they were forced to unite out of fear of being eaten by you.

Li Haoran nodded. He used a twig to draw a large circle on the ground, then drew many smaller circles within.

“This is the Demon Region. The small circles are the demon tribes.

“Unlike Great Xia or the Buddhist Kingdom, the demon race has no order and centralized rule, having never established a dynasty. They are very much like the earliest humans, living in tribes. “Demons revere strength and bloodline. The purer the bloodline, the stronger one is, and the easier it is to earn their respect. Examples are pure-blooded dragons, pure-blooded phoenixes, and pure-blooded xuanwu (black tortoise)—major clans with pure-blooded lineages. They command the highest status among demons.

“Of course, humans are exceptions. At the very least, I’ve never heard of demons respecting us just for being pure-blooded humans.”

Following that, Li Haoran listed taboos of various demon tribes, like never touching a dragon’s reverse scale and never mentioning to a phoenix the matter of them selling blood.

“My knowledge of the Demon Region is limited. After all, I only have half of Qin Haoran’s memories for now. Many things are still blurry, and telling you might mislead you instead. The elders traveled extensively in their youth and have probably been to the Demon Region. You can ask them for advice and any precautions you should take.”

The elders had seen it all—both sides of the law, prisons, brothels, the Buddhist Kingdom, and the Demon Region.

Turns out you wrote it, Shifu!

Ordinary storage rings could only store non-living things.

Chapter 561: The Central Continent and the Demon Region

After strutting around to flaunt their power, the two Golden Core ancestors deftly circumvented the territories of Nascent Soul demon beasts—not because they couldn’t beat them, but to avoid unnecessary trouble.

Just like that, they finally arrived at the depths of the jungle.

“The fog is so thick.”

Before the two lay a fog so dense they couldn’t see their fingers. It was as though they were wading through reeds. Unable to see the path ahead, they could only rely on their instincts as they ventured ahead.

“Ha!” Meng Jingzhou unleashed a palm strike with dazzling, golden palm seals that reached the height of a man. The astonishing palm wind could typically bowl over a Basic Golden Core Cultivator, yet when it struck the fog, it didn’t even create a ripple. Even the palm wind couldn’t disperse the fog before their eyes.

Lu Yang tried to extend his proud spiritual consciousness, only to find it dissipating upon contact with the fog.

“I’ve long heard of the fog in the jungle’s depths, but I never imagined it to be this bizarre. Even our spiritual consciousness can’t penetrate it—no, or I should say it disintegrates our spiritual consciousness.”

During their training at the Demon Suppression Pass, the two had heard of the dense fog shrouding the boundary between the forest’s depths and the Demon Region. The fog lingered all year round, remaining even at noon.

“I thought reaching the Golden Core Stage would trivialize the rumored fog. Looks like I was too naive. I’m afraid this is the work of a demon beast like the Mirage-Clam King.[1]

With their spiritual consciousness nullified and their five senses dulled, their awareness of the surroundings plummeted, leaving them vulnerable to ambush. The two proceeded with extreme caution, minimizing their presence within the fog.

However, their worries were unnecessary. Within the fog, they couldn’t detect their foes, but similarly, their foes couldn’t detect them. No one would choose to launch an ambush here.

“Could this be the anomaly Big Senior Sister mentioned?” Lu Yang suddenly recalled Yun Zhi’s words before their departure.

“What did she say?”

“She told me we might make new discoveries at the border between the Central Continent and the Demon Region, and that if I have any questions, I can consult Third Senior Sister when I meet her.”

Why is there a wall in front of you?” Still groggy, she rubbed her eyes as she warned Lu Yang—the latter was moments from colliding into the wall.

“Wall?” The fog was too thick for Lu Yang to see anything.

“A big and tall wall! I can't even see its end... Wait, something’s wrong!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gasped softly, sensing something amiss. No matter how strange the fog was, it couldn’t obstruct her vision and immortal consciousness; she could perceive their surroundings clearly.

“What’s wrong?” Lu Yang seldom saw such a huge reaction from her. The last time was when she clamored about suppressing me, only to be suppressed by Big Senior Sister after I summoned her.

In front of him was a thick wall so humongous that even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s consciousness couldn’t see its ends!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s immortal sense extended beyond the fog, revealing the wall teeming with shrubs, luxuriant trees, roaming demon beasts, and the congregation of tribes—a scene brimming with prosperity.

Most importantly, the demon beasts Lu Yang saw were standing upon the wall!

“Lu Yang, where are you?”

Unaware that Lu Yang had halted, Meng Jingzhou had continued until he noticed the person beside him was gone.

Lu Yang fell silent. He watched as Meng Jingzhou “walked” onto the wall.

The moment Meng Jingzhou contacted the wall, he stood on the wall at a ninety-degree angle to Lu Yang. Yet, Meng Jingzhou kept walking, which meant he was completely unaware!

“Stop! Come back first!” Lu Yang yelled.

Meng Jingzhou turned back in bafflement. However, he trusted that Lu Yang had discovered something, so he retreated a few steps back, returning to Lu Yang’s side.

“What’s wrong?” Meng Jingzhou was puzzled.

The Central Continent and the Demon Region aren’t connected—they’re two separate continents! And these two landmasses are positioned perpendicularly!

He had always assumed the name came from their central position; to the east was the East Sea, to the west was the Golden Buddhist Kingdom, to the south was the Demon Region, and to the north was the Extreme North.

But if the Demon Region and the Central Continent are perpendicular to each other, how could it be called ‘central?’”

Unless the other three places are also landmasses perpendicular to the Central Continent! It’s sealed off by four surrounding continents. That is why it’s called the “Central Continent!”

“No mistake—this is something only an immortal is capable of,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy concluded.

“The Ancient Nameless One?”

“Likely.”

The Ancient Nameless One hadn’t refined the stars into one continent, but five! I wonder what their motives are.

Refining stars into continents sounded majestic, but the execution was arduous and not to be undertaken lightly. With such painstaking effort involved, there must have been a purpose.

Lu Yang took a deep breath. Big Senior Sister had already anticipated this, which is why she told me to consult Third Senior Sister. Chapter 562: Fleeing From Marriage

By the time they arrived in the Demon Region, night had descended. The bright moonlight cascaded downward, illuminating the scene before them. Stretching out before the two was a forest—a sight exceedingly common in the Demon Region.

Unlike the Central Continent, which had undergone many developments, the Demon Region operated under a comparatively backward system. Villages served as strongholds, and development was lacking, with numerous primitive forests remaining untouched. Furthermore, the tribes eking out a living along the border were all mixed-blood demon tribes. They were considered small tribes and didn’t have the means to develop the woodlands.

“Where’s Third Senior Sister?” Meng Jingzhou asked.

“According to the map Big Senior Sister gave us, we set out from the Demon Suppression Pass, arrive in the Demon Region, and head north for two thousand li. Right at the boundary between the Qiongqi Tribe and the Moonhowl Skywolf Tribe, that’s where Third Senior Sister is waiting for us.” Lu Yang pulled out the crude map with only sketches of the Demon Region’s border, the Qiongqi Tribe, and the Moonhowl Skywolf Tribe. It utterly omitted any demons they might encounter along the way.

“That’s not too far. About three days’ worth of journey.”

“Let’s set off then.”

Having confirmed their direction, the two prepared to depart. Although it was already late at night, their cultivation was flawless, and their eyesight had been honed. With just a sliver of light, they could see the path clearly. Walking under the moon’s glow was no different from traversing under the sun.

Just as they were about to step forward, they heard a series of rustling sounds from the jungle’s depths, accompanied by muffled shouts.

“Stop there!”

“Don’t let them escape!”

“Young Miss, stop running!”

A man and a woman emerged from the jungle’s depths. Spotting Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, they faltered for a split second. They had seized the cover of night to flee a marriage, hoping to run to Great Xia’s territory. Unfortunately, their plan had loopholes. Their tribesmen detected something amiss and gave chase.

Just as success seemed within reach, they realized their tribe had anticipated their escape route all along and had laid an ambush here.

“Break through!” The man gritted his teeth. As long as we get past these two and enter the fog, we’ll be able to escape as far as we like!

He pulled out a broad saber from his storage ring. Gripping it with both hands, his muscles bulged. A mist as cold as autumn frost condensed on the blade, radiating a palpable chill.

In the past, he would never have dared raise a weapon against strong cultivators like Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. But now, with his beloved beside him, pursuers behind him, and freedom before him, he had to gamble and fight with everything on the line!

The woman was no weakling either. She wielded twin swords, whose tips soared like dragons and danced like phoenixes.

“Whoever stands in my way shall die!”

The man and woman leaped high into the air, reaching approximately the height of Lu Yang’s knees, before being unceremoniously kicked away by Lu Yang with a casual sweep of his foot.

Lu Yang crouched down, utterly exasperated as he gazed at the two one-inch-tall figures.

“What are you two doing?”

Before the couple could answer, their pursuers, who were also one inch tall, arrived. Most had human forms, though a minority retained the features of their original race—insects.

The corner of Meng Jingzhou’s eye twitched. Just as we brothers wanted to leave, this pair of tiny insects darted out of the jungle, clamoring something about “those who stand in my way shall die,” then brandished toothpick-sized weapons as they charged over.

Never mind that you hardly have any cultivation; even if you have cultivation, where did you get the courage to pick a fight with us?

Insects were also part of the demon race. If dragons and phoenixes stood at the pinnacle of demons, insects languished at the very bottom. Even relatively harmless races like rabbits or mice held a higher status. As insects were inherently weak, they could only survive by huddling together for warmth. Whether they were ants, mantises, dung beetles, or mosquitoes, they dwelled together and were collectively known to outsiders as the Insect Tribe or Insect Race.

Even after insects achieved a human form, their insufficient cultivation only allowed them to transform into one-inch-tall figures. Only upon reaching the Foundation Establishment Stage would their stature grow to that of a human child, and finally, at the Golden Core Stage, they could assume the size of an adult human.

The man coughed up blood, staring at Lu Yang in despair. With his skills and agility, he could challenge even a Level Two Qi Training cultivator. However, Lu Yang could severely injure him with a single strike. He must be an expert at least at the Level Four Qi Refining Stage!

This wasn’t Lu Yang’s first encounter with the insect race. The Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm husband and wife in the herb garden were insects minimally at the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

But it was his first encounter with insects this small. He had only dismissed such stories as jokes, but now that he had seen these insects daring to draw blades against him...he found it even more amusing.

After the pursuers witnessed Lu Yang’s display of power, reverence surged in their hearts, and they no longer dared to make a ruckus. One of them stepped forward, straining his neck to look up at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. Dropping to his knees, he trembled as he said, “I am Li Shiqiang of the Insect Tribe. We were unaware Your Excellencies had arrived and had offended you. Please forgive us.”

He was the number one expert in his tribe, but facing the unfathomable Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, he dared not show the slightest discourtesy, striving to ensure his etiquette was thorough.

“I wouldn’t call that offending us. We are from the Prison Suppression Sect. I’m Meng Yang, and he’s Lu Jingzhou.” Since the other party had introduced themselves, it was only proper to reciprocate.

This was the cover story they had agreed on during their journey. Posing as rogue cultivators wouldn’t work because demons placed great importance on bloodlines and human ancestry. Claiming to be rogue cultivators would draw contempt and even ill intentions from demons.

Hence, they needed identities with respectable backgrounds. Impersonating someone from the imperial court was risky and could easily land them in legal trouble when they returned.

They couldn’t use their identities as disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

The Hanging Monastery had too few members, making impersonation difficult.

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace comprised only female cultivators, making impersonation possible.

That left the Five-Elements Sect and the Prison Suppression Sect.

Lu Yang had chosen the latter.

Li Shiqiang seemed almost flustered by their politeness. It’s my first time encountering experts who are so courteous. Reasonable demons are scarce in the Demon Region.

“Commander Li, please, just let Xiaomi and me go,” the man who had tried to flee the marriage beseeched piteously, but Commander Li remained unmoved.

In truth, their escape plan had been doomed from the start. Great Xia would never permit insects to enter. This was an ironclad rule. If they entered and proliferated, a swarm of Level One Qi Training mosquitoes would be a nightmare for ordinary people. The Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm couple was an exception. Since they were at the Divine Transfiguration Stage, reproduction was fairly difficult.

Commander Li dared not disobey, so he recounted the story in full detail.

The insect race was internally divided into tribes. Theirs was the weakest, without a single Intermediate Qi Training insect. The son of the chieftain from a more powerful insect tribe had taken a fancy to Song Xiaomi. Using his influence, he pressured Song Xiaomi’s tribe to force her into marriage.

Song Xiaomi’s tribe had no other choice but to hand her over, but Song Xiaomi had a childhood sweetheart named Shi Chui. He was a genius within the tribe, but against the might of the other tribe, his resistance was as futile as a mantis trying to stop a chariot.

Both Song Xiaomi and Chi Shui opposed the marriage, leading to their nighttime escape, where they eventually ran into Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“That’s quite interesting. Come, take us to see your insect tribe.”

Neither Lu Yang nor Meng Jingzhou had seen what an insect tribe was like. It’s rare for us to come to the Demon Region. Wouldn’t this trip be a waste if we don’t see the local specialties?

Chapter 563: Might of a Golden Core Old Ancestor!

With two experts minimally at the Intermediate Qi Refining Stage wanting to visit their tribe, how could Commander Li dare refuse? Though inwardly, he bemoaned his plight, his heart quaking with apprehension.

Our tribe is weak and small. If we offend these two experts, a mere wave of their hands could spell utter annihilation of our tribe.

Any insect race capable of forming a tribe numbered at least in the millions. Although a tribe could be destroyed, exterminating every last member was a nigh-impossible task. It was precisely their overwhelming advantage in numbers and frightening reproductive capacity that allowed the insects to survive from ancient times to the present day. These two monsters are at least at the Level Six Qi Training Stage!

A calamity that could wipe out our entire tribe!

Shouldn’t we at least have a Foundation Establishment cultivator here to lend credence to your performance?

Song Xiaomi and Chi Shui were overjoyed. They never imagined an expert of this caliber would offer to protect them.

The tribe chieftain was equally delighted. He no longer had to marry his daughter off, and their tribe would also gain the protection of formidable experts. This is a heaven-sent fortune!

Upon learning that the tribe would be under the protection of two mighty experts, the entire tribe erupted in cheers and enthusiastically hosted the two guests.
