The duo noticed that human-form insects were rare within the tribe. The majority had yet to achieve human form. These insects possessed intelligence but lacked the ability to speak. The insects capable of assuming human form held important positions in the tribe—guarding the village, managing the village, going out to hunt, and so forth. Those who had chased after Song Xiaomi and Chi Shui were responsible for protecting the village.

The Qiang Insect Tribe hosted the duo to the best of their ability. It seemed this wasn’t their first time receiving humans, as they appeared quite experienced.

The two sat cross-legged as ants worked in teams to carry enormous bowls, utensils, fruits, and decorative flowers for their enjoyment.

Lu Yang took a bite of a fruit whose name he didn’t know. It was crisp and refreshing. Sipping the juice from the bowl, a chilling sensation slid down his throat. These were local specialties of the Demon Region, delicacies unavailable in the Central Continent.

Fireflies acted as bonfires, gathering together like a river of stars and presenting a picturesque sight. From above, it looked like the two sat amidst the Milky Way.

The sole imperfection was the dance segment, where swarms of mosquitoes danced before their eyes. Fortunately, Meng Jingzhou’s willpower was astonishing, and he resisted the impulse to swat the mosquitoes away.

It was a lively night.

Early the next morning, uninvited guests barged into the Qiang Insect Tribe.

A large contingent from the Jiang Insect Tribe arrived. Among them, one human-form insect sat arrogantly upon a leaf, regarding the Qiang Insect Tribe’s chieftain with contempt, not even bothering to step down from the leaf.

He was Qing Dong, son of the Jiang Insect Tribe’s chieftain.

He noticed two hills not far from the Qiang Insect Tribe and was somewhat puzzled. I don’t remember them being there during my last visit.

Forget it, no point overthinking it.

“I heard my fiancée nearly escaped yesterday. Is this true?”

“Nephew Qing Dong, you jest! Absolutely not!” the Qiang Insect Tribe Chieftain flatly denied.

Qing Dong’s eyes narrowed. “Are you suggesting that... I’m wrong?” Aura waves of the Level Four Qi Training Stage emanated from him.

The Qiang Insect Tribe Chieftain was astounded. He’s so young, yet already an expert at the Level Four Qi Training Stage! No such genius had ever appeared in the entire history of the Qiang Insect Tribe!

As the standoff continued, a deep voice boomed like thunder, shaking the earth. The insects were so frightened that they fell to the ground. Qing Dong himself fell from the leaf.

Within Qing Dong’s horrified gaze, one of the hills awakened. It slowly rose, like a great mountain springing up from the earth. The massive mountain blotted out the sun, casting them all into its shadow.

That’s not a mountain—it’s a person!

The person’s eyes shone brilliantly like two miniature suns. The oppressive pressure radiating from him made Qing Dong shudder in fear.

“How dare a mere Qi Training ant prattle on so insolently before this esteemed one?”

Chapter 564: Cover the Sky With a Single Hand!

Qing Dong’s teeth chattered uncontrollably, his entire body trembling like a leaf. He had never encountered such a terrifying presence. Even with the other party just standing there, Qing Dong was overwhelmed with a sense of suffocation and dared not even breathe properly.

He even stated my identity—an ant.

“You dare disturb this esteemed one’s peace? You truly are audacious!” Meng Jingzhou’s tiger-like eyes were naturally ferocious, and even the spirit qi of heaven and earth congealed around them.

Qing Hong was horrified. Solidification of spirit energy—this is a power unique to Foundation Establishment experts who have transformed qi into their foundation! How did the Qiang Insect Tribe find such a powerful backer?!

“So annoying.”

The other colossal figure awakened, his voice languid and his expression icy. It felt like a sword was about to break free of its scabbard, the unsheathed segment radiating dazzling sword light that made everyone avert their gazes.

If Meng Jingzhou’s presence caused spirit qi to congeal, Lu Yang’s arrival imbued that solidified spirit energy with an austere and murderous aura.

An-Another Foundation Establishment expert...

Qing Dong felt as though he could die on the spot. Had I known the Qiang Insect Tribe had connections to two Foundation Establishment powerhouses, I would never have come here to force the marriage.

What does the Foundation Establishment Stage signify? The overlord of this five-li radius is an old mountain goat. Both the Qiang Insect Tribe and the Jiang Insect Tribe have to offer annual tribute to this old goat, praying for safety.

That old mountain goat is a Foundation Establishment expert!

Meng Jingzhou extended a hand, and it seemed like a great mountain slamming down toward the Jiang Insect Tribe.

Qing Dong resisted in desperation. He activated a secret art of the Jiang Insect Tribe and reverted to his original form, temporarily boosting his power from the Basic Level Four Qi Training Stage to the Advanced Level Four Qi Training Stage!

“If you kill me, Overlord Goat won’t let you off!”

“Noisy! What Overlord Goat? Even if he comes, this esteemed one would suppress him all the same.” Meng Jingzhou showed no fear, his large hand continuing its descent.

Seeing his threat fail, Qing Dong could only fight for his survival with all his might. “Whirlwind Sky-Piercing Break!”

Qing Dong spun madly, transforming into a small drill-like whirlwind. A cyan-colored gale whipped up, shredding the grass, plants, and leaves on the ground into pieces. With this move alone, no one in the Qiang Insect Tribe could hope to oppose him. Eyes bloodshot, he screamed as he charged toward the “gigantic” hand.

Unfortunately, before absolute power, any technique was futile. The gigantic hand possessed invincible strength. The Whirlwind Sky-Piercing Break struck its palm without causing even a hint of pain or itch.

Faced with Qing Dong’s attack, Meng Jingzhou’s eyes registered not the slightest fluctuation. He merely uttered a word calmly.

“Suppress.”

The Whirlwind Sky-Piercing Break proved ineffective, and Qing Dong even suffered a backlash, tumbling to the ground. He watched in despair as the hand drew nearer, painfully feeling the chasm between himself and a Foundation Establishment cultivator.

A Foundation Establishment expert can cover the sky with a single hand—figuratively and literally.[1]

Meng Jingzhou’s large hand halted less than an inch from Qing Dong’s head before he withdrew it impassively. He stood with his hands clasped behind his back and used a spell to summon a gentle breeze that rustled his hair and robes.

“Crushing you would be as simple as crushing an insect for this esteemed one. It would merely dirty my hand. You disturbed my peace. This time, it is only a lesson. If there is a next time, you shall atone for your sins with death.”

“Yes yes yes!”

This mighty expert is benevolent and refrains from slaughter. Having narrowly escaped death, how could Qing Dong dare to refuse?

The Qiang Insect Tribe Chieftain watched, dumbstruck. He never imagined these two were actually Foundation Establishment cultivators. Our small tribe has the fortune to form ties with these two experts? If word of this spreads, who would dare provoke us?

Chi Shui gazed at Meng Jingzhou’s towering figure in admiration. This is the image of a mighty expert in my heart. Without such strength, how can I speak of protecting the one I love most?

I’ve made up my mind! After this matter is over, I will temporarily leave the tribe, venture into the outside world, and cultivate until I reach the same heights as this expert!

“Which fellow Daoists are making a ruckus in this esteemed one’s territory and even intending to unleash slaughter here? Isn’t that going too far?” An old voice sounded from the distance, startling both the Qiang Insect Tribe Chieftain and Qing Dong.

It was the old mountain goat’s voice. They had only managed to catch a distant glimpse of him during his birthday banquets. Those worthy of sitting beside the old mountain goat were peerless experts at the Level Eight or Level Nine Qi Training Stage. Among them were numerous geniuses with a chance of breaking through to the Foundation Establishment Stage—a staggering one-in-ten chance!

An old mountain goat with sleek fur emerged from the mountain forest. Witnessing this, members of both tribes knelt in unison. The old mountain goat ignored the weak insect tribes, his gaze fixed on Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Only cultivators of the same level are qualified to speak with me.

He had been in the middle of cultivating when he sensed a terrifying sword qi flash briefly in the southern part of his territory. Clearly, a Foundation Establishment cultivator had entered his land.

Compared to the demon beasts in the jungle, the demon beasts in the Demon Region possessed even stronger territorial instincts. An uninvited arrival without a proper explanation could be viewed as a declaration of war.

The three great cultivators stood tall upon the land. The insects on the ground looked up at these beings who far surpassed them in both cultivation and stature, their hearts filled with reverence.

“Hmph.” Lu Yang snorted coldly. “This esteemed one thought it was some remarkable being. So it’s merely a Foundation Establishment livestock. So what if this esteemed one kills, and so what if I don’t?” Even his nasal tone carried the sharpness of sword qi, making the old mountain goat shudder.

“This oppressive pressure... You are Golden Core mighty experts!” the old mountain goat cried out involuntarily. Others couldn’t sense it, but he could feel Lu Yang’s oppressive aura clearly. It was like the abyss and the oceans, far beyond what an Establishment cultivator like himself could compare to. Moreover, the aura of Meng Jingzhou, who stood beside Lu Yang, was not a whit weaker.

“What? They are Golden Core mighty experts?!” The Qiang Insect Tribe Chieftain’s expression changed drastically; he was so surprised he nearly fainted.

By what virtue or worth of mine do I deserve the privilege of conversing with Golden Core Venerables, even conversing freely with them for an entire night?

What glorious honor have I brought upon my ancestors!

“Golden Core Stage!!!” Qing Dong’s legs trembled again as he recalled the scene earlier. He had assumed Meng Jingzhou held back out of respect for the old mountain goat. From the looks of it now, Overlord Goat is nothing before them.

It was truly a close shave that I kept my life.

“Old Ancestors, thank you for gracing us with your presence. I apologize for failing to welcome you. Could I invite you to my humble abode for a seat?” The old mountain goat put on a fawning smile, his demeanor shifting a full one hundred and eighty degrees as he extended an invitation to the two guests.

He had been fortunate enough to meet three or four Golden Core cultivators, but compared to these two, they were as different as mud to clouds. Could these two be Intermediate Golden Core experts? Then it’s all the more important to befriend them. Even if that’s unachievable, forming positive ties for good karma is essential.

Lu Yang nodded inwardly. Just as I said last night, don’t show off in front of insects. You should at least find a Foundation Establishment cultivator to support your performance. He had intentionally released sword qi earlier to lure the old mountain goat over.

Plan successful.

“A visit is unnecessary. We had a chat with the Qiang Insect Tribe and were guests here last night. It was quite pleasant.”

The old mountain goat hurriedly nodded. “I also think the Qiang Insect Tribe is excellent. Although they are insects, their perseverance is astonishing, and their future holds great prospects. I have often wished to invite their talented youths to my home, but never found a suitable opportunity.” How could the old mountain goat not understand? They’re hinting to me to look after the Qiang Insect Tribe.

“Good that you understand. You may depart.” Meng Jingzhou waved his hand, chasing the old mountain goat away, who left looking extremely delighted.

The Jiang Insect Tribe also seized this opportunity to leave this dangerous place quickly. What if these two suddenly remember what happened just now and change their minds, deciding to kill us instead?

“Alright, it’s time we take our leave as well.” Lu Yang stretched lazily. Having spent a night with the Qiang Insect Tribe, he had witnessed many novel things.

“Please wait, esteemed ones. I have something to give you.” The Qiang Insect Tribe Chieftain gritted his teeth as he resolved himself. Our tribe accidentally discovered this treasure. With our abilities, we certainly can’t protect it, and it may easily bring calamity upon us. Rather than that, it’s better to gift it to these two lifesaving benefactors.

The warriors of the Qiang Insect Tribe dug up a command token from the ground and carried it over.

The token was old and simple, its surface still flecked with soil yet to be cleaned away. A glance was enough to tell it was a valuable item with history.

“This is...” Lu Yang hesitated slightly. Indeed, good people are repaid with good rewards. This token doesn’t look ordinary.

The Qiang Insect Tribe Chieftain motioned for those around to withdraw. He looked up earnestly at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou and spoke solemnly. “We discovered this by accident while digging the ground when our tribe was established. It is said that possessing this token grants access to the hidden treasure site of a Half-Step Nascent Soul old ancestor!”

Even if these two are mighty experts at the Golden Core Stage, the treasure location of a Half-Step Nascent Soul old ancestor should be tempting, right?

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

1. The idiom essentially refers to someone extremely powerful, such that they can blot out the sky with a single hand. ☜

Chapter 565: The Legendary Command Token

“Half-Step Nascent Soul Stage?”

Lu Yang picked up the token. It looked older than he and Meng Jingzhou combined.

The term “Half-Step Nascent Soul” sounds intimidating, just like the real Nascent Soul Stage, but when you get down to it, isn’t it still just the Golden Core Stage? With the combat prowess of us brothers, aside from our cultivation realm not being Nascent Soul, all our other metrics belong to the Nascent Soul Stage.

Any random Nascent Soul cultivator who met them would have to address them politely as “fellow Daoists.” If it were someone without a backbone, their calling the two “Senior” wasn’t out of the question. And if it were someone who knew their true identities, the other party shouting “Give me your life!” wasn’t entirely impossible.

A Half-Step Nascent Soul cultivator’s treasure is truly a chicken rib to us—hardly worth any value.

Even Divine Transfiguration cultivators’ treasures held little appeal to them.

What is my status? I, Lu Yang, am the Heavenly Court Creed’s Young Creed Leader, major shareholder of One More Time Barbeque Shop, and owner of the flying carriage patent. It’s no exaggeration to say I earn buckets of gold daily.

Even a freeloading second-generation rich kid like Meng Jingzhou isn’t qualified to compare with me.

Meng Jingzhou also felt the token was of little use.

I, Meng Jingzhou, am the Meng Family’s Eldest Young Master. It’s not an exaggeration to say I’m the number one prodigal wastrel in the world. Even the slightest thing that slips from my hand could spark a fierce competition among Divine Transfiguration experts.

Even a hustler like Lu Yang, who just got lucky by attaching himself to Big Senior Sister and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, isn’t qualified to compare with me.

“In that case, thank you, Chieftain.”

It’s best to accept the tribe chieftain’s kind gesture. If outsiders learn that a weak tribe like the Qiang Insect Tribe possesses such an item, it would bring catastrophic disaster upon them.

“If I may ask, how did you know this could open a Half-Step Nascent Soul’s hidden treasure site?”

“The corpse of a demon was found beside this token. The corpse’s flesh had been gnawed clean by demon beasts, leaving only a skeleton, a piece of paper, and this token. Our tribe was built right above this skeleton.

“The paper was similar to a diary. It stated the function of this token—to open the entrance to the hidden treasure site—and that the treasure site’s owner is a mixed-blood white snake named Old Ancestor Bai Tan. However, it did not specify the treasure site’s location.”

“I see.” The two didn’t ask further. It seemed the other party didn’t know much about the token.

Demon beasts were a special existence among demons. They possessed pure bloodlines but low intelligence, or rather, they lacked even basic sentience. Since the power of demons was rooted in bloodlines, these demon beasts were often incredibly powerful.

Lu Yang suspected the reason for their low intelligence was inbreeding. Marriage between three generations or five degrees of kinship was extremely common among demons. On the other hand, they wouldn’t even be able to obtain a marriage certificate in Great Xia.

The two set off, heading in the planned direction to meet up with Third Senior Sister Gan Tian.

They stuck Divine Travel Talismans to their legs. These were useful items they had exchanged for at the Great Mission Hall, highly popular among disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. As venturing outside could easily attract trouble, the Divine Travel Talismans could help them quickly escape dangerous situations and preserve their lives.

Setting that aside, Divine Travel Talismans were unmatched for expediting travel on the road. When pasted on the calves, the Divine Travel Talismans’ power generated a propulsive force, pushing the user forward, saving them the effort while accelerating their speed.

Running at extreme speed for a full day, they passed many Foundation Establishment demon tribes along the way. The commotion they caused was so great that many old Foundation Establishment demons came out to investigate. Upon seeing their divine speed, they hurriedly hid back in their lairs.

A glimpse was enough to discern that the two were of a higher cultivation. The demon race had many arrogant individuals; merely glancing at them could be viewed as an insult, easily provoking thunderous rage and inviting calamity.

Not good, not good.

“Hmm? There are so many demons here, but it doesn’t look like a tribe. Is this the marketplace Grandpa Ba mentioned?”

The demon race had no cities, but they often needed to exchange goods, leading to the birth of marketplaces. Those capable of setting up a marketplace in the Demon Region were often hegemons of their region, wielding absolute power over the surrounding tribes. As for being charming, resourceful, and socially adept, that was secondary.

“Let’s check it out.”

The demon race’s marketplace—this is also something new.

The marketplace was filled with shapeshifted demon beasts. According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, this was one of the standardization measures implemented by the Five Ancient Immortals—using human form for interaction.

The demon race varied greatly. The large ones, like the Kunpeng fish-bird, could be hundreds of li long, while others were small, like the Jinwu Golden Crows or Jade Rabbits. Not to mention some had no hands or feet, and their habits for clothing, eating, living, and traveling differed. When diverse demons mingled, these issues were magnified, leading to many disputes over size and appearance in ancient times.

Later, the Five Immortals governed the world, establishing a human-centric principle. Whenever different demon races gathered, they were to assume human form. While the Five Immortals had vanished one after another, their influence persisted to this day.

Shapeshifting wasn’t about taking on a complete human form. With the Qilin Immortal as an example, many demons retained traits of their race when transforming, like rabbits keeping their ears, cats keeping their tails, and so on.

There were also fully shapeshifted demon beasts, so Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou didn’t stand out in the marketplace.

“Come take a look! Arid Qi Pills refined by Master Golden Monkey; five hundred spirit stones each!”

“What? They’re Master Golden Monkey’s pills? Master Golden Monkey is a great Foundation Establishment pill-concocting master with a one-third success rate!”

“Sabers and staffs forged by the Bronze Rhino Tribe! Quality guaranteed! Buy more, save more—bulk purchase discounts available! We even have magical treasures personally refined by the Bronze Rhino Tribe Chieftain! Wield one, and a Basic Level Eight Qi Training cultivator might defeat a Basic Level Nine Qi Training cultivator!”

“What? Such a massive improvement? That’s enough to bridge an entire level!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

What kind of shoddy wet market is this? What junk are they selling? A one-third success rate? If this were at the Pill Cauldron Peak, Seventh Elder would have beaten them to death.

And magical treasures refined by the Bronze Rhino Tribe Chieftain? They’re riddled with impurities and flaws. Even Lu Yang, who doesn’t understand artifact refinement, could craft a better one.

“There aren’t any experts in this marketplace. It’s a bunch of Qi Training cultivators and the few occasional Foundation Establishment cultivators.”

With the duo’s rich combat experience, a brief glance was sufficient for them to roughly gauge the demons’ cultivation levels from their gait and breathing.

“Never mind. This place should have a pawnshop. Let’s just sell the command token.”

The two found a pawnshop in the most bustling area.

The pawnshop rarely opened for business, but when it did, the profit could sustain it for half a year. The servant boy was bored out of his mind, dozing off. On his head were two big horns that resembled a water buffalo’s. He hadn’t received any valuable items in these two months, just worthless trinkets. The boss had even gone inside to sleep.

“Hey lad, help us see how much this command token can sell for.” Lu Yang took out the token from the front of his robe and handed it to the shop assistant.

The shop assistant was initially indifferent, sweeping a cursory glance over it. But then, his eyes seemed glued to the token, unable to move away.

“This...this...” Upon examining the token, his heart missed half a beat.

If this is truly that legendary treasure, we would make a fortune!

Noticing Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s bland reactions, he reckoned they didn’t recognize its value. He quickly called for the boss, who had been lying around asleep.

Hearing the shop assistant’s description, the boss shot up from his bed.

If this is the real thing, we wouldn’t have to open for business for ten years!

It was unclear what race the boss belonged to. He had a single pure white horn on his head and snake scales on his neck; perhaps he was a mixed-blood demon.

The moment he laid eyes upon the command token, his hands trembled, nearly dropping it.

This is actually the famous treasure token of Old Ancestor Bai Tan!

It’s the legendary Old Ancestor Bai Tan, who was only half a step away from the Nascent Soul Stage!

Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s eyelids twitched slightly.

Why are they reacting as if Old Ancestor Bai Tan isn’t at the Half-Step Nascent Soul Stage but the Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation Stage?

Chapter 566: YouYou are Nascent Soul Old Monsters!

Who was Old Ancestor Bai Tan? He was the legendary Half-Step Nascent Soul cultivator, an unattainable goal for countless demons. One must know that even the marketplace’s lord was only at the False Core Stage. Upon meeting Old Ancestor Bai Tan, the marketplace lord would have to respectfully address him as “Senior.”

When Old Ancestor Bai Tan attempted his breakthrough to the Nascent Soul Stage, something went awry. He perished, his Dao dissipated, and his storage ring was shattered, leaving behind only a command token.

He was meticulous, having divided his wealth into two parts—one in his storage ring and another hidden away, accessible only with the token. This token had been the object of fierce competition between numerous tribes, changing hands multiple times before somehow ending up buried beneath the Qiang Insect Tribe.

Rumors claimed the hidden treasure site contained Old Ancestor Bai Tan’s cultivation insights and reflections on his mental state before his breakthrough. Both were priceless treasures that Golden Core demons would give up everything to obtain.

These tribes had once searched extensively for the token but found no clues, and the efforts eventually fizzled out.

The pawnshop boss never expected the token to appear here. He broke out in a cold sweat.

His initial thought had been to sell it to the marketplace lord and seek his protection. But he calmed down and gave it a second thought. If the marketplace lord receives this token, would he protect or silence me? Wealth can sway any demon’s heart. Even with his good reputation, the marketplace lord might commit evil acts under the temptation of profits.

If I’m not selling it to the marketplace lord, all the more I dare not sell it to others.

“Boss, how many spirit stones is this worth?” Lu Yang waited and waited, but the only result was the boss sweating more profusely, still without any answer.

Hearing Lu Yang’s voice, the boss snapped out of his daze and hastily pushed the token back. “Worthless! Absolutely worthless! We won’t take it!” This is a hot potato—taking it means death.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou found it baffling. What’s with the extreme reaction? Was Old Ancestor Bai Tan really a Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation cultivator?

After the two left, the boss’s brows were tightly furrowed as he made a tough decision.

“Boss, what are you doing?” the water buffalo shop assistant shouted.

“Selling a piece of information to the marketplace lord.”

~~~

Departing the marketplace, the two ran for another half a day. As large Golden Core tribes appeared, the number of marketplaces increased. Without exception, these marketplaces knew the rules of the Demon Region and dared not get involved with items belonging to Golden Core old ancestors.

With the token frequently surfacing in marketplaces, more and more people began setting their sights on Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou—two careless fellows.

However, none of these individuals made a move. They weren’t qualified. Several Golden Core old ancestors had already targeted the duo, waiting only to kill them and seize the token.

“Youngsters, it seems you’ve gotten your hands on some good stuff.” Finally, a Golden Core old ancestor could no longer restrain himself and revealed his true form—a cyan-faced ferocious tiger.

He flew in the sky, looking down at them coldly. Two little fellows who can’t fly—at most, they’re at the Foundation Establishment Stage. Foundation Establishment cultivators are mere playthings before a False Core cultivator.

“Fellow Daoist, hogging the feast isn’t appropriate. Senior Bai Tan’s treasure is massive. Are you sure you can swallow it alone?” Another three Golden Core cultivators emerged, planning to join forces to seize the token and split the spoils afterward.

“It’s the Three Snake Bandit Clans!” a Foundation Establishment cultivator hiding in the dark exclaimed involuntarily. These three Golden Core cultivators are notorious, committing robbery and murder without hiding their identities. Yet, they’re absurdly strong, all at the False Core Stage. Together, they could challenge an Advanced Golden Core cultivator.

“How dare three patterned snakes dare covet what this esteemed one has eyes on?!”

Blazing infernos erupted in the jungle. Several Foundation Establishment cultivators screamed in agony as they were burned alive. A male lion with flaming fur appeared. It was the local overlord, the chieftain of the Blazing Savage Lion Tribe.

Shortly after, Golden Core experts turned up one after another. The Foundation Establishment cultivators below watched, dumbstruck and not even daring to breathe heavily. freewebnovel.com

All the nearby Golden Core cultivators had come.

“Old lion, do you really think you control everything?”

“Try and you’ll see!”

The Golden Core old ancestors glared at each other, exchanging threats, releasing their aura waves, comparing their cultivation realms, and trying to overwhelm each other with their oppressive aura. They completely ignored the two below, old ancestors at the Eighth-Layer Golden Core Stage.

“They really think nothing of us.” Lu Yang sighed. Forget we’re at the Eighth-Layer Golden Core Stage; even if we are at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, these old fellows wouldn’t be enough.

“Enough talk! Let’s witness the truth through action!”

The old fellows paid no attention to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou below, focused on fighting among themselves in the sky.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou yawned. These old fellows’ foundations are severely lacking and riddled with flaws. Their fight has nothing worth watching. Any two random participants from the Golden Core category of the tournament’s finals could fight better than them and put on a better show.

Or rather, any two random contestants could defeat this bunch.

“Want one?” Since they were idle anyway, Lu Yang took out two fruits from his identity jade pendant. He had bought them at a marketplace. They looked novel and were supposedly a specialty of the Demon Region. Due to their extremely short shelf life, they spoiled easily, but their taste was sublime.

As Meng Jingzhou took a bite, juice squirted out three zhang away.

“Wow, I gotta say, this tastes pretty good! So juicy, so sweet!” Meng Jingzhou praised the unknown fruit effusively.

Lu Yang held the fruit and thought for a moment, then used the Water-Splitting Technique, instantly turning the fruit into dried fruit. He took a bite. Though it lost its juiciness, it gained an even sweeter flavor.

The two ate their fruits and dried fruits while waiting for the battle above to conclude. We’re Eighth-Layer Golden Core old ancestors, after all—how could we act lightly? Experts always make their move last.

After finishing a few fruits, the battle neared its end.

“Conjure some water; help me wash my hands,” Lu Yang said. His hands were sticky from the fruit.

Meng Jingzhou conjured two water spheres. They washed their hands before standing up, preparing to act.

“Heh, I never expected so many people to covet this old man’s command token.”

Before the two could make a move, an aged voice reverberated through the jungle, startling the Blazing Savage Lion and the others. None of them had sensed the other party’s aura!

“Who is it?!” the Blazing Savage Lion roared in fury. I was moments away from victory.

“You covet this old man’s item, yet you are asking who I am?” A hundred-zhang-long old white snake with murky eyes appeared, hissing as its tongue flicked.

“This old man is Bai Tan.”

“What?!”

“How is this possible?!”

“Old Ancestor Bai Tan, who perished eighty years ago?!”

Gasps broke out one after another. Be it the Golden Core old ancestors in the sky or the Foundation Establishment experts on the ground, all stared at Old Ancestor Bai Tan with shock and doubt.

Old Ancestor Bai Tan had hidden in another space, which meant he could utilize the power of space at a rudimentary level.

This is the hallmark of the Nascent Soul Stage!

Old Ancestor Bai Tan is already a Nascent Soul old monster!

“I’m still short of the Nascent Soul Stage. It’s just that I obtained some paltry benefits when I failed in my advancement eighty years ago.” Old Ancestor Bai Tan smiled modestly, but no one dared to think he was truly being humble.

Despite failing the advancement, he gained spatial power—what terrifying talent!

“So many Golden Core cultivators are enough for me to refine a furnace of Nascent Transformation Pills! Combined with the treasures accessible with the token, I have a seventy percent chance to advance to the Nascent Soul Stage!” Old Ancestor Bai Tan flicked his tongue, his gaze greedy.

Eighty years ago, his breakthrough failed disastrously. Fearing enemies would exploit his vulnerability, he faked his death to escape and preserve his life. To make his feigned death convincing, he even left the command token behind.

Unfortunately, the token changed hands too frequently. With the multiple back and forths, he lost track of it and was wracked with regret. It was his hope for a second attempt at breaking through to the Nascent Soul Stage.

Fortunately, the heavens never close all doors. Yesterday, he heard two young demons had gotten hold of the token and were inquiring about its price everywhere.

A heaven-sent opportunity.

The token’s appearance would inevitably attract many Golden Core cultivators. With their sheer numbers, even he couldn’t handle them all. He could only wait until the battle ended and their energy was depleted before showing himself to claim the final victory.

“What cunning! Lying low for eighty years and using these two juniors as bait to lure us into fighting and mutual destruction, so that you can profit from within.” The Blazing Savage Lion glared fixedly at Old Ancestor Bai Tan, deliberately stalling for time while secretly preparing a backup plan. By activating a talismanic treasure, he could temporarily leap through spatial dimensions and flee.

Old Ancestor Bai Tan couldn’t be bothered with the Blazing Savage Lion’s actions. In his eyes, these Golden Core cultivators were already dead. I’ve disrupted the space; these Golden Core cultivators can’t escape.

This is the gap between the Half-Step Nascent Soul and Golden Core stages.

Time to reclaim what is mine.

Old Ancestor Bai Tan opened his bloody maw and lunged at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. “Two little fellows, hand over this old ancestor’s command token obediently! In return, I will grant you a painless death.”

Lu Yang didn’t speak. He silently extended a single finger. A barely perceptible wisp of sword qi condensed at his fingertip. Then, he made a gentle slashing motion toward Old Ancestor Bai Tan.

An extremely fine line appeared on the snake’s tongue.

Plop.

A section of the snake’s tongue fell to the ground, sizzling with smoke—it was steeped in deadly venom.

An extremely fine line appeared on Old Ancestor Bai Tan’s lower jaw.

It too fell to the ground.

“Flying up there must be tiring. Come down, all of you.” Meng Jingzhou chuckled.

He executed the Heaven-Shaking Six Forms, throwing a powerful punch.

Space trembled. The Golden Core cultivators were terrified as they dropped like dumplings into boiling water.

Old Ancestor Bai Tan crashed to the ground with a thunderous boom, knocking down countless trees.

He couldn’t care about the pain. The situation before him instilled more panic in him. The figures of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou reflected in his pupils grew larger and larger. He cried out in terror and shook uncontrollably, a chill emanating from the depths of his soul. “Condensing qi into swords! A single fist that shatters the heavens!

“You...you are Nascent Soul old monsters!!!”

I thought I was the hunter—the oriole stalking the mantis stalking the cicada. Never have I imagined these two young demons to be Nascent Soul old monsters!

“What? They are actually Nascent Soul old monsters?!”

“Why would Nascent Soul old monsters be so leisurely?!”

“Shush! Do you wish to anger the Nascent Soul old monsters?!”

Everyone shuddered in fear. Nascent Soul old monsters are capricious and overwhelmingly powerful, capable of covering the sky with a single hand. Every one of them is a great demon whose name shakes their territory!

Lu Yang, “...”

Although I knew showing off would be easy in the Demon Region, I never expected it to be this easy.

Is this the cultivation world in Big Senior Sister’s eyes?

Chapter 567: Fragments

The domineering old demons who usually commanded the winds and clouds now trembled in fear, not even daring to breathe heavily. In the past, encountering a Nascent Soul old monster was rare, happening once every few years. This time, they had not only encountered one, but two.

“This token is yours, right?” Lu Yang asked casually, swinging the token by its string in a circle.

“Yes... No no no! It belongs to you, Your Excellency!”

“I heard this token can open a hidden treasure site. Is that true or false? What did you hide in there?” Meng Jingzhou was curious. With such grand fanfare, there should be good stuff.

“It is true. The hidden treasure site contains this little one’s cultivation insights and the materials needed for my next attempt at breaking through to the Nascent Soul Stage.” Ever since losing the token, Old Ancestor Bai Tan had secretly spread information, luring others with profits as bait to help him search for the token.

“That’s it?”

Half-Step Nascent Soul cultivation insights? The Dao-Seeking Sect’s scripture library has several shelves filled with them, available for anyone to read. The half-baked cultivation insights of someone like Old Ancestor Bai Tan aren’t even qualified to be placed on those shelves.

As for materials needed for a Nascent Soul breakthrough, they mattered even less. What materials are required for shattering one’s golden core to form a nascent soul? The Dao-Seeking Sect has no such tradition.

“Y-Your Excellency, this little one truly did not know your identity! Had I known, I wouldn’t have dared to act this way even with ten thousand times the courage!” Old Ancestor Bai Tan felt like dying. He kowtowed violently with loud bangs, as if he wished he could knock his head off.

The other old demons followed suit, kowtowing to express their loyalty.

Truth be told, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had never witnessed such a scene since they entered the world of cultivation.

So satisfying!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy popped up, seizing the opportunity to broaden Lu Yang’s horizons. “Eh, this is nothing. Back when I traveled incognito, I often encountered such situations.

“Generally, they’d see I wasn’t easy to bully, so they’d bring out their backer, boasting about how powerful this backer was. After I defeated the backer, they’d bring out the backer’s backer. This would repeat until the ultimate backer appeared. Bystanders would often introduce this backer, saying he was one of the subordinates of one of the subordinates of the Heaven Mandate Immortal. They claimed he wielded immense power with direct access to an immortal.

“After that, the ultimate backer would see me and stammer things like ‘I-it’s you!’ ‘This lowly one has eyes but no pupils and failed to recognize you, Immortal; please forgive my sins.’ ‘Spare this little one just this once!’ and so on, while slapping himself hard and kowtowing vehemently, as if they wished they could shatter the planets. Sometimes, they’d even place righteousness before family, slaughtering the troublemaker.

“When the ultimate backer kowtowed, others would follow suit, resulting in a vast sea of people kowtowing all at once—it was quite a spectacular sight.

“Finally, I’d mete out punishment based on their crimes—sometimes direct execution, sometimes severing their foundation, or other penalties.

“It’s a pity your cultivation still isn’t enough to witness such scenes.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clicked her tongue, feeling regretful for Lu Yang. This is a treatment only immortals can enjoy.

Lu Yang looked helplessly at his mental space, which had transformed into a tropical rainforest.

After arriving in the Demon Region, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had tried to match the mood of the new environment by transforming the pink mental space, where giant trees shot up, verdant and luxuriant. She often slept on the branches without falling off.

Now, she had built a swing. Wearing stirrup leggings, she swayed back and forth, her dainty little feet dangling in rhythm.

“Immortal Fairy, what about those troublemakers you met before becoming an immortal?”

“That would typically lead to two scenarios.”

“Which two scenarios?”

“One, the other party’s cultivation was higher than mine, and I couldn’t beat them, so I could only run.

“Two, although their cultivation was inferior to mine, I would always end up being chased down through a twist of fate.

“Sometimes, when there were many pursuers, they often fought among themselves. I ran into such situations two or three times. They would surround me, blocking escape routes in all directions. When I could no longer get away, disputes rose over who should deliver the killing blow, and they’d start fighting. I would slip away amidst the chaos.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, your experiences are truly bizarre.

Meng Jingzhou asked quietly, “How should we deal with these old demons?”

With their ruthless behavior, their hands are surely stained with blood. Under Great Xia’s law, they would all receive the death penalty. But this is the Demon Region, and its customs are like this. We can’t possibly exercise cross-regional jurisdiction and forcibly impose Great Xia’s law on them. That’s not how the immortal sects’ enforcement authority is supposed to be used.

Besides, if we were to kill them all, the territories they govern would fall into turmoil, inevitably leading to war and the deaths of many innocent demons.

Suddenly, the exquisite snake mark on Old Ancestor Bai Tan’s brow flashed, casting a spiritual consciousness projection. It vibrated, stunning all demons except Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

A magnificently adorned white snake appeared, looking much younger than Old Ancestor Bai Tan and brimming with greater vitality.

“You are?”

“I am Bai Gu of the White Snake Tribe. Greetings to you two fellow Daoists. This Bai Tan is one of my clones. My original intention was to reclaim him after he broke through to the Nascent Soul Stage, which could aid my advancement to the Divine Transfiguration Stage. It seems Bai Tan encountered a life-threatening danger, triggering the mark I left behind.

“Please spare Bai Tan’s life, fellow Daoists. In return, I’ll offer you this fragment!”

Lu Yang had heard of this cultivation method—refining a clone whose cultivation achievements would be transferred to the main body. Female cultivators practicing Blissful Union arts even used this method to pose as twins, increasing amorous pleasure and boosting cultivation speed.

“What is this item?” freewebnovel.com

“Legends say there are three such fragments. When combined, they formed a key to a certain secret domain. Unfortunately, I never found the other two fragments. By my observation, your fortune and fate are profound, fellow Daoists. You are destined for greatness. I believe you will find the remaining two fragments.”

Before Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou could respond, a mark also flashed on the cyan-faced tiger’s brow, casting a spiritual consciousness projection.

A brightly striped tiger with wings appeared. Seeing the cyan-faced tiger unconscious, its expression twisted, clearly shocked.

As he surveyed the surroundings, he noticed Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and Bai Gu. Cupping his fists, he implored, “I am an administrator of the Qiongqi Tribe. This is my unfilial son. I do not know what he has done to offend you, but I beg you to be magnanimous and spare his life.

“In return, I’ll gift you two this fragment.

“Legends say this fragment is the key to a Divine Transfiguration-level secret domain. Unfortunately, I never found the remaining fragments despite all these years. May I exchange this fragment for my son’s life?”

The flame mark on the Blazing Savage Lion’s brow flickered. An old lion whose eyelids could barely open appeared. Seeing the most outstanding descendant of his tribe unconscious, he knew it was the work of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

He was the old ancestor of the Savage Lion Tribe. The Blazing Savage Lion was the junior he saw the most promise in, which was why he had supported him to become the tribe chieftain. He couldn’t stand by and watch the Blazing Savage Lion be killed.

The old lion produced a fragment. “This is a fragment I obtained by chance. Gathering all three fragments forms the key to a Divine Transfiguration-level secret domain. I wonder if this can be exchanged for his life?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

“Why don’t the three of you see if your fragments can fit together?”

Chapter 568: Third Senior Sister

For a moment, the atmosphere became rather awkward.

When the first fragment appeared, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had originally intended to accept it. After all, it led to a Divine Transfiguration-level secret domain. Perhaps there might be treasures within that Divine Transfiguration cultivators wouldn’t recognize.

The fragments were hard to collect. Bai Gu of the White Snake Tribe had searched for years without finding the other two. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had prepared to spend a year or so in the Demon Region, leisurely collecting the fragments as they played. By then, they would have just reached the Nascent Soul Stage, making it perfectly reasonable to venture into a Divine Transfiguration-level domain.

However, the two didn’t expect the set of fragments to be completed in less than a minute.

“Bai Gu! Jin Xuan! So the other two fragments were in your hands all along!” The old lion flew into a rage. His eyes snapped open and blazed like torches while his fur bristled.

“Old lion, how do you have the nerve to say that?! You hid this fragment well enough!” Jin Xuan, the Qiongqi Tribe’s administrator, was equally furious. He had searched for the other two fragments for over a hundred years, traversing every corner of the Demon Region and almost wearing his legs out, only to realize the fragments were right at his doorstep.

Even through the spiritual consciousness projection, Lu Yang could feel the murderous intent from the three.

Combining the three fragments could open a Divine Transfiguration-level secret domain. This was far more valuable than any clone, illegitimate son, or talented junior. They absolutely could not hand it over!

The three fragments sensed each other’s presence and vibrated violently, shooting out at incredible speed to converge above Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“Oh no!” The three old demon monsters were horrified, blood draining from their faces. They never expected the fragments to be so mystical, breaking free from their control and flying to Lu Yang’s side.

How could they voluntarily surrender a fortuitous opportunity that had fallen into their hands? There was no such kindness in the Demon Region!

“Don’t panic! Even if the two of them obtain the key, it’s useless because they don’t know the secret domain’s location!” Bai Gu sneered. What use is the key alone if they don’t know the door’s location?

Even I don’t know the secret domain’s location.

“The foremost priority now is to intercept these two and seize the key back!” The three of them were great demons at the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage. They refused to believe they couldn’t defeat the two fellows who were also at the Nascent Soul Stage!

“Makes sense.” The other two demons concurred. They had let anxiety get to their heads earlier.

The three fragments collided above Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, forming a white jade disc. Beneath their feet, white light erupted, corresponding to the patterns on the disc.

Boom!

The ground cracked, rumbling incessantly. The two quickly jumped aside.

“The secret domain is right beneath their feet!” Bai Gu’s eyes widened so much they nearly bled from anger.

“Quick! Call any Divine Transfiguration cultivators you know! The three of us alone can’t stop these two!” Bai Gu yelled. Three against two is an easy win, but capturing them is another matter.

Initially, he thought there was plenty of time; they would eventually catch them after trying a few times. But now, the secret domain was right under their noses! We have no time to try a few times. We urgently need Divine Transfiguration cultivators to act. They can have the meat, and we might still get some soup.

The three old demons acted decisively, dispersing their spiritual consciousness projections to seek out their acquaintances at the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

It was more convenient for Bai Gu and Jin Xuan. Their backers within their tribes were Divine Transfiguration cultivators. The old lion needed to ask for help elsewhere.

“So this is the key to the secret domain?” Lu Yang pointed at the white jade disc floating above them with a peculiar expression.

“Judging by their reactions, yes.” Meng Jingzhou’s expression was equally priceless.

Within moments, winds stirred and clouds roiled within an eight-hundred-li radius. Whether someone had leaked the news or some Divine Transfiguration cultivator feared they couldn’t compete alone and called for reinforcements, the opening of the secret domain attracted countless Divine Transfiguration cultivators.

Numerous Divine Transfiguration cultivators were interested in a secret domain left by a peer at the same level. Perhaps there were treasures inside that could assist them in elevating their cultivation realms. Setting that aside, cultivation techniques from a peer were also very valuable.

Whoosh, whoosh, whoosh! Mysterious figures radiating astonishing auras appeared one after another, each with their unique forms, and they were all Divine Transfiguration demons!

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou swallowed hard. Against one or two Divine Transfiguration cultivators, that wouldn’t threaten our lives—if we can’t win, we can just run.

But a whole nest of them? Even the most talented Golden Core cultivator is powerless.

“The white jade disc is in the hands of these two juniors?” An Advanced Divine Transfiguration qiongqi bared his fangs, staring coldly at the duo.

“Senior, it is indeed them!” Jin Xuan lowered his head, replying while kneeling on the ground.

A giant white snake coiled in the sky. It had two bumps on its head, showing signs of transforming into a dragon. He was the Divine Transfiguration cultivator from the White Snake Tribe that Bai Gu had invited.

A skywolf capable of devouring the moon in ancient times, a giant ape that could carry mountains on its back...

As Divine Transfigurations emerged one after another, Bai Gu, Jin Xuan, and the old lion shuddered with fear. Any one of them could easily sweep aside all three of us and forcibly annex our territories without us even daring to fart!

This is the difference in power of one major realm!

Among the three demons, Jin Xuan was the strongest, with his prowess at the Half-Step Divine Transfiguration Stage. However, he could only keep his head down and behave in such a situation, not daring to make any conspicuous movements.

The unconscious Golden Core old ancestors and Foundation Establishment old demons gradually woke up. Seeing the numerous Divine Transfiguration experts in the sky, they wished they could fall unconscious again.

Divine Transfiguration experts are so elusive that we may not see one in decades. How long have we been unconscious? What happened? Why are there so many Divine Transfiguration experts?

Did we exhaust our lifespans just for this opportunity to see them?

“This is a bit tricky. Had I known earlier it’d be like this, I might as well have carried the old horse here.” Meng Jingzhou clicked his tongue. “How about you perform a set of Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist?”

We were just showing off in front of Golden Core demons. How did so many Divine Transfiguration cultivators gather in the blink of an eye?

This isn’t the right script. Where’s the Nascent Soul Stage transition? At least let us kill a few Nascent Soul cultivators first, then have the Nascent Soul cultivators call the Divine Transfiguration cultivators over—that would be more like it.

Lu Yang revealed a troubled look. “We haven’t even met Third Senior Sister yet. Wouldn’t it be inappropriate to summon Big Senior Sister already?” We’re here to help Third Senior Sister with her archaeological work, not to sweep through the Demon Region.

Just as Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou didn’t think much of this group of Divine Transfiguration cultivators, they likewise didn’t think much of the duo. They’re merely two slightly talented Golden Core juniors—not worthy of our attention at all.

“Let’s kill these two juniors first. We’ll discuss how to explore the secret domain later.”

“Sure.”

The Divine Transfiguration cultivators quickly reached a consensus. Their auras surged, killing intent running rampant.

Lu Yang sighed. There’s no other choice then. They insist on forcing me to call Big Senior Sister over.

Suddenly, the melodious sound of a guqin resounded through the sky, its notes tinkling and clinking like a stream flowing over stones, inexplicably calming and soothing the restless hearts.

“Did I permit you all to kill?”

After the music faded, a graceful figure in cyan robes appeared before Lu Yang, blocking all the killing intent. She was peerlessly beautiful, holding a guqin with a languid posture. A black cloth blindfolded her, adding a touch of enigma.

“It’s her!”

“Damn it! How could it be her?!” freewebnovel.com

“Isn’t she being hunted by various tribes? Yet she still dares to show herself?!”

The Divine Transfiguration cultivators’ pupils constricted. They became agitated, and their gazes toward the cyan-robed figure were overcome with panic and disbelief, a wave of terror spreading among them.

This is a ruthless character even Fusion cultivators can’t handle! She’s not someone we, mere Divine Transfiguration cultivators, can provoke!

“Run!”

The Divine Transfiguration cultivators didn’t hesitate and fled immediately.

Clang! A guqin string was plucked. Space shook, and everyone was frozen mid-air, unable to move even a finger. Unconcealable fear filled their eyes.

“Did I allow you all to run?”

“Third Senior Sister?” Lu Yang asked tentatively, a trace of pleasant surprise in his voice.

He had seen her portrait before.

“It is me.”

“Senior Sister, why did you come here? We were just about to look for you!” They were still several hundred li from the location she had provided.

Gan Tian’s tone was one of helplessness. “Big Senior Sister sent me a message saying you two probably wouldn’t come find me obediently, and that if there was any major commotion these few days, it’d likely be your doing. She told me to look for you to prevent any accidents.

“How did you two manage to attract so many Divine Transfiguration cultivators?”

Lu Yang gingerly replied, “...If I said this was all a coincidence, would you believe me?”

“Yes, I believe you.”

“You believe me?” Lu Yang was overjoyed. I’ve never met Third Senior Sister before, yet she trusts me so much.

“Mmm. That’s what I always tell Big Senior Sister when I cause trouble in the Demon Region.”

Chapter 569: Ready-Made First-Meeting Gift

Among the various tribes, Divine Transfiguration cultivators were at least core members, wielding considerable influence. Some were even chieftains, with numerous Nascent Soul cultivators flocking to them. Their power was immense, and when combined, such a force could run rampant across the Demon Region, disregarding all rules. freewebnovel.com

This was how Divine Transfiguration cultivators were viewed in the eyes of the Foundation Establishment experts and Golden Core old ancestors—Divine Transfiguration cultivators were the heavens.

However, the Divine Transfiguration cultivators knew that compared to true cultivators, they were mere ants.

Just like now.

The legendary Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden had appeared. With a single move, she had frozen them all mid-air, rendering them utterly immobile. They could only watch helplessly as the trio chatted and laughed.

“In the past, many accidents occurred during my travels in the Demon Region. I relied entirely on Big Senior Sister to act as my safety net and clean up after me. Now, my cultivation is different. I no longer need Big Senior Sister; I can handle things on my own.” Gan Tian smiled.

Ah, this is growth.

“As for you all...” She turned her head. Although her eyes were covered, she could still acutely observe her surroundings. “All of you have struggled and fought your way through the Demon Region for many years. You should understand its rules: those who kill will eventually be killed. Since you attacked my junior brother, there is no need for you to remain alive.”

“Wait—” The qiongqi desperately tried to break free, hoping to beg for mercy. But he had only uttered one word when Gan Tian plucked the guqin strings again.

Sound waves transformed into invisible threads, slicing the Divine Transfiguration and Nascent Soul cultivators in the sky into pieces. Chunks of flesh from the mangled bodies rained down with a grisly blood shower, striking the earth with sickening thuds.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou swallowed their saliva. Third Senior Sister’s methods are truly brutal.

“What’s the big deal? This is how people killed in ancient times,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy testified. The ancient era was even more dangerous than the Demon Region now. Countless cultivators and demons perished every day.

The Foundation Establishment and Golden Core demons who had just woken up were dumbstruck. The lofty Divine Transfiguration cultivators had been slaughtered so easily. Their minds couldn’t process such shocking information immediately.

After a few seconds, one demon finally screamed and fled frantically. The remaining demons seemed to have been jolted from a dream and also scrambled to escape.

Never mind where we run to—just getting away from here is enough!

Gan Tian had no interest in these small fries and let them leave.

With the rabble either dead or gone, Gan Tian continued observing Lu Yang. Sensing his solid foundation, a trace of wistfulness stirred within her. She shook out a tablecloth, spread it on the ground, and gestured for the two to sit and not to be overly reserved. “Your cultivation progress is pretty rapid. I heard that when you formally became Shifu’s disciple, he happened to be missing, and Big Senior Sister personally taught you.

“You’re so lucky. I also wanted Big Senior Sister to teach me, but the timing was never in my favor.

“I asked Big Senior Sister to send a fellow disciple well-versed in ancient history. I didn’t expect her to send you. To think you’ve become an ancient history scholar recognized by Big Senior Sister at such a young age.”

Lu Yang smiled obsequiously. “It’s all luck, all luck.”

Gan Tian waved her hand, encouraging Lu Yang. “How can you call it luck? Don’t belittle yourself. Luck is only part of it. Your achievements today were built on your hard work.”

Lu Yang thought about it. That’s indeed the case. If I hadn’t worked hard to pass the Immortal Fairy’s trials, I wouldn’t have survived until now.

Gan Tian then turned to Meng Jingzhou, her tone slightly teasing. “Since he is Lu Yang, you must be the eldest young master of the Meng Family? I heard from Big Senior Sister that with your Single’s Spirit Root, you are bold to innovate, forming two Single’s Golden Cores and even mastering Nirvana True Fire to accelerate your cultivation speed, completely unafraid of wavering willpower and falling into Qi deviation. Even diabolic cultivators wouldn’t dare do that! Your Dao heart devoted to pursuing the immortal Dao places you above everyone else!

“As your senior sister, I ought to bring a gift for our first meeting, but I came in a rush. How about this—I’ll open this secret domain and take you inside to find some good stuff.” A senior sister should act like one; I can’t shortchange them.

The secret domain’s entrance was right beneath their feet. She summoned the white jade disc floating in the air. “This secret domain was likely left behind by a Divine Transfiguration cultivator of the Suanni[1] Tribe. Back then, he was a renowned Divine Transfiguration cultivator in the Demon Region and considered a genius. He was high-spirited and arrogant, wiping out several small tribes on a whim. Unfortunately for him, he provoked a powerful entity he shouldn’t have. The formidable enemy attacked, and the suanni was no match and died resentfully in the north. His defensive supreme treasure, the white jade disc, was shattered by the enemy into three pieces, scattered across the Demon Region.”

Gan Tian sighed. “I also tried to search for the white jade disc fragments, but to no avail, and this matter was shelved. I never expected you two youngsters to assemble it today.”

“...Indeed, I also never expected to assemble it.” Lu Yang could swear on his conscience that he did nothing. The white jade disc simply flew into my hands by itself. “Senior Sister, don’t secret domains usually have cultivation realm restrictions? Can you enter a Divine Transfiguration-level secret domain?”

Gan Tian shook her head. “What you’re describing are secret domains left as providence for later generations. With cultivation realm restrictions set in place, future generations must pass the trials within to earn rewards. This secret domain is the suanni’s personal stash. As long as you can open it, you can enter and exit freely. There are no restrictions.”

“I see.”

“Secret domains left as providence for later generations are rarer in the Demon Region but more common in Great Xia. It’s not your fault for having this misconception.”

“Why are they common in Great Xia?”

“There are two reasons. First, some cultivators are particular about fate and prepare for cultivation in the future. If a junior can benefit from their secret domain, they will form positive karmic ties with them, which can reduce the damage suffered during future lightning tribulations.”

“What’s the second reason?”

“In Great Xia, inheritance taxes are mandated by law. Some cultivators are unwilling to pay it and choose to set up a secret domain for fated individuals. This counts as a gift and is not taxed.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Gan Tian hefted the white jade disc in her hand. “This disc is actually quite useful. It’s just that its grade is too high, so you two can’t use it. Otherwise, I’d give it to you.” I’m not like Big Senior Sister, who can place several layers of seals on the white jade disc, letting them unlock one by one as Lu Yang’s cultivation increases.

~~~

The secret domain’s entrance was a vortex of black with specks of starlight. If one rashly charged in without the key, even if the vortex didn’t shred them to pieces, the intruder would be teleported to an unknown location, fraught with danger.

Gan Tian activated the white jade disc effortlessly, as if she already knew how to use it. The white jade disc connected with the secret domain entrance. After she gently twisted it, the entrance opened.

“Done.”

“Senior Sister, you seem very familiar with how to use the white jade disc?” Lu Yang asked uncertainly.

“What’s the big deal about that? When I fought that suanni, he kept using this disc. I watched a few times and learned.”

“...You were the one who killed that suanni?”

“Did I not mention that? Oh right, I said he provoked a formidable enemy. It’s the same thing.”

1. The suanni is a mythical beast that resembles a lion and is said to be one of the dragon’s nine sons. Motifs of the suanni are often seen as decorations on incense burners. ☜

Chapter 570: Enjoying the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s Treatment in Advance

“Back then, I had just arrived in the Demon Region. I was alone and unfamiliar with the place. That suanni saw me as an easy target to bully and tried to take liberties with me. In a fit of rage, I slew him. That suanni was a prodigy of his tribe. Being slain in front of all the other prodigies was a massive loss of face—naturally, the Suanni Tribe wouldn’t let it slide. I had to flee for a long time.”

“What happened after that?”

“After that, I asked Big Senior Sister to help me fight back. Now, the Suanni Tribe is much more well-behaved—at least on the surface.” Gan Tian smiled. Many are chasing me down; perhaps among them are killers secretly sent by the Suanni Tribe.

Hearing that Gan Tian had entered the Demon Region at the Divine Transfiguration Stage, easily slew a demon prodigy of the same level, and evaded the Suanni Tribe’s pursuit, Lu Yang found her truly remarkable.

~~~

The three entered the secret domain. Inside, the sky was smothered with yellow sand, and tornadoes raged with giant rocks mixed within. Anyone swept inside would meet certain death.

The wind was so powerful that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were nearly blown away. Moreover, visibility was extremely low within the sandstorm, and extending one’s spiritual consciousness was hard.

“These are Wind-Stilling Pearls. Take one each.” Gan Tian gave each of them a cyan jade pearl. Holding the pearls, their bodies felt lighter, as if the wind around them had disappeared, allowing them to move freely.

“It’s not that the wind around you has disappeared; the Wind-Stilling Pearls release wind in the opposite direction, counteracting and canceling out the wind in your surroundings,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained casually. “The suanni’s talents and abilities lie in winds and fog. These two pearls were likely refined from the skulls of suanni.

“Fine treasures.”

Gan Tian reminded them loudly, “Follow me closely, else you’ll easily get lost.”

“Third Senior Sister, you can see the path ahead clearly?”

“Not by sight; I can sense it. Since coming to the Demon Region, I’ve covered my eyes to train my other four senses, no longer relying on my eyes or spiritual consciousness.”

As one’s cultivation increased, their five senses and spiritual consciousness would become sharper. But to advance further, relying solely on improvements in cultivation wasn’t enough; one must deliberately train their senses.

“Senior Sister, did you decide to train your four senses after seeing the fog in the Central Continent and the Demon Region?” Meng Jingzhou recalled the fog before entering the Demon Region.

“Yes, the fog served as a reminder.”

“In that case, Senior Sister, do you know why the Demon Region stands vertically on the Central Continent? And what about the East Sea, Buddhist Kingdom, and Extreme North?”

“I knew you’d ask this question. Time is tight now. I’ll explain it to you slowly after we get out.”

“Time is tight?”

“Mmm. If the old fellows know I showed my face here, they’ll definitely send people to kill me. We’d best leave the secret domain before they arrive.”

“Senior Sister, did you expose your identity as a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect?” As a cultivator with dual identities—disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect and the eldest young master of the Meng Family—Meng Jingzhou was always mindful of his safety, taking Grandpa Ba’s advice to heart.

“That I didn’t. I’m being hunted on my own merits.” As Gan Tian spoke, she swung her guqin, batting away large flying rocks with ease.

“We’re here.”

The three arrived before a stone chamber. An unknown array surrounded it, blocking the sandstorms and tornadoes. It was so quiet it felt like another isolated world.

Crouching before the stone chamber were two suanni statues carved from stone. Sensing strangers, they assumed defensive postures, ready to attack.

Gan Tian didn’t even glance at them, shattering the statues with two slaps. She picked up two half-finished keys from the rubble, combined them into a complete key, and opened the stone chamber.

Lu Yang’s eyes narrowed. These two suanni statues aren’t simple. At full power, they can briefly unleash combat strength rivaling that of a Basic Divine Transfiguration cultivator. If only Meng Jingzhou and I had come to this secret domain, these two stone statues alone would have given us a big headache.

“As I thought, this is a place only we two Nascent Soul cultivators can enter.”

The stone chamber door opened with a rumble. What greeted their eyes was a small pile of spirit stones, along with several dual cultivation manuals.

The Suanni Tribe was a branch of the dragons. They inherited the dragon’s inherently lustful nature and were addicted to dual cultivation. This was why that suanni initially provoked Gan Tian.

Aside from these, there were all sorts of natural treasures, the assortment dazzling one’s eyes. freewebnovel.com

Meng Jingzhou picked up a bronze-colored fruit. It felt like ice-cold jade to the touch, and he could sense the vitality contained within. “Is this Wood-White Gold-Jade?”

Wood-White Gold-Jade was a natural treasure that had existed since ancient times. The conditions for its formation were extremely strict. Only the roots of spirit plants that had developed sentience could absorb earth-metal qi to produce this fruit. It greatly benefited Metal Spirit Root cultivators, increasing their vitality and control over metals.

Based on what Meng Jingzhou knew, only the Five-Elements Sect currently had such fruits. They were produced by spirit plants growing on their Metal Branch and had a very low yield. “Could it be that this suanni killed a Five-Elements Sect disciple, murdering for loot...”

“I don’t think so,” Lu Yang said from the side.

“Why?”

Lu Yang picked up a piece of paper nearby and shook it. “This is a purchase certificate issued by the Five-Elements Sect. If there’s a quality issue, you can return the product.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Why does the Five-Elements Sect stick by the book more than our Meng Family?

Lu Yang picked up another piece of paper. “This is a debt note from the suanni. He borrowed a lot of money from the merchant guild to buy the Wood-White Gold-Jade. It’s probably a bad debt now.”

The suanni didn’t have Qin Haoran’s ability to transfer karma, whereby whoever picked up the debt note would become the new debtor. He was only one of the Suanni Tribe’s prodigies. Competition within the tribe was fierce, and there were some things they needed to earn, snatch, and borrow by themselves!

“Perfect then. I’ll give this fruit to you. It can enhance your sword qi.” Meng Jingzhou tossed the fruit to Lu Yang.

“Alright, quickly use your identity jade pendants to collect everything. You can sort through it slowly and pick what you like after we get out.” With her rich experience of being hunted, Gan Tian estimated that time was almost up. If they lingered any longer, it would be too late to escape.

Hearing this, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou activated their identity jade tablets, sweeping away all of the suanni’s bequest.

Gan Tian took out a piece of beast hide, had the two sit on it, then charged through the sandstorm and out of the secret domain.

Boom! The moment the three emerged, they were assaulted with fierce attacks. The beast hide swayed precariously, nearly falling.

“Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden! Let’s see where you can run today!”

“Surrender your life!”

“With the countless evil deeds you have committed, you will surely be vanquished today!”

Several Fusion cultivators blocked the secret domain’s exit. Their accumulated, charged-up strikes bombarded the beast hide, startling Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

We are merely at the Golden Core Stage. How are we already enjoying the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s treatment in advance?

The onslaught of attacks continued. The beast hide was riddled with holes, and the three people on it gradually faded.

“Oh no! This is an illusion created by the Mirage-Clam Pearl!”

“You think you can catch me with the likes of you?”

The illusion shattered. Gan Tian sneered and transformed into a streak of light, seizing the chance to break through the encirclement.

This scene reminded her of the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s first lesson.

“Little Gan, as my third disciple, the first thing you must learn is how to escape.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s teachings had played a pivotal role in helping her narrowly escape death numerous times.

Chapter 571: An Immortal’s Secret Art!

“Stop there! Don’t let her escape!”

“Prepare to die!”

“Kill her!”

A group of Fusion-Stage demons roared in pursuit behind them, their bloodlines stimulated to the extreme. Multifarious powers rained down like a storm, striking empty ground. The earth rumbled, forests collapsed in swathes, and clouds of dust billowed upward.

Whoosh! Gan Tian skillfully piloted the beast hide, darting out from the smoke and dust and leaving the pursuers far behind with dust in its wake.

She didn’t forget to reassure Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. “Don’t be afraid, junior brothers. I learned flight techniques from Fifth Elder. Although I’m not as proficient as he is, it’s more than enough to shake off these few pursuers.”

Gan Tian erected a barrier on the beast side, shielding them from the wind’s impact, but the rapid speed was still something Golden Core cultivators couldn’t endure.

Moreover, Gan Tian’s flight path was genuinely not something ordinary individuals could withstand. Put nicely, it was like a butterfly dancing gracefully. Put bluntly, it was like a tornado spinning wildly—even more ferocious than when Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and Man Gu fused and spun together.

Fortunately, the two had experience riding Fifth Elder’s speeding flying shuttle, so they didn’t pass out immediately this time.

Along the way, Gan Tian continuously launched attacks rearward—some real, some feints—wearing down the pursuing Fusion cultivators until they gradually gave up the chase.

“Told them they couldn’t catch me, yet they insisted on chasing. A waste of time,” Gan Tian grumbled as she made a temporary landing. She had set up a base nearby. “Hey, you two, are you alright?”

After landing, Gan Tian noticed her two juniors swaying unsteadily, unable to stand firmly.

“I'm...f-fine...never mind, I’m not fine.” They tried to stubbornly claim they were fine, but their bodies betrayed them—they collapsed and passed out.

Gan Tian shook her head helplessly. She controlled the beast hide to roll the two up and brought them to her hideout.

Lu Yang heard the sporadic sound of rain outside and struggled to open his eyes. His mind felt like a mass of glue paste, unable to recall what had happened before he lost consciousness. He stared blankly at the cave ceiling until a drop of water formed and fell onto his face. Only then did he reluctantly turn his head, gradually remembering what had transpired.

He turned his head and saw a pair of legs... They’re Meng Jingzhou’s. His gaze passed over Meng Jingzhou to see a crackling bonfire and Gan Tian sitting beside it.

In the dim cave, the flickering firelight cast Gan Tian’s shadow, elongating and shortening it rhythmically. The shifting shadows on her face presented a different sense of beauty. Gan Tian strummed her guqin and hummed softly. Her voice was melodious and pleasing to the ear, creating a comfortable sensation as if one was immersed in water and supported by an invisible force.

“You two are awake? It looks like your physical constitution is better than I’d estimated.” Gan Tian smoothed the guqin strings, a smile tugging the corner of her mouth. This melody was her original composition, possessing the effect to calm the soul and soothe the mind.

The reason the two had woken up early was also related to the remains of the Epoch Immortal gifted to them by Shangguan Yu.

“We two?”

Both Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had woken up at almost the same time. Lu Yang was facing Meng Jingzhou’s feet, and naturally, Meng Jingzhou was facing Lu Yang’s feet.

The two sat up abruptly. The aftereffects of the high-speed ride had yet to dissipate; a wave of dizziness nearly sent them crashing back to the ground.

“Don’t rush, you two. Catch your breath first.”

“Where is this?”

“It’s a hideout I established a hundred years ago. It seems my luck is not bad; no one has discovered it in all these years. It’s very safe.

“Those old monsters won’t give up. They’ll probably search this area for a few days before they’re willing to leave. The three of us can take this chance to rest and recuperate here.

“We left in a hurry earlier. Now that we have time, we can sort out the treasures we picked up in the secret domain.”

Hearing this, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou opened their identity jade tablets, pouring out a large pile of natural treasures.

Lu Yang casually picked up the Wood-White Gold-Jade, munching on it as he rummaged through the other treasures. As he consumed it, the effects of the Wood-White Gold Jade integrated into his body, enhancing his sword qi and vitality. And as his vitality increased, the dizzy feeling gradually faded.

“Let’s split these spirit stones equally.” Lu Yang divided the pile of spirit stones in half.

“These cultivation manuals are for you.” Meng Jingzhou handed Lu Yang a large stack of manuals.

Lu Yang glanced at them—they were dual cultivation manuals.

“What would I need these for?”

“Then would they be any more useful to me?”

Lu Yang thought about it and felt Meng Jingzhou had a point. He took the manuals, flipped through a few randomly, and showed a look of disgust.

Orthodox dual cultivation techniques involved the mutual complementation of yin and yang. However, the suanni only possessed unorthodox techniques focused on plundering yin to supplement yang, which were utterly pernicious.

“Let’s burn them.” Lu Yang casually threw the manuals into the fire, and they quickly turned into a pile of ashes.

“Hmm? There’s something inside the manuals?”

Characters from the cultivation manuals drifted out within the flames, gathered together, and transformed into a sheet of golden paper that remained undamaged despite the flames.

Lu Yang was stunned. Looks like this is the true cultivation technique hidden within the manuals. It can only be revealed through burning.

“Break first, then build—could it be a coincidence?” Lu Yang murmured as he reached directly into the fire to retrieve the golden paper.

The paper was covered in dense, small characters. It was indeed some kind of cultivation technique.

“This is...”

“What is it?”

“An immortal’s secret art!”

“What?!”

It wasn’t just Meng Jingzhou; even the silently meditating Gan Tian was taken aback. No one expected such an astonishing secret art to be hidden within the dual cultivation manuals.

This yang-boosting technique was written in ancient language, and only Lu Yang could fully understand it.

“What type is it?”

“Yang-boosting technique.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Are you pulling my leg?

“Wait, why would immortals need a yang-boosting technique? Which immortal had to boost his yang?”

Meng Jingzhou reacted, recalling an ancient rumor. “Is it the Heaven Mandate Immortal? I heard he could manage a hundred women every night, had a fetish for married women, and could impregnate countless women in a single night!”

Lu Yang stared at Meng Jingzhou in surprise. Where did this rumor come from? Aren’t you afraid the Heaven Mandate Immortal would strike the rumormonger with lightning during their tribulation?

After an immortal died, their Dao Fruit wouldn’t vanish. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was a prime example. Lu Yang couldn’t determine whether the Heaven Mandate Immortal was still alive based on the existence of heavenly tribulations alone.

“It was for the Qilin Immortal. He had two wives.” Lu Yang revealed the true intended user of the yang-boosting technique.

“Qilin Immortal?”

“People often call him the Demon Immortal. His true form is a qilin, the only one in the world. He had two wives, one from the Dragon Tribe and one from the Phoenix Tribe. This yang-boosting technique was developed by the Demon Immortal’s two wives.”

Gan Tian revealed a surprised expression. There’s a theory in academia that the Demon Immortal’s true form was a qilin, but without concrete evidence, no one dares to be certain.
