This theory has been questioned since its inception. But judging by Little Junior Brother’s tone, he sounds very sure. Could it be that he possesses definitive evidence?

As for the Demon Immortal having two wives, I’ve never heard of it despite all my years researching ancient history.

There were indeed two unparalleled experts from the Dragon and Phoenix tribes in ancient times who reached the Half-Immortal Stage. Is Little Junior Brother saying these two were the Demon Immortal’s wives?

No wonder Big Senior Sister sent him here. Although Little Junior Brother’s cultivation isn’t high, his understanding of ancient history is truly profound.

Chapter 572: Little Junior Brother, What You’ve Said Is Wild Unofficial History?

“Little Junior Brother, have you heard of the battle between the Demon Immortal and the two Dragon and Phoenix ancestors?” Gan Tian recalled a certain legend, thinking perhaps her little junior brother had a different version or interpretation.

“The three of them fought?” Lu Yang thought to himself, Didn’t the Qilin Immortal kneel on sword arrays every day? Were you three fighting in bed?

“Yes, it’s rumored to be a battle between the Demon Immortal and the Dragon and Phoenix tribes for a position in immortal ascension. In other words, it was a battle for immortal ascension. It’s famous in history, ranking among the top ten battles of peerless experts. Many scholars wish to conduct deep research on that battle. However, existing records of that battle are very vague, making research fraught with difficulties.

“Multiple ancient texts record that the Demon Immortal and the two Dragon and Phoenix ancestors were all half-immortals. The three possessed the power to obscure the heavens and battled among the stars. They fought until heaven and earth dimmed, the sun and moon lost their light, the world plunged into a darkness where one couldn’t see their hand before their eyes, and pandemonium swept across the populace. In the end, the Demon Immortal, fighting one against two, paid the price with his life and won the battle. He changed the heavens and replaced the sun, allowing the world to regain light.”

“Immortal Fairy, are you familiar with that battle?”

“What kind of question is that? Those two dragon and phoenix lasses are my unofficial disciples, while the Qilin Immortal is someone I have beaten since childhood. I have close bonds with all three. How could I not have spectated such a major battle?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt Lu Yang had underestimated her. I always care for my friends.

“It wasn’t just me—Heaven Mandate, Epoch, and Nine-Layers were all watching from the side. That battle was indeed pretty fierce. The Qilin Immortal’s combat prowess was fearsome. Despite fighting one against two, he didn’t get beaten to death.

“Originally, it was a three-way melee. But as they fought, the two Dragon and Phoenix lasses found that the Qilin Immortal was the toughest to deal with and needed to be taken out first, so they joined forces to attack him.

“The Qilin Immortal was severely injured, beaten until his face was bruised and swollen. It was unsightly beyond words. He realized this wouldn’t do and that everyone below was watching. If this image of him got out, how would he show his face in public again?

“During the fight, he intentionally or unintentionally moved closer to the sun and moon, nearly frightening the Jinwu Golden Crow and Jade Rabbit to death. With three half-immortals battling, even a slight brush would lay them up for half a year, and two brushes would lay them up for a lifetime. The Jinwu Golden Crow and Jade Rabbit quickly fled with the sun and moon.

“After they fled, heaven and earth turned pitch black because there was simply no light. We could see the Qilin Immortal’s battle, but mortals and ordinary cultivators couldn’t. The Qilin Immortal’s plan had succeeded.

“Fighting one against two was still challenging for the Qilin Immortal. Fortunately, there was no light at the time. Otherwise, if the sight of him being pummeled had spread, he’d probably have wanted to die on the spot. My painting skills are superb, so I seized the opportunity to draw the scene. The Qilin Immortal asked me for the painting many times, but I never gave it to him.

“As the Qilin Immortal was beaten by me since childhood, he had robust vitality. The Survival of the Fittest Incipient Dao Fruit allowed him to grow stronger the more he fought, which made it very suitable for prolonged battles. And you know about burning lifespan, right? It’s essentially an offensive method that trades injury for injury. The Qilin Immortal used his Incipient Dao Fruit to adapt to burning lifespan beforehand. The result was that he could elevate his combat power without reducing his lifespan.

“Toward the end of the battle, the moves of the two Dragon and Phoenix lasses had minimal effect on him. The Qilin Immortal emerged triumphant, and the two lasses conceded defeat wholeheartedly.

“After winning, the Qilin Immortal wanted to invite the Jade Rabbit and the Jinwu Golden Crow back, but they refused to return, no matter what. He had already scared them away, so how could asking them to return be easy?

“Out of options, the Qilin Immortal could only invite two different Jinwu Golden Crow and Jade Rabbit.”

Lu Yang, “...”

What a magnificent “sun and moon lost their light,” “changing the heavens and replacing the sun,” and “paying the price with his life.”

Lu Yang faithfully recounted the battle to Gan Tian, whose expression turned peculiar after listening to the story.

“Little Junior Brother, what you’ve said is...wild unofficial history?” This wild unofficial history is truly wild—it dares to spread such rumors about the Qilin Immortal.

“No, this is official history.”

Gan Tian, “?”

Seeing that neither Meng Jingzhou nor Gan Tian needed the immortal-level yang-boosting technique, and that he couldn’t damage it with his cultivation, Lu Yang could only keep it for now, intending to hand it over to the scripture library next time in exchange for contribution points.

“What’s this?” Lu Yang picked up a palm-sized cage. Chains locked a small golden suanni inside the cage. The little suanni resembled a flame, flickering and unpredictable.

Hearing Lu Yang’s description, Gan Tian quickly provided an answer. “This is a suanni’s essence soul, refined from a suanni’s soul. It’s already a dead object. If it’s absorbed, it can further stimulate one’s bloodline and grant even more powerful abilities. It seems the suanni I killed had murdered a fellow tribe member and intended to absorb their essence soul for his own use. But before he could do so, he was killed.

“Murdering a tribesman is a grave crime. Moreover, the suanni victim was definitely pure-blooded and of high status. So much time has passed. Even if we hand this over to the Suanni Tribe, I’m afraid they would only think I was making excuses.

“This was originally a Divine Transfiguration-level essence soul; you two shouldn’t be able to absorb it. But nearly two hundred years have passed. Even if it bears seals, they’re no longer effective. A significant portion of the essence has leaked out, and it’s now downgraded to a Nascent Soul-level essence soul, just right for you two to absorb.

“Junior Brother Meng, you can absorb this essence soul. Suanni are a race born from the union of dragons and lions. They innately possess characteristics of both dragons and lions, though their mastery is not complete. If you absorb a suanni’s essence soul, you have a chance to gain dragon and lion traits. In particular, you might glimpse parts of the renowned Fearless Lion Seal in Buddhist sects.”

“It’s yours.” Lu Yang passed the suanni essence soul to Meng Jingzhou.

Good brothers need not say thanks. Meng Jingzhou placed one hand over the cage while his other hand supported it. The suanni essence soul transformed into strands of golden light that entered his body through his Eight Extra Meridians. Beads of sweat appeared on Meng Jingzhou’s forehead, soon drenching his whole body. His teeth chattered as he engaged in fierce combat with the essence soul in his mental space.

“Just shout if you want to. I’ve set up seals in the cave; outsiders can’t hear anything inside,” Gan Tian kindly reminded him, feeling that Meng Jingzhou was suppressing himself.

The moment the words left her mouth, Meng Jingzhou seemed to have found an outlet to vent. His pupils narrowed into vertical slits, turning golden, and his throat trembled, emitting a sound beyond human capability.

Roar!

It was a lion’s roar.

“No dragon’s roar. It looks like what you mastered is the lion’s roar. A pity—dragon traits are far more powerful than lion traits. Nevertheless, it’s still not bad. This roar of yours has some of the flair of the Buddhist Lion Roar. I heard you also learned the Arhat Fist. Your affinity with Buddhism is deep. In the future, you may master the Fearless Lion Seal.”

“Umm, Senior Sister, if I may ask, what are these dragon traits you mentioned?”

“There are many. For example, summoning the wind and rain, robust physical body, riding clouds and mist, the dragon’s inherently lustful nature, and whatnot—all are good traits.”

Meng Jingzhou couldn’t help but feel there was one trait he absolutely must not acquire.

“It’s fine even if you acquire them. Big Senior Sister praised your willpower effusively. If you obtain that last trait and still preserve your primordial yang, your cultivation speed will definitely surpass Little Junior Brother’s.”

Meng Jingzhou shook his head vigorously, shuddering with belated fear. Luckily, I’ve already broken free from the Meng Family and accumulated virtue through kind deeds, thus narrowly avoiding this calamity.

Right now, I’m already struggling to hold it in. If I gain the dragon’s inherently lustful nature on top of that, even if the Hanging Monastery members take turns chanting scriptures for me, and Master Jiesha takes over my body, I wouldn’t be able to resist my physiological urges.

Chapter 573: Cage

“Cultivation is about pressing forward courageously, undaunted by hardships. Look at Shifu. He made enemies everywhere, and under immense pressure, his cultivation advanced by leaps and bounds, making him the number one of his generation.” Lu Yang advised Meng Jingzhou not to assume that avoiding the dragon’s inherently lustful nature was a good thing.

Such a mindset is detrimental to cultivation. The greater the pressure, the greater the potential—this is the principle I learned from Big Senior Sister, and this is the principle she learned from Shifu.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest had personally put this into practice, perfectly validating his theory, and even now, he still saw it through. This tireless spirit earned Lu Yang’s deep admiration.

Meng Jingzhou shot a glance at Lu Yang. Brat, you can say that easily because your waist doesn’t hurt when standing! Let’s swap places and see how you like it.

The suanni killed by Gan Tian truly lived up to being a prodigy; he had quite a lot of good stuff.

“Is this a bottle of Nascent Transformation Pills?” Lu Yang found a small vial and poured out a pill. It looked like the Nascent Transformation Pills described in books, which could help one break through from the Golden Core Stage to the Nascent Soul Stage. However, Lu Yang had never seen one in person as the Pill Cauldron didn’t refine such things.

“These three bottles are all Nascent Transformation Pills.”

“What kind of pill is this?” Meng Jingzhou found a pill stored alone in a small vial. Upon opening it, a pill fragrance assaulted his nostrils, smelling incredibly valuable.

“This scent... It should be Divine Concentration Pills, pills for breaking through from the Nascent Soul Stage to the Divine Transfiguration Stage.” Gan Tian sniffed the air and identified the pills.

Not long after, Meng Jingzhou came across another Divine Concentration Pill.

Gan Tian leaned against a stone wall and explained, “The suanni was already at the Intermediate Divine Transfiguration Stage. Divine Concentration Pills were useless to him. He probably accumulated these pills to win over subordinates.

“The Suanni Tribe is internally divided into many factions. To compete for the tribe chieftain position, one needs not only support from the higher-ups but also subordinates to serve them, such as by collecting materials and intelligence. I have seen many subordinates bullying the weak in small tribes under the guise of collecting materials. I killed them in passing, and that’s how I made some of my enemies.

“As for methods to win over subordinates, there are many. Some are based on pure trust, while some are through establishing life-and-death contracts or master-servant contracts, and there are also sacrificial soldiers and whatnot trained by the older generations.”

“By the way, Third Senior Sister, we were short on time in the secret domain, and you didn’t get to explain in detail. What exactly do the Central Continent, the Demon Region, the Buddhist Kingdom, the East Sea, and the Extreme North look like? Big Senior Sister also said to ask you directly if we encountered any strange phenomena at the border between the Central Continent and the Demon Region.”

Hearing Lu Yang bring up this topic, Gan Tian no longer leaned lazily against the wall. She sat up straight, her tone becoming solemn. “Actually, this isn’t something you should know at your cultivation level. But since Big Senior Sister said so, she must have her considerations. Let me confirm again—are you sure you want to know the answer to this question?”

The two nodded simultaneously. The question was right before them; not knowing the answer truly made their hearts itch with curiosity.

Seeing this, Gan Tian sighed. She casually drew a few lines in the air with her fingertip, forming an undulating and orderly continent, and labeled it the “Central Continent.”

“Most cultivators believe the world is flat, that whether it’s us, demons, or seafolks, we all live on one single continent. But that is not the case.”

As she spoke, a continent the same size as the Central Continent appeared to its east, standing vertically against it. This vertical continent was a vast ocean.

“This is the East Sea.”

To the west of the Central Continent, a continent shrouded in yellow sand rose from the ground, parallel to the East Sea continent.

“This is the Buddhist Kingdom.”

To the south of the Central Continent, a continent covered in towering mountains jutted up.

“This is our current location—the Demon Region.”

To the north of the Central Continent, a white continent stood tall, completing the final gap in the encirclement.

“This is the sparsely inhabited Extreme North.”

Gan Tian pinched the air, and a red, scalding sphere appeared between her fingers. She placed this sphere directly above the five continents.

“This is the sun and the moon.”

Gan Tian paused, then continued.

“There is one more continent, not recorded in any books. It’s a continent only high-level cultivators know about.”

A sixth continent appeared, covering the top of the box and sealing it.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou jolted simultaneously, their pupils constricting and their faces filled with disbelief.

“This continent is called the Spiritless Continent. As the name implies, it’s a land completely devoid of spirit energy and utterly worthless. Not only cultivators, but even mortals are unwilling to go to such a place.”

Spirit energy had the effect of clearing meridians and strengthening the body. If mortals went to the Spiritless Continent, their physical constitution would decline.

“You should have heard of the legend where the Ancient Nameless One refined the stars into the continent three hundred thousand years ago. But the Ancient Nameless One didn’t refine the stars into one continent—it was six. These six continents are indestructible, forming a cube that locks everyone inside.

“During this time, many cultivation experts attempted to break through the continents to reach the world outside, but without exception, all failed. Even cultivators proficient in spatial spells couldn’t penetrate the bottom layer of the continents. There are even rumors that not even an immortal can break the continents. Besides, it remains unknown why exactly the Ancient Nameless One did this.

“In fact, whether it’s six continents or one single continent makes no difference to cultivators. These six continents are vast enough that neither cultivation nor combat feels constrained.”

“This...” Although Lu Yang had long anticipated the existence of a sixth continent and suspected they lived in a gigantic, boundless box, witnessing it firsthand still felt like a fantasy.

He had long been puzzled about why the Ancient Nameless One refined the stars into continents. Now, this question that had perplexed him endlessly had its answer revealed—the Ancient Nameless One did it to lock something away.

Using stars as material and continents as barriers, the Ancient Nameless One constructed a box impenetrable by any power and so massive its size couldn’t be calculated.

“If you don’t believe me, you can go down and see for yourselves—that is if you know the Earth Escape Technique,” Gan Tian added. Many cultivators found the truth hard to accept upon first hearing it. Seeing is believing; it is understandable.

“I’ll go take a look.” Lu Yang didn’t hesitate, standing up and diving downward.

This wasn’t just his idea, but also the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s.

~~~

The continent’s barrier was very thick. At Lu Yang’s speed, it would take days. Fortunately, he was already at the Golden Core Stage and could achieve internal circulation, not needing to breathe for long periods.

The only problem was that continuously maintaining the Shrinking Earth technique would deplete his powers. But this problem could be solved with Great Rejuvenation Pills.

Employing the Shrinking Earth technique, he burrowed into the ground with a whoosh.

Three hours passed.

Lu Yang’s spirit energy was exhausted. He built a small space underground using the Draw Underground Prison technique and consumed Great Rejuvenation Pills here. After resting briefly, he continued his descent.

Repeating this twenty times, five days passed.

His descending body suddenly halted. It felt as if he had stepped on solid ground. Even with the Shrinking Earth technique, he could not proceed further.

He had reached the very bottom of the continent.

Chapter 574: The True Identity of the Ancient Nameless One

Many cultivators possessed the ability to reach the very bottom of the continent, but very few actually did so because the thought simply didn’t occur to them.

Lu Yang was no exception. He had never considered continuously using Shrinking Earth to reach the continent’s bottom and see the scenery on its other side. It was only after Gan Tian mentioned it that he took action.

The bottom of the continent was pitch black, and nothing was visible. Lu Yang wanted to use his spiritual consciousness to scout around, but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stopped him.

“Don’t use your spiritual consciousness to look. This thing isn’t something you can understand. Your mind wouldn’t even be able to endure a single glance.”

Lu Yang obediently retreated. Matters of immortals should be handled by immortals. I shall not get involved.

“Stay farther away. I’m afraid something unexpected might happen and implicate you.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was seeing something like this for the first time. From what that little lass Gan Tian described, its characteristic is being impenetrable. But who knows if it has other effects, like reflecting damage, refraction, and whatnot?

Lu Yang retreated once more.

“Why are you in such a hurry to run so far?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy called Lu Yang back again.

Lu Yang obediently returned. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gently tapped Lu Yang’s head twice, connecting them with her immortal consciousness. This way, no matter how far Lu Yang ran, they could still communicate as long as he didn’t leave the range of her immortal consciousness. However, to prevent Lu Yang from suffering mental shock, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t share her vision like last time.

“Alright, you can go now.”

After ensuring Lu Yang was in a safe zone, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy extended her immortal consciousness, analyzing inch by inch. Under her powerful immortal consciousness, the structure of the continent’s bottommost layer was presented before her eyes. The more she looked, the tighter her brows furrowed.

“There are two barriers set here, corresponding to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and the Immortal Stage respectively. The first barrier cannot be pierced by Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, and the second barrier cannot be pierced by immortals.”

“Is there none that corresponds to half-immortals?”

“The biggest difference between a half-immortal and a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator is whether one wields an Incipient Dao Fruit. You can think of half-immortals as a transition phase between the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and the Immortal Stage. If you master the Incipient Dao Fruit at the Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage, you’re a half-immortal. If you master it at the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage, you’re still a half-immortal.

“The difference between these two types of half-immortals lies in their base power. Only when a half-immortal fully condenses their Dao Fruit and becomes an immortal will their overall strength make a significant leap.”

“I see.” Although Lu Yang was only at the Eighth-Layer Golden Core Stage, he already possessed a vast amount of knowledge that even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators might not grasp.

“Such a complex structure. Who set this up?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gently knocked the first barrier. It was punctured, and countless runes flickered, converging into a beam of white light. The white light flashed, and the barrier returned to its original seamless state, as if it had never been damaged.

This process took less than half a breath.

When the Everlasting Immortal Fairy knocked the barrier again in the same way, the barrier showed not the slightest change, with not even a single scratch or gap.

“This is...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy hesitated.

“Immortal Fairy, is there a problem?”

“There are two types of Dao Fruits at work in this barrier.”

“Two types?”

“The Epoch Immortal’s Epoch Dao Fruit and the Qilin Immortal’s Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit. The Epoch Dao Fruit reverses time, restoring the damaged barrier to its original state. The Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit prevents the same attack from breaching the barrier again.

“Wait, that’s not right. This barrier’s strength also contains the Nine-Layers Immortal’s Yin-Yang Dao Fruit. The Yin-Yang Dao Fruit imbues the barrier with the concept of ‘Hardest,’ making the first barrier so hard that Transcendent Tribulation cultivators can’t pierce it, and the second barrier so hard that even immortal power can’t pierce it.”

The essence of Dao Fruits was to add a rule to the world. If the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wished, she could add an ‘Everlasting Rule’ to the world, granting everyone eternal life.

The barrier followed the same principle. The Epoch Immortal, the Qilin Immortal, and the Nine-Layers Immortal extended their Dao Fruits’ rules onto the barrier, causing it to become indestructible, the hardest existence even immortals couldn’t penetrate.

“It’s still not right. If these three Dao Fruits are present, I should have recognized them at a glance, not through repeated experimentation and deduction of the Dao Fruits from the phenomena...unless the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit is also involved.

“Yes, the Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit should be here too. The Heaven Mandate Immortal used his Dao Fruit to cast the ‘Immeasurable Tribulation,’ completely disrupting the rules of the other three Dao Fruits, shattering and reorganizing them.

“What’s the Immeasurable Tribulation?”

“It’s complicated to explain. You can understand it as the greatest and most chaotic tribulation. Once cast, even the Heaven Mandate Immortal himself cannot break it. Furthermore, casting the Immeasurable Tribulation on the barrier is akin to tying a dead knot. You can only cut the rope; no one can untie it.”

Lu Yang clarified, “That is to say that this barrier is the work of the Four Ancient Immortals, but even if you summon all four of them, they can’t remove the barrier?”

“That’s the idea.”

Lu Yang sucked in a cold breath. The Four Ancient Immortals were really ruthless. What were they trying to do?

“So, the so-called Ancient Nameless One is actually the Four Ancient Immortals?” If the barrier’s construction is the work of the Four Ancient Immortals, does that mean the Ancient Nameless One from the legend, who refined the stars into continents, is the Four Ancient Immortals?

Everyone has fallen into a fallacy—the Ancient Nameless One wasn’t one person but four.

“It was the four of them!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded affirmatively, a relaxed smile spreading across her visage. “I knew my death had nothing to do with those four.”

Lu Yang hesitated, feeling the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was jumping to conclusions too early. Can this really rule out the possibility of the Four Ancient Immortals joining hands to murder the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

“I naturally have my reasons for reaching this conclusion.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy changed the subject. “Do you know how to break this barrier?”

This was a cage laid down jointly by the Four Ancient Immortals. According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, even immortals couldn’t open it. All living beings would be forced to live inside this cage, life after life, generation after generation.

“How to break it?”

“The Immeasurable Tribulation is the biggest problem. It’s like a chest locked with ten thousand locks, and you hold ten thousand keys without knowing which key fits which lock. You need to use one key to open one lock, and you can’t fail in this process. One wrong attempt means starting over. It’s purely a matter of luck.

“To break the Immeasurable Tribulation, one must attack continuously with immortal-level power. But due to the presence of the Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit, immortal-level attacks cannot be repeated.”

“Then...” Lu Yang followed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s line of thought to devise a solution.

“So my existence is needed. My self-detonation isn’t restricted by the Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit. Every self-detonation method is different.

“To unlock the cage barrier, we Five Ancient Immortals must act simultaneously. The Heaven Mandate Immortal and I will crack the Immeasurable Tribulation, while the Epoch Immortal, the Qilin Immortal, and the Nine-Layers Immortal will undo the rule restrictions!”

Lu Yang’s mind buzzed. Combining the existing evidence and connecting everything, he envisioned the scene from three hundred thousand years ago and understood why the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could be certain the Four Ancient Immortals weren’t the culprits.

After the Everlasting Immortal Fairy died, the Four Ancient Immortals couldn’t find the culprit. At the same time, they weren’t able to resurrect the Everlasting Immortal Fairy for some reason. Thus, they joined forces to perform a world-shocking feat, refining the stars into continents. freewebnovel.com

This is a blatant message to the culprit: either resurrect the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to unlock the cage, or all of us shall stay trapped inside with no hopes of escape!!!

Chapter 575: The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s Two Lessons

The camaraderie of the Five Ancient Immortals deeply moved Lu Yang.

Laying down an unprecedented cage to trap the murderer within, whereby it can only be unlocked by gathering the power of all Five Ancient Immortals—what grand boldness, what a magnificent feat. Lu Yang was filled with admiration.

He had no other thoughts now; only one question remained. If the Epoch Immortal is gone, how are we supposed to gather the power of the Five Ancient Immortals?

This question also stumped the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. After contemplating a moment, she proposed a plan that sounded unfeasible. “How about you become an immortal and form the Epoch Dao Fruit?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, don’t you think you are overestimating me too much?

The rules of time are incredibly hard to master. The Epoch Immortal relied on his identity as the Jianmu World Tree and used his endless lifespan to grind slowly, trading time for time. Only then did he grasp the rules of time.

I’m only eighteen this year, and I’m already planning ahead to wield the Epoch Dao Fruit?

How do I master it? By taking over the Epoch Immortal’s corpse? Or will you teach me the temporal rules, Immortal Fairy?”

“It’s a pity that the fates of the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others are unknown. Even if they are alive, we have no idea where they’re hiding. Otherwise, we could seek them out directly and ask to get all the answers.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head regretfully, though Lu Yang could tell she was in good spirits.

Previously, the culprit’s identity was unknown and suspected to be one of the Four Ancient Immortals. After this investigation, the possibility of the Four Ancient Immortals was finally ruled out, allowing her to relax.

“Alright, time to go back.”

With the bottommost layer of the continent investigated, there was no need to stay any longer.

The human and the immortal fused back. Lu Yang employed the Shrinking Earth technique, swimming through the ground as if it were water. He pushed off with both feet, his hands pushing aside layers of soil, like a fish traver—

There was no traversal.

Lu Yang blinked. His movements were precise, but he just couldn’t swim upward.

With a spurt of energy, he pushed off with both feet again, his hands pushing aside layers of soil, like a fish traver—

There was still no traversal.

He looked down at the bottommost barrier of the continent. This thing is sucking me back. freewebnovel.com

Noticing Lu Yang’s predicament, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly realized something. “Oh, I forgot. This place has gravitational pull. You’re stuck.”

The Four Ancient Immortals’ methods were superb. Refining stars into continents wasn’t just kneading them together like clay. They also preserved gravity during the process, or perhaps, constructed a gravity array with spells... In any case, the continents have gravity.

“Use more strength, and you’ll go up.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy spurred Lu Yang on.

Descending hadn’t been strenuous for Lu Yang. At most, when his descent speed was too fast, he used “Draw Underground Prison” to slow it down.

But going up now was too troublesome. Lu Yang had no other choice but to strive to swim upward.

It took him five days to descend to the bottom, but thirteen days to return to the surface. He was left panting with exhaustion.

Fortunately, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s directions had prevented him from veering off course. If he had strayed even a little, he might have ended up in the territory of the Suanni or Qiongqi tribes.

“Your trip took quite a while.” Meng Jingzhou was meditating with his eyes closed, but he woke up in advance when he sensed Lu Yang burrowing toward the surface like an earthworm.

Lu Yang rolled his eyes at Meng Jingzhou. “It would take you just as long to go down and come back.”

Gan Tian looked at Lu Yang, slightly surprised. Little Junior Brother’s round trip took a few days faster than I had estimated.

With such speed, even a Nascent Soul cultivator would feel ashamed in his presence. Little Junior Brother is stronger than I thought. No wonder Big Senior Sister made him the acting sect leader.

“Well, any gains? Your senior sister didn’t lie to you, right?”

Lu Yang nodded. It was a fruitful trip, though I can’t share my gains with others. The implications are too great. Besides, speaking about the Four Ancient Immortals’ Dao Fruits is futile—the listeners will forget immediately.

“Since you’re back, you two stay here and keep watch. I’ll go outside to see if those old fellows have left.” Gan Tian stood up and stretched. She reminded the two not to run around and that she would return shortly.

She picked up a talisman, and it ignited spontaneously. Before their four eyes, she vanished on the spot. Neither sight nor spiritual consciousness could detect Gan Tian. This was a highly advanced invisibility talisman. Only the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could see her.

After about half an hour, Gan Tian returned as promised, with good news. “They’re all gone! We’re safe!”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou heaved a sigh of relief. We’re finally safe.

“Where do we go now?”

“The Qiongqi Tribe. I have a second base there.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou inhaled sharply. Third Senior Sister, you’re leading us right into their stronghold.

“It’s fine. I’ve lost count of how many times I’ve been to the Qiongqi Tribe. Don’t be fooled by their formidable reputation outside. Their internal management is quite lax. It can’t compare to our Dao-Seeking Sect’s.”

The two followed Gan Tian out. Only upon emerging from the cave did they realize they weren’t in a mountain but beneath one. To leave, they had to climb upward.

The mountain was shrouded in thick fog and dew. The muddy path was riddled with potholes, and small puddles were everywhere, likely because it had rained not long ago.

Gan Tian suddenly stopped in her tracks.

“What’s wrong, Senior Sister?”

Gan Tian pointed at a small puddle. “Follow me and jump in.”

“Ah?”

Without further explanation, Gan Tian jumped into the puddle. This puddle was just accumulated rainwater, seemingly only two or three inches deep, yet she vanished when she jumped in.

Although the two were puzzled, they didn’t doubt Gan Tian and followed suit in jumping in.

Lu Yang felt his body completely submerged, as if he was entering the depths of the East Sea. He lost all sense of direction, unable to tell east from west, and swam desperately in one direction. After a few strokes, his head lightened, and he surfaced, climbing out of the puddle.

The surrounding scenery was exactly the same as before he jumped in.

“This is the real outside world.” Gan Tian smiled. She had built this place when she first arrived in the Demon Region. To have remained undiscovered, it naturally hid mysterious principles.

Lu Yang understood. Third Senior Sister leveraged the mountain forest’s rainy characteristics, using a puddle as an entrance to create a mirrored underground space. We have been hiding in this underground space all these days.

“This is the second lesson Shifu taught: learn to hide.”

The first lesson the Taciturn Daoist Priest taught Gan Tian was escape, and the second lesson was concealment.

Lu Yang recalled Yun Zhi’s teaching process. The first lesson had me swinging large vats like a circus act, and the second lesson had me bathing in boiling water.

Hard to say which is superior.

“The Qiongqi Tribe is a hundred and fifty li away from here.” Gan Tian pointed in a direction. “Along the way, we’ll have to pass through a branch tribe settlement of the Qiongqi Tribe.

“Take these two invisibility talismans. Ignite them when we get close to the branch tribe.” Gan Tian gave each of them a talisman.

“Branch tribe?”

“Basically, qiongqi with impure bloodlines. They aren’t qualified to be recorded in the Qiongqi Tribe’s genealogy. As you’ve seen, the Demon Region is dangerous. Thus, they cling to the Qiongqi Tribe and stay nearby to survive, acting as guards and servants.”

“Wasn’t the first demon beast we killed a mixed-blood qiongqi?” Meng Jingzhou asked softly.

Lu Yang nodded. It was, indeed. That was when he, Meng Jingzhou, and Man Gu went to eliminate a tiger demon. The tiger demon had Qiongqi bloodline and was a mixed-blood.

Chapter 576: The Qiongqi Tribe’s Tomb

The Invisibility Talismans Gan Tian provided were of an extremely high grade, with no level restrictions for the user. Upon burning the talisman, Lu Yang turned invisible and moved unimpeded through the branch Qiongqi Tribe as if it was a no man’s land.

Although it was called a branch tribe, that was relative to the main Qiongqi Tribe. In the outside world, these branch tribes would be revered by other demons. freewebnovel.com

Despite walking only a short distance, Lu Yang already encountered a patrol squad. The captain was a Foundation Establishment expert, and every squad member was powerful, at the eighth or ninth layer of the Qi Training Stage.

And this was just a small squad leader. A medium squad leader was likely a Golden Core old ancestor or a Half-Step Golden Core old ancestor.

“The chieftain of this branch tribe is at the Basic Fusion Stage. With such cultivation, he could hold a seat even in the Qiongqi Tribe’s elder council. However, he was injured in his early years, so he can’t act easily.” Gan Tian reminded them. This branch tribe has the strength of a first-class sect, albeit the weakest kind, but we still can’t afford to be careless.

The two nodded in unison, assuring Gan Tian. While we brothers may not have many strengths, being cautious is definitely one of them.

Lu Yang also saw a young mixed-blood qiongqi training diligently, panting heavily as he jumped around in a small courtyard. His fur was soaked in sweat, yet he didn’t stop for a rest.

“I must evolve my bloodline into a pure-blood qiongqi and bring honor to my family!” The young mixed-blood qiongqi’s eyes sparkled, full of hope.

The demon race had unique cultivation methods that could purify bloodlines, enabling the possibility of a carp leaping over the Dragon Gate[1]—going against the tide and rising to prominence. However, those who could achieve this were few and far between.

“Ah, the bloodline evolution method has been passed down to this day.” Having dealt with demon beasts for a long time, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy recognized the young mixed-blood qiongqi’s movements at a glance. It was a bloodline evolution technique compiled by the Qilin Immortal.

Before the Qilin Immortal, bloodline evolution methods did exist, but their efficiency was too low.

“Immortal Fairy, can he evolve into a pure-blood qiongqi?”

“This little tiger’s bloodline is quite mixed; his ancestors include six or seven different demon beasts. With his talent, he’s counted as a genius in the branch tribe, and if he cultivates like this, he can indeed advance to a pure-blood. But that’s all. Once he becomes a pure-blood and enters the Qiongqi Tribe, he’ll realize geniuses like him are a dime a dozen. He won’t stand out in the Qiongqi Tribe.”

“That tragic?”

“That’s not called tragic—it’s reality. The talent disparity is clear. If this little tiger were in Great Xia, he wouldn’t even qualify for the tournament finals. The Qiongqi Tribe has many geniuses like him, equally hardworking, and these geniuses enjoyed better resources than him in the past. How can he rise above them?

“To become the strongest, both talent and resources are indispensable. Your talent is strong enough, right? Forget placing you in a second or third-class sect; even in a first-class sect, could they fully bring out your potential? No, they can’t.”

Lu Yang nodded. Not to boast, but my talent absolutely can’t be fully realized in a first-class sect, perhaps not even in the Five-Elements Sect.

“So you see, hard work does lead to success, but no matter how hard you work, you can’t surpass someone equally hardworking and more talented than you.”

“Immortal Fairy, are you telling me all this to encourage me to cultivate harder?”

“No, what I mean is that Lass Yun has great talent, is willing to endure hardship, and has cultivated several hundred years more than you, so you probably can’t catch up to her. When our Everlasting Lineage fights her, I’ll be the main force, and you’ll provide support.”

Lu Yang, “...”

~~~

The three passed through the branch tribe without incident and arrived at the Qiongqi Tribe. Squads of five qiongqi patrolled both the sky and the ground. Every ten minutes, another squad would pass by.

“Strange, why is the Qiongqi Tribe so heavily guarded? Are they about to fight the Moonhowl Skywolf Tribe?”

“Should we change locations?”

“No need. It’s not targeted at us anyway.”

“How do you know, Senior Sister?” Meng Jingzhou was curious.

“If it were targeted at us, the Qiongqi Tribe elders would be patrolling outside. What use are these small fries? Such heavy security is probably for show.”

“...Makes sense.”

“Every noon, the tribe’s great protection array has a gap lasting three breaths. We need to seize that opening to enter.” Gan Tian knew her way around and was familiar with the Qiongqi Tribe’s arrays. One could only wonder how many times she had been here.

Fifteen minutes later, Gan Tian signaled with her eyes. The three timed it perfectly and successfully entered the Qiongqi Tribe.

Qiongqi were accustomed to living in jungles and caves. Hence, hollowed-out tree holes and mountains were ubiquitous in the Qiongqi Tribe.

While moving through the tribe, the trio occasionally encountered small groups of qiongqi conversing. Lu Yang faintly heard phrases like “envoy visit,” which inevitably piqued his curiosity.

Is this the reason for the Qiongqi Tribe’s tight security? An envoy is visiting? What level of envoy warrants such a grand display from the Qiongqi Tribe?

Lu Yang quietly asked Gan Tian.

“Envoy? A visit from an equal wouldn’t result in such a fuss. It’s probably a race even stronger than the Qiongqi. That would have to be at the level of Dragons or Phoenixes.”

“Third Senior Sister, where are we going?”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou followed Gan Tian. The further they went, the more remote it became. They walked for half a day without seeing a single qiongqi, and the atmosphere felt eerie.

“The Qiongqi Tribe’s tomb. To conduct archaeology and unearth secrets hidden in history, one must go to such places. Whether murals or burial objects, they are all cultural relics worth studying.

“Didn’t I ask Big Senior Sister to send someone knowledgeable about ancient history? It was here, in the Qiongqi Tribe’s tomb, that I discovered something strange.”

“Something strange.”

“It’s hard to explain in a few words. You’ll know when you see it.”

The Qiongqi Tribe placed much importance on their tomb, stationing a Fusion-Stage qiongqi as a tomb guardian. Unfortunately, this guardian was nothing more than a decoration to Gan Tian; she even had energy to spare to bring two youngsters in.

Upon seeing the Qiongqi Tribe’s tomb, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were utterly awed.

Before them was a colossal qiongqi statue huge enough to fill their field of vision. It was carved from three mountains and joined together with great powers. The qiongqi statue was lifelike—a fearsome tiger with wings upon its back, its eyes stern and majestic. Its stance was poised for flight, as though it was ready to spread its wings and soar at any moment. Just looking at this statue was intimidating.

The Qiongqi Tribe’s tomb lay beneath this enormous statue.

“It’s said this tomb was constructed in ancient times. This style was very popular for demons then,” Gan Tain explained, expressing that they didn’t need to be so startled.

Suddenly, Meng Jingzhou halted. He pointed at the qiongqi statue above them and dared not look up. “Why do I feel like this statue is alive and constantly watching us? Is it an illusion?”

Lu Yang froze, a chill running down his spine. He actually had the same feeling. If two people felt it, it isn’t an illusion.

Gan Tian transmitted an auditory message to the two. “I also feel like we’re being watched.” She revealed a secret. “There’s always been a legend in the Qiongqi Tribe that the thing above isn’t a statue but an ancient qiongqi turned to stone. It has slumbered until now and accumulated strength, possibly awakening at any moment!”

The two grew even more tense and gulped, their hearts pounding violently. It felt as though the ancient qiongqi above them had already awakened, opening its bloody maw toward the three intruders, saliva dripping...

The knowledgeable and experienced Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained, “That feeling of being watched is due to an array researched by the Heaven Mandate Immortal. He advocated for everyone to set up this kind of array when building their tombs. It can scare people and give rise to legends.”

1. It’s a folk tale where the carp can transform into a dragon if it’s able to jump over the Dragon Gate, a canyon of the Yellow River. The meaning is explained in the next part of the sentence. It is a famous idiom often used to encourage students to succeed through hard work and perseverance. In the past, it was mainly through the imperial examinations, and now it is through the gaokao, the national high school leaving examinations. ☜

Chapter 577: The Heaven Mandate Immortal’s Painstaking Efforts

The three of them felt like they were being watched, a bone-chilling sensation.

Gan Tian continued, “It is precisely because of this legend that very few qiongqi come to the Qiongqi Tomb. This is a place even their own tribesmen are reluctant to visit. They fear they might disturb the slumbering ancient Qiongqi.

“But you don’t have to be afraid. I’ve been here several times. Although there’s a feeling of being watched, that’s all it is. Once we enter the tomb below, this feeling will disappear.

“Historically, the Qiongqi Tribe has produced several Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. They all came to the Qiongqi Tomb to check if their old ancestor, the ancient Qiongqi, truly slumbered here. But they always ended up empty-handed. They said the ancient Qiongqi’s cultivation was far above theirs, and that they were unworthy descendants who were not qualified to investigate their old ancestor’s situation.”

In the demon race, Fusion cultivators were referred to as “king,” and Transcendent Tribulation cultivators were referred to as “emperor.” With the Qiongqi Tribe producing several Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, it implied they had several demon emperors—a truly terrifying number.

Qiongqi could be considered the pinnacle of “tiger demons.” Their fame even spread to the Central Continent, giving rise to the idiom “like a tiger that has grown wings,” illustrating the qiongqi’s might.

“Acknowledged by several qiongqi demon emperors, the ancient Qiongqi is recognized as the strongest existence in the Qiongqi Tribe.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Third Senior Sister, please stop talking. I’m afraid you might curse the immortals after learning the truth, increasing the difficulty of your tribulation.

Heaven Mandate Immortal, you really know how to mess around.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal said that in one’s lifetime, one should not only care about their reputation while alive but also their posthumous fame. That was why he developed this great array to leave behind legends for future generations. freewebnovel.com

“Aside from the Qiongqi, he probably also set up this array in the ancestral tombs of the Kunpeng, Taowu, Zhuque, and other races—not too many, for building too many would diminish the mystique.”

The great array had lasted three hundred years without failing and could still scare people. This was a testament to the exceptional quality of arrays developed by the Heaven Mandate Immortal. From another angle, it demonstrated how much care and concern he put into this.

“Moreover, to form a legend, the truth cannot be known to later generations. Thus, the matter of the tomb arrays was covered up, becoming a secret.”

Judging by the Qiongqi Tribe’s fear of approaching the tomb, the arrays had indeed become a secret.

“...The Heaven Mandate Immortal is really quite fond of helping people.” Lu Yang racked his brains for words to praise the Heaven Mandate Immortal, hoping to reduce the danger during his future tribulations.

“He wasn’t exactly fond of helping people. Think about it. Whether it was the old Qiongqi or the old Kunpeng, they are what you call ancient demons with boundless powers, right?

“But no matter how boundless their powers are, could they be more powerful than immortals? Probably not.

“The more mysterious the old Qiongqi and the others are, the more it highlights the strength of we Five Ancient Immortals, doesn’t it?”

Immortal Fairy, please stop talking. If you continue, I’m afraid I might truly grow highly disrespectful thoughts toward the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

Similar to how Meng Jingzhou trained his willpower, Lu Yang also trained his willpower when he listened to ancient history.

The three entered the Qiongqi Tomb. The feeling of being watched indeed vanished, and their psychological pressure decreased drastically.

“This is...”

Inside the Qiongqi Tomb were many murals. Most had suffered the ravages of time and become dilapidated. The pigments used for the murals were extremely exorbitant—it wasn’t an exaggeration to say they were worth a thousand gold per drop. Even so, the murals could no longer withstand the cleansing of time and were reduced to this state. This reflected the long-standing age of the Qiongqi Tribe and their tomb.

Lu Yang saw a mural depicting a small qiongqi with wet fur, clearly just born. Then this little qiongqi ran forward, gradually growing larger until it reached its prime, and then it gradually aged, losing its fur and becoming stooped as it walked toward death.

The endpoint of death was the Qiongqi Tomb.

The murals also depicted many major historical events of the Qiongqi Tribe, which they viewed as glories to be engraved in their memories.

Above the murals was a line of ancient text: Death is not the endpoint. One has witnessed your glorious lives.

“These are words left by the ancient Qiongqi, regarded by the Qiongqi Tribe as their spiritual pillar. Because of this, the Qiongqi Tribe does not fear death and accepts it with equanimity.

Gan Tian truly lived up to being a professional archaeological scholar; she could speak of the demon race’s multifarious cultures at will.

“This line... The Heaven Mandate Immortal couldn’t have written this too, right?”

“No, it wasn’t. This was the old Qiongqi’s own improvisation. The Heaven Mandate Immortal couldn’t possibly help each one of them come up with a line—that would make them sound too similar and risk exposure.” The Heaven Mandate Immortal is meticulous in his work and considers things thoroughly.

“Senior Sister, where is this hideout you mentioned?”

“Almost there, almost there.”

The tomb’s interior was pitch black and as complex as a maze. Without guidance from a Qiongqi Tribe elder, it was easy to get lost. One could only wonder how on earth Gan Tian had managed to figure out the structure of the Qiongqi tomb.

The three walked about two li before reaching the end of the passageway. Gan Tian rapped a brick, and a hidden door opened. She gestured for the two to follow.

Lu Yang noticed many arrows facing outward on the hidden chamber’s walls and immediately understood. The Qiongqi tomb contained many traps. If someone stepped in the wrong place, a barrage of arrows would be launched, killing the intruder. After the arrows were shot, they needed to be replenished, hence the mechanism chamber, where the three had paused to rest.

“Senior Sister, you even found a place like this?”

The two were astonished. Hiding in a tomb was one thing, but hiding in the tomb’s mechanism chamber—who would think someone was hiding here? No wonder Third Senior Sister had confidently claimed that hiding in the Qiongqi Tribe is very safe.

The trio rested here for a few hours to adjust their conditions. Although they had Invisibility Talismans and weren’t afraid of being discovered, maintaining invisibility was still draining. Gan Tian was fine, but Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had been using the talismans for almost an entire day, from the branch tribe to the Qiongqi Tomb. Rest was necessary. The two fell asleep as soon as they hit the floor of the mechanism chamber.

While the two slept, Gan Tian took out paper, ink, brush, and inkstone, and wrote about their experiences over the past few days. She had been writing her experiences in the Demon Region into Accounts of the Demon Region, having already completed eight volumes. She was now working on the ninth.

Despite their brief contact, she was certain that her little junior brother knew more about ancient history than she did. Little Junior Brother is so well-versed in ancient history. As long as he’s around, I believe the ninth volume’s content will be even richer than the previous eight volumes.

“Mmm...”

Hearing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou stirring and about to wake, she put away the Four Treasures of the Study and sat quietly.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had slept a full three hours. Upon waking, they felt clear-headed and refreshed.

“You’re awake? Perfect timing. I’ll take you to the main tomb. The ancient Qiongqi is said to be buried there.”

“Said to be?”

Gan Tian nodded. She slung her guqin behind her back and tied the strings across her chest. Along with her eyes covered with black cloth, she looked like a hermit walking out of a bamboo forest.

She explained, “At the very least, the ancient Qiongqi’s coffin is there. As for whether a qiongqi truly lies inside, I have no idea. But that’s irrelevant to us. We’re here for archaeology, not tomb raiding.”

As a professional scholar, Gan Tian adhered to the principle of seeing is believing.

Chapter 578: Burial Objects

The main tomb buried the ancient Qiongqi, who was regarded as the strongest qiongqi. The place was lavishly decorated, with manifold rare treasures and ancient magical artifacts displayed within. It was as if the ancient Qiongqi could come alive at any moment, wielding these magical treasures to wage war and slay enemies.

Auctioning off any one of these treasures would warrant half a year of preparation and extensive publicity, fetching astronomical prices as the centerpiece item. Even with Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s discerning eyes, they couldn’t identify the origins of these items and could only consult Gan Tian.

Fortunately, Lu Yang had two ears—perfect for listening to Gan Tian’s explanation with his left ear and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s explanation with his right ear.

Three identical fluorescent spirit grasses grew on the wall with tenacious vitality.

Gan Tian: “Kunlun Grass. Legend says this can improve one’s foundation, cleanse tendons and marrow, and even grant a one-third chance of transforming one’s body into the Kunlun Immortal Physique!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy: “Kunlun Grass. If you eat a lot of it, your body will change into the Kunlun Immortal Physique. It’s pretty much useless. The Kunlun Immortal Physique is the most trash among all immortal physiques. The first immortal physique I fought was the Kunlun Immortal Physique.”

A feather radiating a pure white light was encased in a shell as tall as a person; both looked extraordinary.

Gan Tian: “Qiongqi Feather. It’s a feather right from the center of the ancient Qiongqi’s back. Legend says this feather allows its owner to request aid from any race within the ‘Demon Alliance.’ The feather also encompasses true words from the ancient Qiongqi. Whoever hears them must agree to any condition raised by the Qiongqi Tribe.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy: “Qiongqi Feather. It’s a feather plucked from the old Qiongqi’s back. He grimaced in pain for half a day. Holding this thing can let one ask other demons for help. Only the Qiongqi Tribe can use it. To use it, they drip blood on it and activate it with magic power. Then the feather will emit the old Qiongqi’s voice—‘Give me some face.’”

A palm-sized black mountain stood on the ground. It was immensely heavy and distorted the space around it. If not for the array’s reinforcement, it would likely have already collapsed into a black hole.

Gan Tian: “Mount Buzhou[1] Mountain Essence. Legend says that in ancient times, two mighty experts controlling water and fire fought in an epic battle to vie for a position as an immortal. Water and fire clashed, volcanoes erupted, oceans turned to lava, and stars exploded into countless meteors. Finally, the water wielder crashed into Mount Buzhou, toppling it. The mountain’s collapse gave birth to the mountain essence.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy: “Mount Buzhou Mountain Essence. Remember that Golden Core cultivator who could conjure saltwater? He had pretty good luck, cultivating all the way to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. A conflict with a Phoenix Tribe’s prodigy broke out, and the two came to blows, smashing several spheres. The Phoenix prodigy had received a few pointers from me and was a terribly strong fighter. The saltwater Golden Core cultivator lost his temper after losing and crashed into Mount Buzhou, resulting in this thing.”

“Is this the core of Mount Buzhou?”

“This is him being headstrong. He used his head to compress Mount Buzhou into this tiny piece.”

Lu Yang, “...”

These treasures all bore seals. The slightest movement would alert the Qiongqi Tribe, and the entire tomb would be sealed off, making escape impossible for tomb raiders.

As Gan Tian said, she was here for archaeology, not tomb raiding. She wasn’t tempted by these items.

The very center of the main tomb displayed a black, heavy, massive coffin. Rather than calling it a coffin, it was more like an isolated, large, black ship that could ferry across the Nether River for another life.

“This is hundred-thousand-year-old Netherwood, the best material for coffins. It cuts off all detection by spiritual consciousness,” Gan Tian said.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy chimed in. “I remember this thing. The old Qiongqi bought it from the Epoch Immortal, who used the Tree-Planting Mantra and the Epoch Dao Fruit simultaneously to turn the sapling into hundred-thousand-year-old Netherwood.

“The older the natural treasure, the higher its value. People often asked the Epoch Immortal to add years to their treasures. Sometimes, adding too many years could even create Little Herb Kings.”

The Epoch Immortal had performed the orthodox Tree-Planting Mantra—Lu Yang couldn’t compare.

As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke, she spread her immortal consciousness to probe the black coffin. As a fellow individual from the ancient era, she wanted to know if the old Qiongqi was dead or alive.

How could there be anything in this world that blocks immortal consciousness?

“It’s a pity; he truly passed away.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sighed. An old acquaintance lay in a coffin not far away; it was an indescribable feeling.

Without a complete Dao Fruit, one’s lifespan was ultimately limited. The old Qiongqi had no external injuries—he died of old age.

However, she wasn’t too sad. She didn’t have much dealings with the old Qiongqi, and the latter also often ate people, only stopping during the era of the Five Ancient Immortals. That was why she didn’t help when the old Qiongqi implored her to extend his lifespan.

“Look here, there’s writing.” Lu Yang whispered as he pointed to a line of small characters at the bottom of the wall.

“‘Meng Potian was here.’ Who is Meng Potian?”

Meng Jingzhou’s expression was somewhat embarrassed. “My dad.”

In his youth, the Meng Clan Leader believed in “reading ten thousand books and traveling ten thousand li.” He journeyed everywhere, including the Demon Region, where he left his mark.

Given Dad’s personality, leaving such graffiti is perfectly normal.

Gan Tian nodded. “The Qiongqi Tribe also discovered this line.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Why is the Demon Region more dangerous than I’d imagined?

Wait, I’ve already run away from home. I don’t count as a member of the Meng Family.

Lu Yang patted Meng Jingzhou’s shoulder, showing loyalty to his friend. “Don’t be scared. If we get discovered by the Qiongqi Tribe, I’ll throw you out to buy time.”

“That won’t happen. The Qiongqi Tribe won’t do anything to Junior Brother Meng.”

Lu Yang was stunned. I didn’t expect the Qiongqi Tribe to be so noble, capable of requiting evil with good.

“It’s not exactly ‘requiting evil with good.’ Several hundred years ago, the Qiongqi Tribe was also in a rush to seek trouble with the Meng Family. But the Qiongqi Tribe had their own problems and couldn’t spare the energy for the Meng Family.”

“What problems did the Qiongqi Tribe have?” Lu Yang asked. Could it be that a chaotic war happened in the Demon Region several hundred years ago, where the Qiongqi Tribe participated, got caught between two fronts, and was barely able to fend for themselves? Or did internal strife occur within the Qiongqi Tribe, like two qiongqi vying for the position of tribe chieftain?

Gan Tian explained, “The Qiongqi Tribe is born with an impoverished destiny. Several hundred years ago, they suffered heavy losses in business, and complaints echoed through the tribe. If not for the Meng Family providing loans, the Qiongqi Tribe likely wouldn’t have survived that crisis.

“I heard they just finished repaying the debt fifty years ago. Junior Brother Meng, you’re the eldest young master of the Meng Family. If the Qiongqi Tribe learns of you, they will probably treat you with courtesy. I reckon they’d probably agree if you were willing to be buried in the Qiongqi Tomb.”

Meng Jingzhou finally breathed a sigh of relief. It seems my Meng Family identity doesn’t draw hatred all the time.

Lu Yang shot a sidelong glance at Meng Jingzhou. Brat, your Meng Family identity is quite adaptable, huh?

Gan Tian bowed three times to the black coffin, her posture dignified and her attitude deferential. Proper etiquette is necessary. “Senior Qiongqi, apologies for the offense.”

One can't possibly just seize burial objects directly; that isn’t in line with etiquette.

She walked to the corner of the main tomb, carefully enveloping a pottery jar with magic power and lifting it. This pottery jar was a burial object of the lowest grade and wasn’t even considered a magical treasure. Its purpose was for decoration.

The few patterns on the pottery jar puzzled her greatly. “Little Junior Brother, take a look at this pottery jar.”

1. Mount Buzhou is one of the ancient Chinese mythological mountains, and it lies toward the northwest of Kunlun Mountain. It is said that the water god Gonggong smashed his head against it in a fit of anger. More information on the legend is in the Translator’s Thoughts section below. ☜

Chapter 579: The Battle of the Highest Scale in History

“Pottery jar?”

Hearing Gan Tian call him, Lu Yang interrupted the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s explanation.

Unlike the aged and crude pottery jar paintings Lu Yang was familiar with, which required guesswork to decipher their contents, this jar painting from the ancient Qiongqi’s burial objects was exceptionally exquisite.

The painting depicted cataclysmic changes in heaven and earth, resembling the impending arrival of doomsday. All living beings were like ants. Even through the pottery jar, Lu Yang could feel the extreme sense of despair and the inability to resist before such mighty power. The ancient Qiongqi spread its wings, desperately protecting its race.

The painting’s intent was to illustrate the ancient Qiongqi’s glorious achievements, for it had protected the Qiongqi Tribe during a great catastrophe.

However, Lu Yang’s focus wasn’t on the ancient Qiongqi, but on the painting’s background.

This doomsday-like catastrophe originated from four figures in the background. They were blurry, but their every movement displayed their boundless power.

“These four figures should be the Four Ancient Immortals,” Gan Tian stated confidently. Only the legendary Four Ancient Immortals could have forced the ancient Qiongqi to spread its wings to protect its clansmen.

“That should be the case.” Lu Yang nodded, his expression slightly solemn. He had roughly deduced the contents of the painting.

“But the question is, what kind of opponent could warrant the Four Ancient Immortals to join forces?” Gan Tian was especially perplexed.

Judging by how they’re standing in a row, the Four Ancient Immortals should be on the same side. What enemy in ancient times could have made these four legendary invincible beings unite? Gan Tian sifted through all the ancient texts in her mind but found no enemy that fit the bill.

Lu Yang fell silent. Of course, there was one—the mysterious existence capable of assassinating the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and enraging the Four Ancient Immortals.

This painting depicted the Four Ancient Immortals confronting the immortal who assassinated the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. It was different from the usual sparring among the Five Ancient Immortals, which aimed to exchange cultivation insights, learn from one another, identify weaknesses, and mutually improve—they never delivered lethal blows with the intent to kill.

This time was different. The Four Ancient Immortals battled with the mysterious immortal. The five immortals fought fiercely, not holding back. Perhaps no battle in history could match the scale of this one!

It was the most powerful battle in history!

An unparalleled battle of the era!

Not even half-immortals were qualified to intervene in this battle!

But Lu Yang couldn’t tell Gan Tian all this. Big Senior Sister had warned that the mastermind’s identity and purpose are unknown, and that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence must not be revealed. If the mastermind discovers the Everlasting Immortal Fairy resurrected, who knows if they would kill everyone who knows of her existence?

Lu Yang shook his head, indicating he also had no idea who the Four Ancient Immortals’ opponent was.

Just as Gan Tian was disappointed, Lu Yang pointed out another detail in the painting. “Third Senior Sister, look. There are other planets in the background of this painting. These planets have a ring of light around them, probably protective barriers.”

The Four Ancient Immortals did not lose their reason to anger. Even while fighting, they had spare attention to protect these planets. Without this layer of protection, more than half of the living beings in the entire universe might have become casualties.

“It really is.” Gan Tian was extremely surprised. This is a major discovery. Current historical records only mention the Nine-Layers Immortal saving people with Xirang Soil; there are no other records of the other three immortals saving anyone. This had led to endless debates in historical academia about the other three immortals’ characters.

One thing can now be confirmed—the Four Ancient Immortals didn’t view all living beings as ants.

Lu Yang was actually not the one who discovered that the Four Ancient Immortals had protected the planets. He never saw them act and didn’t know what the light rings around the planets were; it was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy who recognized them.

In his mental space, Lu Yang furrowed his brow. He had ascertained that the Four Ancient Immortals were the Ancient Nameless One. However, if they had employed methods to protect the stars and planets during the battle, it would contradict the historical records he knew.

Historical records documented that the Ancient Nameless One refined the stars into continents, causing countless casualties and a gap in history where even the ancient language wasn’t passed down. The Great Qian Dynasty was built on the ruins, inaugurating the era of human dynasties.

If the Four Ancient Immortals had refined the stars, how could they have disregarded life and death during this process and caused a historical gap?

“Could it be that after refining the stars into continents, something else happened, resulting in the historical gap?”

Another memory suddenly struck Lu Yang. There was also the Ember Legacy Dynasty, whose origin is unknown!

We discovered the Ember Legacy Dynasty in the Everlasting Secret Domain. Calculating the years, it should be in the ancient era. Yet strangely, there are no records of the dynasty now, with not even its name being mentioned!

What exactly happened in the Ember Legacy Dynasty?

“Old Lu, what’s painted on this pottery jar? Come take a look.” Meng Jingzhou called Lu Yang over. It’d be a waste not to use such a living fossil.

The pottery jar that Meng Jingzhou referred to was on the other side of the main tomb. It depicted a fierce battle between giants. A qiongqi and a true dragon were engaged in a huge battle, and a figure radiating light descended from the sky, stopping the fight between these two peerless demon emperors.

Before Lu Yang could answer, he heard Gan Tian, the history scholar, explain. “This is a famous Buddhist legend you’ve probably heard. The Qiongqi Tribe and the Dragon Tribe are natural enemies with irreconcilable conflicts. Once, a qiongqi and a true dragon fought, flooding the eight wildernesses and plunging the world into chaos. Fortunately, an enlightened Buddhist intervened, subduing the qiongqi and the true dragon in exchange for peace in the world. This is the origin of the Buddhist saying that enlightened Buddhists have the ‘ability to subdue dragons and vanquish tigers.’

“According to my research, this battle was likely a competition between the ancient Qiongqi and the Dragon old ancestor for a position as an immortal, but they were interrupted by someone.

“Actually, I’m also puzzled about why the painting is placed here. It clearly shows the scene of subduing a dragon and vanquishing a tiger, which tarnishes the Qiongqi Tribe’s reputation. Why would it be displayed here as a burial object?”

Meanwhile, Lu Yang was listening to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s immortal words with rapt attention.

“The old Qiongqi had a young daughter. She was very beautiful and talented, nearly catching up to the old Qiongqi. The little Qiongqi had many pursuers, but she wasn’t interested in any of them; she only liked the Qilin Immortal. Coincidentally, the Qilin Immortal also liked her, and they hit it off. Later, a prodigy from the Dragon Tribe found out about it. She was so incensed that she went to confront the little Qiongqi, and they ended up fighting.

“However, how could the little Qiongqi be a match for the Dragon prodigy? She couldn’t win. Right then, the Qilin Immortal came to mediate, blatantly taking sides. Only after much persuasion did he manage to pacify both. I heard he had to kneel on sword arrays every day after returning home.

“Later on, the few of us put our heads together and wove this incident into a Buddhist story.”

Lu Yang, “...”

What should I do? Should I tell Third Senior Sister about the Qilin Immortal’s affair being discovered by his wife?

If the Qilin Immortal finds out, can I even leave this tomb alive? freewebnovel.com

“But speaking of which, why is only the old Qiongqi buried here? Where’s her daughter? Given the old Qiongqi’s favoritism, they should be buried together.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was bewildered. The little Qiongqi was only at the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage, not even a half-immortal. She should have died of old age before the old Qiongqi.

Chapter 580: The Might of an Ancient Great Demon

“No wonder I kept feeling like something was amiss with this coffin. So it’s because someone is missing. Where did Jin Caiwei go?”

The Qiongqi Tribe used “Jin” as their surname. Jin Caiwei was the “little Qiongqi” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mentioned.

Lu Yang, “...”

Why does that sound so strange?

“Wait, someone’s coming. Quickly tell your senior sister and the Meng boy to leave immediately,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy warned.

“People come to this place?” Lu Yang was baffled but knew the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wouldn’t lie to him, so he followed her instructions.

“Third Senior Sister, we need to hide right now! Someone’s entering the tomb!”

“How do you know?” Gan Tian was confused. I didn’t detect anyone; how did Lu Yang?

And why would someone be in the tomb? Did another qiongqi die?

Lu Yang was composed. “Before we left, Big Senior Sister gave me a magical treasure with a warning feature. Right now, it’s warning us that we’re in danger. Someone must have entered.”

“Big Senior Sister is so biased?” Gan Tian didn’t doubt it. Such a magical treasure sounds like something Big Senior Sister could provide.

The three hastily returned the items to their original positions and stealthily returned to the mechanism chamber. To prevent tomb raiders from discovering the tomb’s mechanisms and traps, the mechanism chamber had the function of blocking spiritual consciousness, making it perfect for hiding.

The moment the trio hid, they heard footsteps from the passageway’s entrance.

“Judging by the sound, there are two demons. One is an adult qiongqi, and the other seems like...a Dijiang Bird?” Gan Tian’s hearing was astonishing. She could identify the races just by their footsteps.

“Qiongqi and Dijiang. This combination doesn’t seem like tomb raiders or funeral attendees.” Meng Jingzhou scratched his head.

The two demons passed by the mechanism chamber.

Lu Yang was trembling, afraid of being discovered.

“Chieftain Jin, the meeting place you suggested is truly...unique.” The dijiang wore a smile, though he felt somewhat scared inside. When we entered the tomb, I felt like something was watching me, but apart from Chieftain Jin, there shouldn’t have been other demons.

Could it be the ancient Qiongqi statue above watching me?

The ancient Qiongqi is still alive?

The thought sent a chill down his spine. He shook his head discreetly, tossing this terrifying idea out of his mind.

Chieftain Jin chuckled. “It’s a major matter, after all. It must be decided under our ancestors’ witness to demonstrate the importance our tribe attaches to the Dijiang Tribe’s proposal.”

Lu Yang dared not speak. He transmitted an auditory message to Gan Tian. “Such grandeur is needed when the Dijiang Tribe visits the Qiongqi Tribe?”

The Qiongqi Tribe is heavily guarded outside—a level of security usually reserved for visits from the Dragon or Phoenix tribes. Although the Dijiang Tribe is a major one, surely it doesn’t warrant such treatment from the Qiongqi Tribe, right? And the Qiongqi Tribe even brought them into their own tomb?

Gan Tian frowned, also bemused. She had been busy with archaeology in various major tribes’ tombs recently and hadn’t paid much attention to the affairs in the Demon Region.

As the Chieftain Jin and the Dijiang envoy walked further away, their voices became barely audible. Only someone like Gan Tian, who had specially trained her hearing, could make out their conversation in the main tomb.

~~~

“Greetings, Old Ancestor.” Chieftain Jin knelt and bowed to the black coffin.

Due to the ancient Qiongqi’s imposing authority, the Dijiang envoy could only follow suit in kneeling and bowing.

“The Dijiang Tribe has been very active in the Demon Region lately, huh? Several of my old friends have mentioned your tribe. When the Taowu Tribe Chieftain told me about your tribe’s idea, it truly startled me. Unifying the Demon Region and establishing a demon kingdom—that’s an extraordinary idea.” Chieftain Jin stared coldly at the Dijiang envoy. “What surprised me even more was that the Taowu Tribe agreed to your proposal and voluntarily pledged allegiance.”

This was why Chieftain Jin had treated it as a grave threat and brought the Dijiang envoy to the Qiongqi Tomb. The Taowu Tribe’s strength is comparable to the Qiongqi Tribe’s. Without a special reason, how could they have sworn fealty?

The Dijiang envoy sighed. “There was simply no choice. The imminent arrival of the Great Era brings about countless fortuitous opportunities. Great Xia’s national power is strong, flourishing daily, and with the Five Great Immortal Sects as pillars of support, even the Four Great Diabolic Creeds can’t stir up waves there. In fact, one diabolic creed, the Everlasting Creed, was eliminated.

“In contrast, our Demon Region’s lineage has never been broken, being passed down from ancient times. Our overall strength is greater than Great Xia, yet we fight separately and are divided into three factions based on our stance toward humans.

“Our Demon Region is like a sheet of loose sand, unable to cooperate. How can we compete for fortuitous opportunities in the future?

“If our Dijiang Tribe unifies the Demon Region and absorbs the sea tribes to establish a supreme demon kingdom, what is Great Xia or the Buddhist Kingdom? Nothing!”

Chieftain Jin looked at the Dijiang envoy, his wariness rising drastically. His expression is fanatical and doesn’t seem feigned. This means that he truly believes this is achievable. Where does the Dijiang Tribe’s confidence come from?

~~~

Meng Jingzhou asked through an auditory message, “Does the Dijiang Tribe have any peerless experts?”

“In my memory, the Dijiang Tribe does have a Transcendent Tribulation demon emperor. You could say he’s strong, but that’s not enough to support such grand ambitions. Going back three hundred years, they did produce one half-immortal, but that expert died of old age long ago.”

~~~

“Your tribe’s concern for the Demon Region is admirable. I, Jin, am impressed. Unfortunately, my Qiongqi Tribe has no interest in contending for the world, nor do we care about any demon kingdom. Please leave, envoy.” Chieftain Jin bluntly asked the other party to leave.

The Dijiang Tribe spoke with nice-sounding and lofty rhetoric—the supreme Demon Kingdom, the Battle of the Great Era, and both Great Xia and the Buddhist Kingdom being dust. But how could Great Xia be so easy to get along with? A fierce battle is inevitable.

As tribe chieftain, I can’t lead my race into danger.

“Leave?” The Dijiang envoy revealed a sinister smile, appearing even more terrifying in the tomb. “Chieftain Jin, you seem to have misunderstood something. I didn’t come here to negotiate with you.”

“What are you trying to do?!” Chieftain Ji roared at the sky in rage as he spread his wings, his tiger eyes widened.

As he spoke, the Dijiang envoy took out a bone token from the front of his robe. The character “Monarch” was written on it.

The moment the token emerged, a frightening oppressive pressure permeated the air, like a hundred thousand mountains crushing Chieftain Jin. The entire space shook and trembled.

Several figures surfaced from the token.

One had a body crimson as blood, nine snake heads, and cold eyes—the great demon Jiuying.

Another had a body as massive as a mountain and resembled a male lion with two upward-growing tusks like heavenly blades—the great demon Taowu.

And there was also the Baihu, master of the killing aura, majestic and imposing, eyes glaring in all directions.

Aside from these, there were many other peerless great demons emanating similar auras and oppressive pressure.

Chieftain Jin trembled like a leaf, barely able to stand and nearly kneeling. These great demons are actually the old ancestors of various races—they’re entities called “demon emperors!”

This means that these demon emperors have all submitted to the Dijiang Tribe!

And the most eye-catching was the colossal figure among the great demons. It was red like the blazing sun, had six legs and four wings, and its eyes were spirited and greedy.

The ancient Dijiang, a half-immortal great demon!

“Chieftain Jin, submit to my ancient ancestor’s mark!” The envoy laughed heartily, activating the token again.

The oppressive pressure intensified. He had already branded many major tribes with servant marks using this method.
