“This grandson is still alive?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recognized the ancient Dijiang at a glance. “Like the Phoenix Tribe’s prodigy, he has the Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit. This Incipient Dao Fruit can control beings weaker than oneself and even decide life and death!”

“That strong?” Lu Yang was astonished.

“Average. When I was a half-immortal, he was only worth ten moves.”

The ancient Dijiang wasn’t very strong in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes, but to Chieftain Jin, it felt like the sky was falling!

Under the immense oppressive pressure, Chieftain Jin forced a smile as he struggled to stand firm and slowly open his tiger paw. Resting on it was a pure white feather.

The ancient Qiongqi’s feather!

When he was paying respects to the black coffin earlier, he had seized the chance to break the seal and retrieve this feather!

The envoy suddenly felt uneasy. Unlike his ancient ancestor, a half-immortal famed for controlling living beings, the ancient Qiongqi was renowned for combat prowess!

Chieftain Jin activated the ancient Qiongqi’s feather. A tiger’s roar reverberated through the heavens, the tomb quaked, and the earth trembled. A body larger than mountains filled the entire main tomb, emitting an oppressive pressure that made the envoy shudder.

The ancient Qiongqi lowered its head, its pupils reflecting the image of the ancient Dijiang and those entities referred to as demon emperors. He looked at the ancient Dijiang with contempt and opened his huge maw, exhaling a breath reeking of blood. With a smile that didn’t reach his eyes, he slowly spoke. freewebnovel.com

“Fellow Daoist, give me some face?”

Chapter 581: Give Me Some Face

The ancient Dijiang stared fixedly at the figure of his old friend, the ancient Qiongqi. He didn’t dare to be the slightest bit careless. Although it was merely a backup plan, he could already feel the pressure the ancient Qiongqi exerted on him. Nevertheless, he was unafraid.

We’re both half-immortals. Who’s worse than whom? I didn’t fear the ancient Qiongqi when he was alive; why would I when he is dead?

“And what if I don’t give you some face?”

Boom!

Without another word, the ancient Qiongqi brought his tiger paw down, as if he was smashing a watermelon, creating a frightening whirlwind that swept through the Qiongqi Tomb.

“You dare try to control my Qiongqi Tribe? I see you’ve grown tired of living!”

Under this strike from the ancient Qiongqi’s paw, the Transcendent Tribulation demon emperors within the token exploded one after another. They had merely left a wisp of oppressive pressure in the token; how could they withstand the ancient Qiongqi’s attack?

The ancient Dijiang was undaunted as he beat his wings, meeting the assault head-on.

The ancient Qiongqi had long been dead, while the ancient Dijiang was far away on the eastern side of the Demon Region. As the two half-immortals fought across time and space, the entire Qiongqi tribe could feel the tremor.

Outside the Qiongqi Tomb, the many colossal qiongqi seemed to have been summoned by their bloodline, bowing toward the tomb’s direction like collapsing hills.

Inside the Qiongqi Tomb, the ancient Dijiang laughed heartily and ceased attacking.

“Brother Jin Shi, you and I are as close as brothers. You were the one I wished to see most when I woke from my slumber. Now, seeing your imposing might no less than in those years, I am extremely delighted. It was precisely because I wanted to visit you that an envoy was sent to your esteemed tribe, Brother Jin Shi. Since that purpose has been achieved, I wish you a good sleep. Goodbye!”

The unification of the Demon Region is proceeding orderly. There is no need to provoke such a formidable enemy without cause. One more or one less Qiongqi Tribe won’t matter much.

This trip can be considered as testing the Qiongqi Tribe’s foundation.

Plop. The token fell to the ground, then turned to dust.

Coldly watching his old rival, the ancient Dijiang, the ancient Qiongqi snorted disdainfully and dissipated into the air.

~~~

“Immortal Fairy, this is the ‘give me some face’ you mentioned?” Lu Yang gulped. No wonder it’s said that this feather can make any demon tribe do one thing. It’s because if they don’t agree, the ancient Qiongqi will just attack directly.

“That's right. Was there any mistake in my description?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy retorted matter-of-factly. That said, the tone was off. The old Qiongqi had always spoken politely to me to “buy face,” but his tone when speaking to others is slightly worse.

“...No mistake,” Lu Yang relented. “Do you want to go chat with the ancient Qiongqi? He didn’t look completely dead to me; he moved like he was alive.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand. “He’s completely dead. At most, he left behind a divine thought. After that exchange of blows, the divine thought and consciousness in the feather were fully depleted.”

“What if the ancient Dijiang attacks again?”

“He can’t. It’s a flaw of the Law of the Jungle Dao Fruit. Since the Dijiang had voluntarily conceded in the battle earlier, he no longer occupies the ‘strong’ position. In that case, he can’t control the Qiongqi Tribe anymore.”

“Immortal Fairy, the ancient Dijiang said he woke from a slumber. Does that mean he slept from ancient times until now, also for the sake of becoming an immortal?”

“If he says so. He probably used some ice to freeze himself into an ice block, which only thawed now. Or maybe he soaked in something. There are many methods. Essentially, they all simulate time stasis.”

Not long ago, Lu Yang had met another archaic half-immortal who had slumbered—the Great Yu Imperial Preceptor.

“However, the higher one’s cultivation is, the more precious the natural treasures needed for slumber. It can be said that the treasures used by half-immortals are the most valuable. Moreover, since the Dao Fruit is still in an incipient form during their slumber, its power will gradually dissipate, leaving only an empty shell. After waking, there’s a long recovery period before one can return to peak condition.”

Immortals had infinite lifespans and didn’t need to slumber.

“Should we go find the ancient Dijiang?” Lu Yang asked. Aside from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, this is the second ancient figure who has appeared. He should know many things.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy revealed an expression of disgust. “Tch, that old fellow is not a good thing. He’s treacherous and cunning, hiding in very deep places. It’s hard to find him. Get Lass Yun here to turn the Demon Region upside down, and you’ll probably locate him.”

Lu Yang, “...”

~~~

The clash between the two half-immortals had settled. Chieftain Jin’s eyes were icy as he stared at the trembling Dijiang envoy kneeling on the ground.

“Envoy, will you get lost from my Qiongqi Tribe, or shall I ask someone to carry you out?”

“I’ll leave now!”

The Dijiang envoy never expected the Qiongqi Tribe’s foundation to run so deep. Even the ancient ancestor has voluntarily left. How can a mere envoy like me still linger here?

All dijiang had six legs. At this moment, he wished he could grow six more legs. He half scrambled and half crawled out of the Qiongqi Tomb and fled the Qiongqi Tribe.

~~~

After Gan Tian had listened to everything from start to finish, she perfectly reproduced the brief battle in the main tomb, as though she was a vocal mimicry virtuoso.

Meng Jingzhou was dumbfounded. We’re just here for archaeology. How did we encounter such matters—the ancient Dijiang awakening and the unification of the Demon Region?

Gan Tian wasn’t any better. She had lost count of how many tombs she had entered, but this was the first time she encountered such matters.

The unification of the Demon Region was a heaven-shaking event, yet no news had leaked. Presumably, the ancient Dijiang used his Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit to control the higher-ups of major tribes. Such control was absolute and ensured secrecy. It was only today, through a combination of coincidences, that they stumbled upon the Dijiang Tribe’s plan.

She took out xuan rice paper[1] from her identity jade tablet to report the incidents in the Demon Region to Yun Zhi, while Lu Yang ground ink beside her.

Yun Zhi replied quickly.

“Have Junior Brother answer. How is the ancient Dijiang’s combat power?”

Gan Tian was very surprised. Little Junior Brother knows even such matters?

Lu Yang thought for a moment and wrote back to Yun Zhi.

“Can’t withstand ten self-detonations from a half-immortal.”

“Then ignore it.“

The exchange ended.

Seeing there was nothing else for her to do, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy yawned out of boredom. She climbed onto a tree and hugged the trunk to sleep.

Before sleeping, she kindly reminded Lu Yang. “By the way, there’s a small matter you should note.”

“What is it?”

“The Qiongqi Tribe’s chieftain has discovered you all.”

Lu Yang was horrified. Before he could warn Meng Jingzhou and Gan Tian, the mechanism chamber’s door slowly opened.

Chieftain Jin’s massive tiger head peered in, his cold pupils reflecting the three figures. “If not for the old ancestor’s reminder, I truly wouldn’t have expected three little thieves to be hiding here.

“Let me see—Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden, Lu Yang...from the Dao-Seeking Sect. You’re the Meng Family’s Meng Jingzhou. Are you following in your father’s footsteps?”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Why does that sound so much like an insult?

Confirming the trio’s identities, Chieftain Jin’s expression softened, replaced by an affable smile. “You three, don’t stay here; come out with me. Otherwise, word might spread that the Qiongqi Tribe lacks hospitality.”

These three are suspected of tomb raiding, the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden has many enemies in the Demon Region, and the Dao-Seeking Sect is notorious—none of them are anything good.

But considering the Qiongqi Tribe’s recent financial strain and the need to borrow money from the Meng Family...

...I suppose it’s better to be polite to these three.

1. Xuan paper or rice paper was used in ancient China for writing and painting. It is smooth, preserves color well, durable, and offers great resistance to corrosion, crease, cracks, and decay caused by insects, among other benefits. The main materials for creating xuan paper are blue sandalwood bark and shatian rice straw. If you are interested in the production process, you could check out this short video. ☜

Chapter 582: Your Uncle Has Nothing Good to Give You on Our First Meeting

“Chieftain Jin, you know the two of us senior and junior brothers?” Lu Yang asked gingerly.

Chieftain Jin isn’t just large in size. To have risen to become the Qiongqi Tribe’s chieftain means he is absolutely a top-tier ruthless character.

Before we set out, Old Meng and I were wondering if anyone in the Demon Region would recognize us. The conclusion was that those in the Demon Region knew our names at best, but hadn’t seen our faces.

But seeing Chieftain Jin now, it looks like our previous conclusion had been too hasty.

Chieftain Jin glanced at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou with an ambiguous smile. “Originally, I didn’t care about who the Golden Core geniuses were. Before they grow up, it’s all nonsense. But you, Lu Yang, are different.”

“How am I different?” Lu Yang subconsciously smiled. Could it be that my talent is peerless through the ages and caught Chieftain Jin’s attention?

“You are the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Upon learning the champion was the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple, I specifically ordered someone to find a portrait.

“As for Meng Jingzhou, you are the eldest young master of the Meng Family. I also obtained your portrait.

“I didn’t expect you two to be with the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden. Could there be some relationship between you?” Chieftain Jin narrowed his eyes, scanning the three.

The Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden enjoys entering tombs and often slays demons, making many enemies. Yet her cultivation is proficient, and no one could catch her. Her origins are mysterious; no one knows her background.

It must have been through the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden’s assistance that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou could enter the Qiongqi Tomb. But why help them of all people? Could the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden also be from the Dao-Seeking Sect...

Chieftain Jin didn’t pursue that line of thought. The Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden’s identity has nothing to do with me.

As he walked, Chieftain Jin emitted a thick mist. A burly middle-aged man with tiger ears emerged from the mist.

“This way, please.”

He led the three to a small wooden house. Its interior was exquisitely constructed, unlike the rugged caves and tree holes prevalent in the Qiongqi Tribe. It was very much aligned with human aesthetic tastes, likely prepared by the Qiongqi Tribe for receiving humans.

The Qiongqi Tribe wasn’t some isolated race. On the contrary, they often interacted with various demon tribes and humans to make money. It was just that they often failed in business due to their lack of talent.

With their rich heritage and foundation, if they sold even one or two items from the main tomb’s burial objects, even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators would likely go mad for them, fetching astronomical prices. These were items kept at the bottom of the trunk—their most prized possessions. Selling them would be pure waste and debasing their worth. Chieftain Jin didn’t want to leave behind a tarnished reputation.

He called a shapeshifted tribesman to serve tea for the three. Chieftain Jin’s enthusiasm made the three somewhat uneasy and stumped.

Gan Tian was worried there might be some conspiracy. With my skills, I can escape easily, but my two junior brothers may not. Big Senior Sister had entrusted me with their care. I can’t let something go wrong on my watch.

“Potian and I address each other as brothers. You can call me Uncle Jin.” Noticing how reserved they were, Chieftain Jin laughed out loud.

Meng Jingzhou’s eye twitched. He never expected that Chieftain Jin’s good attitude toward them was because of him. Recalling Gan Tian’s explanation of the relationship between the Meng Family and the Qiongqi Tribe, Chieftain Jin’s attitude made sense.

But the problem is that I’ve already run away from home. Although Dad has forgiven me, I’m still unsure.

After hesitating briefly, he chose to respect Chieftain Jin’s wish and called out, “Uncle Jin.”

Hearing this, Chieftain Jin laughed heartily and handed Meng Jingzhou a piece of paper. “Good nephew, your uncle has nothing good to give you for our first meeting. Please keep this debt note.”

Meng Jingzhou instinctively wanted to decline but still accepted the gift. “This is too valuable... Wait, what did you say this is?”

“A debt note.”

Meng Jingzhou turned the paper over. The front clearly stated how many spirit stones Chieftain Jin owed the Meng Family, the interest, and the repayment deadline.

Chieftain Jin, a great demon king, had extremely strong mental fortitude. Without a change in expression, he said, “Could you speak to your family about forgiving my debt?”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

In my memory, no one has dared to welch on a debt to the Meng Family, let alone ask for forgiveness of a debt.

Chieftain Jin probed tentatively. “What about just forgiving the interest?”

Meng Jingzhou remained silent.

Chieftain Jin was unwilling to give up. “Postponing repayment for two years should be fine, right?”

Meng Jingzhou was worried that remaining silent might make Chieftain Jin consider kidnapping him for ransom from the Meng Family. “No problem. I’ll tell my dad when I return. Two years later, no interest charged.”

Chieftain Jin breathed a sigh of relief. It seems I won’t have to worry about being struck by lightning for a while. “Speaking of which, it’s been a long time since I saw Brother Potian. I often ask traveling merchants about Potian and the Meng Family’s recent situation. I heard that the Meng Family is the human race’s number one ancestral clan and spreads goodwill across the imperial city—generous in charity, fond of helping others, and treating all with kindness. They are held in high regard by the imperial city’s cultivators. Anyone who sees a member of the Meng Family would greet them with a smile.

“Brother Potian is even more outstanding, shining brightly in officialdom. Both civil and military officials praise him effusively, acclaiming him as having the talent of a prime minister of the ages...”

Meng Jingzhou became restless as he listened. None of these descriptions or adjectives seems to be related to the Meng Family. “Uncle Jin, if you have something to say, please say it directly.”

“Nephew, you’re a person of refreshing candor. One can tell you’re cut out for great things! Your uncle isn’t asking for much. I just hope the Meng Family could lend us some spirit stones.”

“Borrow again?” Meng Jingzhou was astonished. You just tried to welch, and now you have the nerve to ask for another loan. Is this how thick a great demon king’s skin is?

Chieftain Jin put on a solemn expression. “I’m not borrowing again. Previously, it was borrowed in my personal name. This time, it’s in the Qiongqi Tribe’s name. Don’t confuse the two.”

“...I can go back and talk to my family, but I can’t guarantee it’ll succeed.”

Chieftain Jin was overjoyed, his face even reverting to its original form. “Then I’ll trouble you to put effort into this matter, nephew!”

“Small matter, nothing worth mentioning,” Meng Jingzhou hurriedly replied. For safety’s sake, I should ask Steward Xu to speak to my dad when I return.

Calculating the time, he should be released by now.

Originally, Chieftain Jin wanted to call out the Qiongqi Tribe’s prodigies to spar with Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. However, considering these two were the champion and runner-up of the Intermediate Golden Core Stage, he figured their tribe’s prodigies would likely struggle to win.

Besides, if they beat Meng Jingzhou, how would the Qiongqi Tribe borrow money?

For these reasons, he had to abandon the idea.

Chieftain Jin hosted them for two days before seeing them out of the tribe. He didn’t pursue the matter of entering the tomb for archaeology partly because of Meng Jingzhou’s identity, but there was another reason—he wanted to inform Great Xia about the ancient Dijiang’s unification of the Demon Region through the mouths of these three.

According to records, the ancient Dijiang had a violent temperament. Letting such a great demon unify the Demon Region could result in unpredictable fortune and calamity. freewebnovel.com

Yawn~ The Everlasting Immortal Fairy woke up in the tree. Seeing the three safe and sound, she knew what she thought was correct—Chieftain Jin wouldn’t make things difficult for them. “See, I told you it was a small matter. The Qiongqi Tribe was already poor in the past and has remained poor until now. It’s really not easy. In the past, I suggested to the old Qiongqi that the name ‘Qiongqi (extremely impoverished)’ was no good, for it signified the loss of wealth.[1] They ought to change their name.”

“Immortal Fairy, what did you suggest the qiongqi change their name to?”

“Wangcai (prosperous wealth)[2] and Fugui (rich and noble).”

1. The first character in “qiongqi” means poor. One of the meanings of “qi” is very/extremely. If you flip the name around, it can mean “extremely poor.” ☜

2. “Wangcai” is a common name for dogs. ☜

Chapter 583: Ninth-Layer Golden Core Stage!

In the Qiongqi Tomb, two figures, one large and one small, stood silently before the black coffin, not uttering a word. The oily green glow from their pupils added a touch of terror in the pitch-black darkness.

If any Qiongqi Tribe elder were present, they would recognize the larger figure as the Qiongqi Tribe’s living fossil and the most senior existence, a Transcendent Tribulation old qiongqi who had lived for nine thousand years.

But strangely, between these two figures, the Transcendent Tribulation living fossil stood slightly behind, treating the petite figure with utmost deference, not daring to overstep the slightest.

The petite figure gently caressed the burial objects. They emitted a series of buzzing sounds, as if yearning to break through their seals and follow their master into battle.

“It’s not yet time,” the petite figure murmured.

Hearing their master’s command, the burial objects quieted down.

Chieftain Jin hurriedly entered the tomb chambers on all fours. As he neared the main tomb, his pace slowed, and he gradually assumed human form. Seeing the two figures, he steadied himself and bowed. freewebnovel.com

“Little Ancestor, the people from the Meng Family and the Dao-Seeking Sect have been sent off. The Meng heir promised to speak to his father about lending us spirit stones upon his return.”

The figure addressed as “Little Ancestor” turned around. It was a petite girl, looking about thirteen or fourteen years old.

The girl nodded, quite satisfied with Chieftain Jin’s actions. “That’s good news. With the imminent arrival of the Great Era, that old fellow from the Dijiang Tribe can no longer restrain himself. He wants to unify the Demon Region and seize the initiative. His Incipient Dao Fruit is indeed suited for this.

“Our Qiongqi Tribe need not imitate others. There is still time before the true Great Era arrives. During this period, what you all need to do is improve your own cultivation realms.”

“Yes,” Chieftain Jin and the living fossil replied simultaneously, a hint of excitement in their eyes.

The scale of the Battle of the Great Era rivals that of ancient times. If anyone today knows the situation in the ancient era best, it’s undoubtedly Little Ancestor.

Then, as if remembering something, Chieftain Jin hesitated slightly.

The girl prompted him. “If you have something to say, feel free to speak.”

“Little Ancestor, with our Qiongqi Tribe’s strength, can we truly develop to the point of being qualified to compete with behemoths like Great Xia and the Buddhist Kingdom for fortuitous opportunities in the Battle of the Great Era?”

The girl rolled her eyes, somewhat exasperated at them for not meeting her expectations like iron not turning into steel. “I didn’t say we should compete for first. Can’t we just aim to be in the top ten?”

“Oh.”

~~~

The black market was a gathering ground of fish and dragons alike, a chaotic mix of people, and rumors flew everywhere. As long as you were willing to spend money, there was no intelligence you couldn’t obtain.

In a tavern, two figures in black robes with obscured features were conversing. This was the most common attire in the black market.

“Have you heard of the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden?”

“What kind of question is that? Who hasn’t heard of the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden? When her guqin resounds, millions of sound threads slice demons to pieces, leaving not even a whole piece of flesh. That she-devil is on every tribe’s wanted list. The combined bounties would tempt even Fusion cultivators. If not for my lack of ability, I would have tried to catch her too!”

“Hai, I’m not talking about that old news. I’m asking about the news from four months ago—about the two attendants appearing beside her.”

“Two attendants? To be honest, old brother, I’ve been in seclusion for half a year and haven’t paid attention to such news.”

“Buy me a drink, and I’ll tell you all about it.”

“Waiter, bring two barrels of your finest monkey wine!”

The person sniffed. Catching a whiff of the wine fragrance, he chuckled and said, “I won’t elaborate on the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden; everyone knows about her. Just four months ago, two attendants suddenly appeared by her side. They were also human and were at the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage.

“Since gaining these two attendants, news of the Heavenly Maiden’s appearances has become more frequent. She often goes in and out of various tribe’s ancestral tombs. By the time this trio is discovered, it’s too late—they’ve already fled without a trace.

“Even if they were discovered on the spot, the Heavenly maiden had plenty of means to escape with her two attendants, infuriating those tribes that could only stamp their feet in anger.

“I heard some tribe’s tomb guardians actually welcomed the Heavenly Maiden. They steal what they guard, looting a significant number of burial objects. If the Heavenly Maiden came, they could push the blame for the missing burial objects onto her.

“Alas, these tribes weren’t worthy of the Heavenly Maiden’s attention. The tribes she targets have lineages exceeding three hundred thousand years and ancient origins.

“I heard the Heavenly Maiden’s next target is the Zhuyan[1] Tribe. She even sent an advance-notice letter.”

“So arrogant?! The Zhuyan Tribe has a Transcendent Tribulation old ancestor overseeing it. What is the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden’s background?”

“My guess is that she might be a personal disciple of Great Xia’s Thief Ancestor, and she’s here in our Demon Region to undergo a trial.”

By now, people in the tavern had crowded around, all listening to the matter of the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden. One person frowned and questioned, “Why did I hear that the Heavenly Maiden’s two attendants once introduced themselves in the Insect Tribe, saying they were from the Five-Elements Sect?”

“Don’t talk nonsense! As one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Five-Elements Sect is aboveboard in their actions. How could they do something as vile as tomb raiding?!”

“So what if they’re one of the Five Great Immortal Sects? Isn’t the Dao-Seeking Sect also one of the Five Great Immortal Sects?”

While the crowd argued over the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden’s origins, the first dark figure who shared the intelligence slipped away quietly to the outskirts of the black market.

“Senior Sister, we’re back.”

The dark figure lifted his hood—it was Meng Jingzhou.

“How did intelligence gathering go?”

“I pretended to be an informed source and spouted nonsense for half a day, and everyone in the tavern was listening. It seems they still don’t know our identities or location.”

Lu Yang soon left from another exit of the black market and met up with Gan Tian to report. “When I went to the Bai-Ze Tribe to buy intelligence on our identities and location, they said they only had guesses and no confirmed information. Seeing they didn’t know, I came back.”

Gan Tian, “...”

I gave you spirit stones to gather intelligence in the black market, yet you two didn’t spend a single one.

Over these four months, the three had been exploring ancient history in tombs while cultivating. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had progressed rapidly. At the Ninth-Layer Golden Core Stage, each step was like climbing to the sky. The two had risen from the eighth layer to the ninth layer of the Golden Core Stage. Now, they were merely half a step away from the legendary, seemingly unattainable Nascent Soul Stage!

Just as the three were inquiring about information on themselves to confirm their safety, a shocking piece of news spread through the Demon Region, reaching the entire cultivation world.

The ancient Dijiang had emerged out of nowhere. Hundreds of major tribes had pledged allegiance to the ancient Dijiang, deferentially addressing him as the Demon Monarch and establishing a Demon Kingdom. The ancient Dijiang declined three times before reluctantly accepting the demon populace’s request.

The Dijiang Tribe was in full swing, unstoppable as a wildfire as they busily prepared the coronation ceremony. The ancient Dijiang sent out invitations far and wide: to the Qiongqi Tribe, the Dragon Tribe, the Phoenix Tribe, Great Xia, the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Buddhist Kingdom, the East Sea...

Every major power had received invitations from the ancient Dijiang to attend the coronation ceremony.

“So many demon tribes have submitted?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was slightly surprised. That’s pretty fast. Is he letting loose because he thinks there are no more immortals in the current era?

One characteristic of the Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit was that the more powerful beings one controlled, the more powerful oneself became.

“These major tribes definitely have Fusion or Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. To be controlling so many demon kings and demon emperors, the ancient Dijiang’s strength is likely even greater than it was in ancient times. He rivals the old Qiongqi and is among the strongest tier of half-immortals. No wonder he dares to proclaim himself the Demon Monarch.”

Chapter 584: Invitations

The ancient Dijiang was originally very powerful. The Great Yu Imperial Preceptor survived being blown up by the Everlasting Immortal for ten days because he desperately hid in a corner of the space and was only hit by the shockwaves of the self-detonation, sustaining minimal damage. However, when the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said the ancient Dijiang could withstand ten blows, that meant standing right at the center of the explosion and taking ten direct hits—a completely different challenge compared to the Imperial Preceptor’s situation.

Moreover, how could the explosion power of the Everlasting Immortal compare to that of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

Now, with the ancient Dijiang on the path to unifying the Demon Region, his strength had reached a higher level, placing him in the first echelon of half-immortals. Even the second-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage was no match for him, a testament to the ancient Dijiang’s power.

~~~

The Dijiang Tribe.

“Have all the invitations been sent out?” The ancient Dijiang fluttered his wings slightly, emitting a faint, ancient, and mysterious oppressive aura that instilled fear in people.

The Demon Region revered the strong. Those kneeling below were the strongest of each tribe. It was by controlling these strongest individuals that he controlled these major tribes.

Upon closer inspection, one would find a complex patterned mark deep within the eyes of these demon powerhouses—a master-servant mark planted by the ancient Dijiang. Anyone marked had to obey the ancient Dijiang; their life and death were not up to them.

The Dijiang envoy had tried to plant this master-servant mark on Chieftain Jin. But who would have thought the Qiongqi Tribe’s profound foundation would shatter the token?

The Dijiang Tribe Chieftain looked at the ancient ancestor nervously. “Your Excellency, all major factions have been sent invitations. Only the Four Great Diabolic Creeds are hard to locate, and we couldn’t send them.”

“Four Great Diabolic Creeds? Wasn’t the Everlasting Creed eliminated?”

“There’s also a rising force called the Heavenly Court Creed. Its members are all from the ancient Heavenly Court...” The Dijiang Tribe Chieftain recounted the Heavenly Court Creed’s deeds in detail, from Dou Heavenly Sovereign’s appearance in Hanshui City to the young creed leader disrupting the Dao-Seeking Sect’s celebration. All the events demonstrated the Heavenly Court Creed’s strength.

The ancient Dijiang snorted coldly. “Heavenly Court? No idea what that is. I roamed the ancient era for tens of thousands of years and never heard of any Heavenly Court Creed. It’s probably fabricated by someone, like the Everlasting Creed. As for Dou Heavenly Sovereign, who knows if it’s just a play scripted by Great Yu cultivators? Nothing to fear!”

“The Ancient Ancestor is wise!”

“And our Dijiang Tribe’s prodigy has been hidden for so long. It’s time to let the world know the might of our Dijiang Tribe.” The corners of the ancient Dijiang’s mouth curved into a smile. The Dijiang Tribe’s prodigy was personally groomed by me and is considered my legacy successor—absolutely powerful.

Then, he coldly looked at the Dijiang Tribe Chieftain lying prostrate on the ground. “Who permitted you to speak to this ancestor? Don’t you know what hierarchy is? Have a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator speak to this ancestor instead.”

~~~

“Everyone should have received the ancient Dijiang’s invitations. What are your thoughts?”

The Xia Emperor had summoned the sect leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects. Six invitations lay on the table.

Qiu Jin’an shrugged. “What can we do? Just go. Watching the spectacle doesn’t cost money. Didn’t Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi mention this before? The conclusion of the discussion then was that the ancient Dijiang unifying the Demon Region could actually restrain those demons hostile to demons. In the future, whether for business or cultivator exchange, it would be much more convenient. The benefits outweigh the drawbacks. We Great Xia need not get involved.

“As for his appearance at this juncture, it’s surely related to the upcoming Great Era. However, the ancient Dijiang is still not strong enough to threaten Great Xia. We can just be spectators.”

“True.”

~~~

Golden Buddhist Kingdom.

“The ancient Dijiang wants to establish a demon kingdom?”

The Buddhist Kingdom’s ruler was tall, with a gleaming bald head. He sat on a lotus throne with the upper half of his body naked. Behind him was a Buddha statue made of immortal gold.

He gazed at the invitation he had received, turning his prayer beads quietly.

He wrote the names of those qualified to attend on paper, tore them into strips, crumpled them into balls, and began drawing lots.

“Never mind, I’ll just randomly pick someone to go.”

East Sea.

The old Dragon Emperor, nearly ten thousand meters long, coiled around a stone pillar. His cyan scales showed age, and his claws were thick with calluses. But no one dared to underestimate this old dragon. Whether it was in the East Sea or the Demon Region, no demon alive was likely older.

In his youth, he single-handedly quelled the Nine Dragons Civil War that nearly fractured the entire East Sea into warring factions.

“It so happens that it’s been a while since we had contact with our kin in the Demon Region. Sending a few young dragons over to catch up would be good. We can also ask if there’s any news about the Ancient Ancestor.”

Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

Mu Baiyi happily looked over the barbeque shop’s income. At this rate, we can definitely repay the loan within my lifetime and even have leftover resources to complete the construction of Fengdu Ghost City.

“It’s all thanks to the Heavenly Court Creed.”

Just as he was rejoicing, a subordinate delivered an intelligence that shocked him to the core.

“The Demon Region wants to establish a demon kingdom and has sent invitations far and wide to ask major factions to stand witness? Why is our Nine-Netherworlds Creed not included?

“Oh right, they can’t find our location.”

This is such huge news, yet not a single bit was leaked beforehand? Is the ancient Dijiang’s ability to control intelligence this strong?

Mu Baiyi was troubled. Theoretically, we should follow Young Creed Leader Lu’s plan and focus on earning money with the barbeque shop, not getting involved in this matter.

But then again, not attending a historic event like the Demon Region establishing a kingdom would feel like a loss when I think back about it in the future.

After brief contemplation, he called Shi Huagu over. “Ask Young Creed Leader Lu what the Heavenly Court Creed’s view is.”

Shi Huagu was similarly astonished upon learning about the ancient Dijiang establishing a kingdom. He hastily took out the Nine-Netherworlds Token and input a long message, consulting Lu Yang.

Soon, Lu Yang replied: I’ve been in the Demon Region all this time.

Mu Baiyi and Shi Huagu inhaled sharply. Who goes to the Demon Region for no reason? Young Creed Leader Lu must have known about the ancient Dijiang’s kingdom plans early and rushed over there in advance!

So this is the Heavenly Court Creed’s depth.

“Little Junior Brother, are you replying to someone?” Gan Tian noticed Lu Yang writing something.

“...Nine-Netherworlds Creed?” Gan Tian was silent for a moment before speaking in a rhetorical tone. It was the first time she doubted her hearing.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou fully disclosed the matter of the Heavenly Court Creed, emphasizing that Yun Zhi was the creed leader, with the eight elders and the Taciturn Daoist Priest acting as heavenly king protectors.

This was met with even longer silence from Gan Tian in response.

Each generation surpasses the last. Even Shifu didn’t do such things in his youth. freewebnovel.com

At the moment, the three were sitting on a beast hide, not heading to the Dijiang Tribe yet. With a month left until the palace’s construction was completed, there was no need to rush over there early.

They were going to another place—the Creation Ancient Domain.

If not for the founding of a demon kingdom, the centennial opening of the Creation Ancient Domain would be the major event that commanded the most attention in the Demon Region. When the Creation Ancient Domain opened, all prodigies of the Demon Region would participate.

Apart from cultivation level restrictions, there was only one requirement to enter the Creation Ancient Domain: pure-blood.

Coincidentally, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were pure-blooded humans, perfectly fulfilling the condition.

Chapter 585: Demon Prodigies

According to legend, the Creation Ancient Domain was a secret domain that existed since ancient times. Its master was so distant in the past that investigation was impossible, and the secret domain’s name was also lost to time.

The only known fact was that the secret domain held many fortuitous opportunities. If youth demon prodigies entering it were lucky, they could directly advance by a major realm without side effects, significantly reducing cultivation time.

Therefore, the Demon Region named the secret domain “Creation.”

Additionally, there were various natural treasures only found in ancient times. With the shift from the ancient to the modern era, environments had changed drastically, and some natural treasures with strict growth conditions couldn’t adapt and had gone extinct.

Only ancient secret domains contained these extinct natural treasures.

If not for the restrictions on cultivation levels, even demon kings would want to enter the secret domain to seek fortuitous opportunities.

“Immortal Fairy, have you heard of the Creation Ancient Domain?” Lu Yang asked. Matters of antiquity naturally require asking someone from antiquity.

“The description matches a few secret domains in my memory, but none were called Creation Ancient Domain. Names in ancient and modern times differ. Perhaps the name changed.”

Three pure-blooded humans stealthily landed in the distance and walked near the secret domain’s entrance.

It wasn’t time for the secret domain to open yet, but most major tribes of the Demon Region had already arrived. The trio had visited the ancestral tombs of these tribes and were very familiar with them. If they took out the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s cookbook, they could basically find their names there too.

Among these major tribes, the Dragon and Phoenix tribes were the most conspicuous. They were the two largest races in the Demon Region, with countless demons following them.

The dragon had nine sons. Tribes like the Chaofeng[1], Qiuniu[2], and Baxia[3] all looked up to the Dragon as their leader.

This generation’s Dragon prodigy was named Ao Yue. He appeared at the secret domain entrance in human form, with dragon horns on his head. He had handsome features and donned a yellow robe seamlessly woven with gold and silver threads.

As a clear phoenix cry resounded through the air, all the demons lifted their heads. In the distance, multicolored lights sparkled, glowing from the feathers of multifarious birds—Chongming Bird Tribe,[4] Bifang Tribe, Qingluan Tribe[5]...

Flying at the forefront were several colorful phoenixes. The Phoenix Tribe was the king of avian demons.

The avian demons landed and transformed into human form. One of them was a bright-eyed, beautiful girl with black and red eyes, brimming with vitality. Her name was Jiang Shishi. Among the elders accompanying Jiang Shishi was someone all three recognized—Jiang Shan.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had met Jiangshan at the crime scene of the forged Phoenix Blood Stones. As Jiang Shan had been taught a lesson by someone from the Dao-Seeking Sect, he became very cordial upon learning they were from the Dao-Seeking Sect.

As for Gan Tian, she was the one who had taught Jiang Shan that lesson.

The trio had also visited the Dragon and Phoenix tribes’ ancestral tombs. In fact, they could be said to be Lu Yang’s key investigation targets. He wanted to know the whereabouts of the Dragon and Phoenix prodigies, hoping they could uncover clues in the ancestral tombs.

Unfortunately, things weren’t that simple. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had scanned both tribes with her immortal consciousness and figured out their foundation and heritage, even learning many ancient secrets that the two tribes themselves didn’t know. But still no clues were found.

Aside from the Dragon and Phoenix tribes, many other demon tribes had generational feuds and were diametrically opposed.

For example, the conflict between the Heavenly Dog and Jade Rabbit tribes was well-known in the Demon Region. The legend of the Heavenly Dog eating the moon had circulated since ancient times, while the Jade Rabbit Tribe used to live on the moon.

Eating the Jade Rabbit Tribe’s home for no good reason naturally led to enmity.

“White head, red feet, looks like an ape—is that a zhuyan?”

“And that low-key and unassuming one dressed plainly—is that the Qiongqi Tribe’s prodigy who has never shown himself before?”

“I heard he voluntarily went to the humans’ Luodi Merchant Guild to learn the art of business, offering to work for free. The merchant guild was worried he would establish a merchant guild in our Demon Region upon returning and seize their territory, so they kept refusing him entry!”

“Why did I hear that the Qiongqi Tribe is plagued by poverty, and the Luodi Merchant Guild didn’t even dare to take free labor out of fear that they’d be implicated?”

“Must be rumors. The Qiongqi Tribe always has many false negative rumors. There’s even a legend that an ancient immortal suggested they rename themselves to Wangcai (Prosperous Wealth) or Fugui (Rich and Noble). That obviously sounds fake.”

“Makes sense.”

“Look! That’s the genius from the Qingqiu Nine-Tailed Fox Tribe. It’s truly like the legends—every smile and frown strikes the chords of one’s heart!”

The Nine-Tailed Fox genius was named Su Lian’er. She was dressed in white, and nine white tails swayed behind her. Red eyeshadow at the corners of her eyes added a hint of allure. Though she looked about Lu Yang’s age, she already possessed a charm that could enchant the human realm. Many demon prodigies surrounded Su Lian’er, showing infatuated expressions.

“I heard the ancient Nine-Tailed Fox was peerlessly beautiful, with legends of her captivating beauty that ‘made fish sink and geese fall, eclipsed the moon and shamed the flowers.’”

“She does resemble her old ancestor a little,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said with a nasal tone.

“She was really beautiful enough to ‘make fish sink and geese fall, eclipse the moon and shame the flowers?’”

“More or less.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted. “It was spring then, and flowers were in full bloom. The Nine-Tailed Fox and the Heavenly Dog were dueling by a lake. Their battle was so powerful that the fish in the lake dove to the bottom in fear. The geese couldn’t escape in time; caught in the attacks, they were scorched and crackled as they fell to the ground.

“The Nine-Tailed Fox used the moonlight to cast an illusion. The Heavenly Dog almost got tricked. In desperation, he used his Heaven-Earth Manifestation and swallowed the moon whole.

“By the time the two were done fighting, the ground was a mess, and flowers had withered.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Why is this different from what I’d imagined?

“After the battle, people said the Nine-Tailed Fox possessed the beauty that ‘made fish sink and geese fall, eclipsed the moon and shamed the flowers.’ I’ve always suspected she spread that legend herself. After all, when the Heaven Mandate Immortal organized sessions for high-level cultivators to learn how to maintain lofty airs, the Nine-Tailed Fox was quite into it.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was disdainful of the Nine-Tailed Fox’s petty tricks.

The ancient Nine-Tailed Fox was among the Ten Ancient Beauties, but in terms of appearance, she still couldn’t compare to me, who ranked first.

The Ten Ancient Beauties was a list determined by appearance, strength, and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s subjective evaluation. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy undisputedly put herself in first place.

From what Lu Yang knew, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy ranked the Dragon and Phoenix prodigies and her follower Qing He second to fourth based on the closeness of ties. The little Qiongqi Jincaiwei and the ancient Nine-Tailed Fox were also on the list, their rankings varying with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s mood.

Luckily, this is a list the Everlasting Immortal Fairy made up to boast about herself after knowing me. If this list had existed in the ancient era, these ten people would probably have fought fiercely over the rankings. I can only imagine the chaos.

Correction—nine people. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy proved her Dao with strength; her seizing first place is undisputable.

“Immortal Fairy, did you learn how to maintain lofty airs from the Heaven Mandate Immortal?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy raised an eyebrow, her expression bold and confident. “As the head of the Five Ancient Immortals, my every action encompasses profound meaning. Why would I need to learn from others?”

At that moment, the mental space transformed into a tropical rainforest. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy wore beast hides and a grass skirt, exuding a primitive, wild beauty.

Watching this scene, Lu Yang simply couldn’t see the lofty airs in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy at all.
