2. Qiuniu is the eldest son of the dragon. ☜

3. Baxia is the sixth son of the dragon. It is also called the Bixi, Guitie, Tianxia, or Longgui (Dragon Turtle). ☜

4. The Chongming Bird resembles a chicken and has two pupils in its eyes. ☜

5. The Qingluan is a divine bird and is considered a phoenix. It is cyan in color, thus “qing,” and frequently appears as a mount. It also often accompanies Queen Mother of the West. ☜

Chapter 586: Alliance

The Creation Ancient Domain had two rule restrictions.

One: Those who had entered the Creation Ancient Domain before could not enter a second time.

Two: Those who had entered the Creation Ancient Domain could not disclose the contents of the trials within the ancient domain.

The purpose of these two rules was to ensure the fairness of the ancient domain’s trials as much as possible. Thus, the demons and the pure-blooded humans were all equally ignorant about the Creation Ancient Domain.

That said, these rules weren’t absolute restrictions. If Yun Zhi were here, she could likely enter and exit the ancient domain without any hindrance. But such methods were too difficult; Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou couldn’t learn them.

“This ancient domain originates from ancient times, so it should be quite complex. How about finding an ally?” Lu Yang proposed.

Golden Core cultivators were the most malleable. How a cultivator cultivated and formed their golden core would affect their entire life. A classic example was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Although her Unbeatable Golden Core had shattered into a nascent soul, its profound influence persisted to this day. Hence, the Creation Ancient Domain’s entry restriction was at the Golden Core Stage.

To the entire Demon Region, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were outsiders. Even if they could fight, once the demon prodigies swarmed them, even the Unbeatable Golden Core wouldn’t help. The safest approach was to find allies.

“Sure.” Meng Jingzhou nodded steadily. Not only are we human, but we also have the dual identities of the Dao-Seeking Sect and the Meng Family. If our identities get exposed, it may bode ill for the demon prodigies.

“What about the Phoenix Tribe? They have some dealings with the Dao-Seeking Sect, and I also have acquaintances there,” Gan Tian suggested. At the moment, she had a pair of tiger ears, a blindfold, and a swaying tiger tail.

She was temporarily impersonating a member of the Qiongqi Tribe.

“The Phoenix Tribe... Senior Sister, do you know who wrote Dragon Phoenix Transformation?”

“No.”

“Our shifu wrote it.”

Gan Tian was stunned for a second. I didn’t know that.

Once again, she felt that her shifu’s misdeeds were numerous and inexhaustible; they could pop up at any time. She sighed. “Had I known, I wouldn’t have been so heavy-handed the last time I sparred with the Dragon and Phoenix tribes.”

“...How heavy-handed were you?” Meng Jingzhou asked cautiously.

“I’m afraid their future heart devils might be my image. Anyway, let’s not talk about that; it’s irrelevant now. The Dragon and Phoenix tribes probably don’t know about Shifu’s misdeeds yet. We can ally with them.”

“What about the Dragon Tribe?”

“That wouldn't exactly work. Back then, I often challenged the dragons to duels to advance through combat. My relationship with the Dragon Tribe isn’t too good. At the time, I was at the Apex Divine Transfiguration Stage. To seek a breakthrough, I circled the Dragon Tribe’s territory. If I encountered someone at my level, I’d challenge them, and if I encountered someone I couldn’t beat, I’d hide from them.

“It wasn't just the Dragon Tribe; I’ve fought the Baihu (White Tiger) Tribe, Zhuyan Tribe, Taowu Tribe, and so on.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were speechless. Third Senior Sister’s bounty is still too low.

Gan Tian continued, “However, I was caught by the Phoenix Tribe, so I had to ask Big Senior Sister for backup. She handled the elders and had me fight my peers. The Phoenix Tribe knows my identity but has never leaked it. They’re pretty reliable.”

“Then let’s cooperate with the Phoenix Tribe.” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou nodded in unison, trusting Gan Tian’s judgement.

The three approached the phoenixes, drawing wary looks from them and their avian followers.

““Halt! Who are you?” Jiang Shan shouted, eyeing the three with vigilance—especially Gan Tian, who he couldn’t help but find dangerous.

“It’s me, Gan Tian,” said Gan Tian coolly as she introduced herself.

Hearing the name, Jiang Shan staggered several steps backward.

It wasn’t only Jiang Shan. Two other phoenixes recalled the day Gan Tian pinned them to the ground and thrashed them. Their faces turned pallid, and they also retreated a few steps back.

Escorting the Phoenix Tribe’s prodigy, Jiang Shishi, was an elder of the Phoenix Tribe who had exchanged cultivation insights with Yun Zhi and knew Gan Tian’s identity.

Gan Tian asked, “We have matters we wish to discuss with the Phoenix Tribe. Could we find a quiet place?” She was referring to the Phoenix Tribe’s followers. The Phoenix Tribe is trustworthy, but I can’t say for certain about these followers.

“Alright.”

Gan Tian called the Phoenix Tribe elder, Jiang Shan, and Jiang Shishi aside. “Let me introduce you to my junior brothers, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.”

Hearing the names, Jiang Shishi was visibly moved, sizing up the two with surprise. As the Phoenix Tribe’s prodigy and future chieftain, she held herself to the highest standards and paid close attention to Great Xia’s prodigies, especially her peers of the same generation.

These two are mentioned the most in the intelligence I’ve gathered.

Lu Yang’s spells are peerless. Rumors even say he is a sword cultivator, but no one has seen his sword drawn.

Meng Jingzhou’s Pure Yang Body repels ghosts and evil. He trains hard in physique cultivation and has integrated fists and spells. His trump card is still undetermined.

Despite considering herself supremely talented, she wasn’t confident she could defeat the two.

“What do you intend to do?” the Phoenix Tribe elder asked.

“Form an alliance with you and enter the ancient domain together.”

The Phoenix Tribe elder didn’t decline immediately but contemplated seriously, weighing the pros and cons.

These two are the strongest Golden Core Stage duo in Great Xia. In terms of combat prowess, they’re undoubtedly stronger than the Phoenix Tribe’s followers.

Moreover, they are from the Dao-Seeking Sect. Jiang Shishi has been carefully protected and praised by followers since birth; her heart is too pure, and her skin is too thin—she can’t become the chieftain like this.

It’s a good chance to let the Dao-Seeking Sect’s influence rub off on her. Although the Dao-Seeking Sect had a notorious reputation in the Demon Region, the Phoenix Tribe elder knew they didn’t betray their own, so their credibility was assured.

“Sure,” he agreed.

“Fellow Daoist Jiang, I look forward to your guidance,” Lu Yang said with a smile, cupping his fists.

Jiang Shishi reacted a beat late before returning the gesture. “Likewise, Fellow Daoist Lu. I look forward to your guidance.”

“Senior Brother Jiang, we meet again.” Meng Jingzhou cupped his fists. Since they had established an alliance, they could address each other as senior and junior brothers as per Great Xia’s custom.

“It’s been a long time. The last time we met, you two were still at the Foundation Establishment Stage. I knew you would shine brilliantly at the Golden Core Stage, but I didn’t expect you to be this strong.” Jiang Shan got quite sentimental.

“Shishi, who are these two?” A hearty laugh came from the Jiuying Tribe’s young lord. Following behind was his protector from the Jiuying Tribe, who emitted a faint oppressive pressure.

Despite the hearty laugh, his eyes glinted with a gloomy hue as they scanned Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Jiang Shishi frowned, displeased with the Jiuying Tribe Young Lord. “Qin Feng, I’ve told you many times that our relationship isn’t that close. Don’t address me with such familiarity!”

“Who is this?” Lu Yang asked Jiang Shan through an auditory message.

“Qin Feng, young lord of the Jiuying Tribe. He is the final disciple of the Jiuying Tribe’s Transcendent Tribulation old ancestor. His status is no less than the chieftain’s. Since his debut in the cultivation world, he has pursued Shishi without success. He probably sees you two as rivals. Be careful.”

“Alright.”

Qin Feng didn’t pester Jiang Shishi further. After shooting warning glances at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, he left.

The Jiuying Tribe’s protector never spoke, but the oppressive pressure he deliberately released said it all.

Gan Tian sensed this and furrowed her brows.

Two more hours passed.

The ancient domain opened. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou followed Jiang Shishi inside.

Outside, the protectors and guardians of various tribes remained.

Once her junior brothers entered the ancient domain, Gan Tian left the Phoenix Tribe’s contingent. Before leaving, she told them, “When I return later, act like you don’t know me.”

Another thirty minutes passed.

Gan Tian flew in from afar on her beast hide, swaying unsteadily. Blood dripped from the beast hide—it was her blood. She was severely wounded.

“Look! It’s the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden!” An expert with sharp eyes recognized Gan Tian.

“It is her! How is she injured?!”

Gan Tian was gravely injured, biting her lip. She had flown here on sheer willpower. She bellowed in rage, “Qiongqi Tribe! You have no credibility! You hired me to explore the tombs of various tribes to uncover their secrets, and now you kill the donkey after it’s done grinding, sending assassins to get rid of me once I’m not useful!

“Even if I die, I’ll drag you down with me!”

Chapter 587: The Trials Begin

The Qiongqi Tribe elder’s expression twisted menacingly as he noticed Gan Tian’s grievously wounded state. His brows furrowed, and he retorted in a booming voice. “Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden, do not spout such venomous slanders! When did our Qiongqi Tribe ever instruct you to do such a thing?!”

The onlookers, who had been ready to capture Gan Tian the moment she appeared, tacitly held back upon witnessing this scene. Since she was gravely injured, she couldn’t flee. This was a perfect opportunity for them to uncover who was pulling the strings behind her.

Gan Tian snorted coldly. “You’ve never done it? You dare act but not take responsibility? Cowards!

“Previously, your Qiongqi Tribe sent someone to get in touch with me, asking me to secretly probe the foundations of the various tribes, focusing on determining whether any ancient old ancestors remained. I saw that your Qiongqi Tribe offered generous terms, so I accepted the commission and risked my life to investigate the tribes’ ancient tombs.

“At first, I didn’t understand what your Qiongqi Tribe intended to do. Now, I finally see the truth! Your tribe has long pledged allegiance to the ancient Dijiang. Probing the foundations of the various tribes was to make it easier to control them all!

“Now that the ancient Dijiang’s influence is firmly established, you seek to kill the donkey after it’s done grinding and silence me!”

The Qiongqi Tribe elder rebuked her furiously. “What a bunch of nonsense! Everyone knows our Qiongqi Tribe is so poor that we had to take out loans from the Meng Family! How could we be described as ‘generous?!’ If we have truly pledged allegiance to the ancient Dijiang, how could we still be this impoverished?!”

Gan Tian was momentarily stumped for words. He seems to have a point.

“Wait! I remember the first to step forward and pledge allegiance to the ancient Dijiang was the Jiuying Tribe! And the one who hired me also told me to investigate the Jiuying Tribe first!” Gan Tian suddenly pointed a quivering finger at the Jiuying Tribe elder. She trembled slightly, though it was unclear whether it was from her injuries or the betrayal. “It was your Jiuying Tribe that hired me! To wash yourselves of suspicion, you had me investigate your own tribe’s ancient tomb first!”

The Jiuying Tribe elder nearly spat out a mouthful of blood. I’ve been comfortably watching the show. How did I suddenly become part of the show?

“Preposterous!”

Gan Tian sneered. “Whether it’s actually preposterous, you know the truth in your heart! This enmity of assassinating me today shall be repaid in the future!” With that, she prepared to leave.

“Stop her!”

Seeing the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden attempting to escape, the elders of the various tribes immediately moved to surround and intercept her.

Seeing the situation turn dire, Gan Tian spat forth a mouthful of essence blood. Mustering the last of her energy, she activated the beast hide to ride the clouds and mist, leaping through space several times before vanishing without a trace. The demons were left fuming and cursing incessantly, the Jiuying Tribe being the most vehement.

Another thirty minutes passed.

After doing her makeup, Gan Tian returned to the Phoenix Tribe’s contingent, not looking in the least like someone who had been severely wounded.

Even the Phoenix Tribe elder couldn’t help but transmit an auditory message. “Was it truly the Jiuying Tribe that hired you?”

“Naturally, it’s false. That was merely a show I acted out with the Qiongqi Tribe elder, who can leverage this chance to clear the Qiongqi Tribe of suspicion. The ancient Dijiang unified the Demon Region by force, so the tribes will inevitably be discontent. Teaching the Jiuying Tribe a lesson is a perfect opportunity to sow discord amongst all the races.”

The Phoenix Tribe elder pressed further. “Did you really investigate the Jiuying Tribe first?”

“It’s false. In matters like these, wouldn’t you all believe whatever I say?” Gan Tian indeed lacked direct evidence to frame the Jiuying Tribe.

But to frame someone, what need is there for evidence? Suspicion is enough.

Gan Tian stated coldly, “Since the Jiuying Tribe has indulged their young lord, they must bear the repercussions of that indulgence.”

~~~

Having already entered the Creation Ancient Domain, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were unaware of Gan Tian’s actions. They were listening intently to the ancient domain’s rules.

The moment they stepped into the ancient domain, an androgynous voice echoed above them.

“Welcome to the secret domain. It is divided into three tiers. Only by reaching the second level may you obtain fortuitous opportunities. The higher your evaluation on each level, the more abundant the fortuitous opportunities.”

A three-storeyed pagoda materialized before the crowd, each storey representing a distinct space. It was a miniature version of the Creation Ancient Domain.

They were currently at the entrance to the first level.

“This level contains a large number of Nascent Soul demon beasts. For each demon beast slain, you shall receive one essence soul. Acquiring ten essence souls shall count as passing the first trial.

“The time limit for the first level’s trial is ten days.

“At the deepest part of the first level lies the heavenly stairway to the second level. You may ascend to the second level by possessing the requisite number of essence souls.

“Note that the second level’s trial will only commence after the first level’s trial has fully concluded.

“The first level’s trial begins now.”

A gigantic hourglass appeared in the sky, visible from any location within the first level. The sand trickled downward, marking the ten-day countdown.

“Immortal Fairy, have you seen this secret domain before?” Lu Yang asked.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “No. I don’t know if I’ve never seen it or if it appeared only after my death.”

After hearing the rules, most demon prodigies scattered, venturing into the first level to hunt demon beasts. Slaying ten Nascent Soul demon beasts was no simple feat. Not everyone could challenge those at a major realm higher like Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. Moreover, the rules stated that a higher evaluation on each floor meant better rewards. Surely, slaying more demon beasts was preferable.

Meng Jingzhou remained at the same spot, scratching his chin. The rules sound stringent, but upon closer thought, there seems to be plenty of room for manipulation.

He shot Lu Yang a meaningful glance: What’s the plan?

Lu Yang roughly deduced Meng Jingzhou’s thoughts and returned a glance: Let’s kill a few demon beasts to get a feel for it first.

“You two, shall we join forces to kill the demon beasts?” Jiang Shishi asked. The situation on the first level is well-suited for an alliance. Two can surround and kill demon beasts for higher efficiency, while the third keeps watch to prevent others from stealing the spoils.

As for the Phoenix Tribe’s followers, they could form their own teams to hunt, regrouping at the entrance to the heavenly stairway later. The followers were not bodyguards—battling the demon beasts was an excellent training opportunity, and they didn’t need to protect Jiang Shishi.

“Let’s first see the quality of these demon beasts,” Lu Yang suggested prudently. Imagine if we really run into a demon beast as talented as we are, capable of unleashing Divine Transfiguration Stage combat power while at the Nascent Soul Stage.

“Alright.” Before Jiang Shishi entered the ancient domain, her elder had advised her that if she encountered any issues within, it would be best to consult these two people’s opinions for reference.

The first level’s environment was a dense forest. Deep within the woods, Nascent Soul demon beasts watched with covetous eyes.

The trio cautiously extended their spiritual consciousness. The noise of combat not far away alerted a Broadback Giant Ape concealed in the trees.

The ape had a patch of white fur on its chest. It hammered its chest and swung from tree to tree, roaring and brandishing its fists as it lunged at the trio ferociously.

With their wealth of combat experience, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had long noticed the ape’s presence.

“Arhat Fist!”

“Slash!”

The two attacked simultaneously. freewebnovel.com

Meng Jingzhou met the giant ape’s fists with his Arhat Fist. Losing to Meng Jingzhou in strength, the ape was blasted upward into the sky.

Lu Yang pushed off with his feet, leaping upward. His sword flashed out and back into its scabbard in a single fluid motion.

The giant ape was cleaved cleanly, its massive head separating from its body and rolling to a stop at Jiang Shishi’s feet.

Jiang Shishi stared, dumbfounded. This is a Broadback Giant Ape at the Apex Basic Nascent Soul Stage, and a pure-blood at that! Yet it was dealt with so effortlessly?

“Done!”

The two high-fived, relaxed and at ease.

“Looks like they’re all ordinary Nascent Soul cultivators. We can execute the plan.”

Chapter 588: Plan

“What plan?” Jiang Shi asked curiously. With the rules this transparent, is there even room for a plan? Besides, it hasn’t been that long. Yet you’ve already devised a strategy?

“It’s quite simple, actually. Through our combat earlier, we confirmed that the demon beasts on this first level are ordinary Nascent Soul entities, well within the capabilities of you demon prodigies to handle. Therefore, to pass this first trial, anyone can accumulate the required number of demon spirits just by hunting the demon beasts diligently.

“However, to acquire more demon spirits and secure a better evaluation, one must employ some extraordinary methods.”

“By working as a trio to accelerate our hunting progress?” Jiang Shishi probed.

Meng Jingzhou shook his head, rejecting her idea. “The efficiency is too low. Moreover, did you notice the map displayed at the beginning? This first level is absurdly huge. It would take a full day just to run from the entrance to the heavenly stairway exit on the opposite side. Relying solely on the three of us to hunt would mean spending several hours merely locating the demon beasts.”

“Then what should we do?” Jiang Shishi lacked experience and wasn’t as meticulous in her observation as Meng Jingzhou was.

Instead of answering her directly, Meng Jingzhou posed a question. “You are now aware of the combat power we two brothers displayed. How would you assess it?”

Jiang Shishi stared at them for a moment before offering a fair appraisal. “Not beneath Ao Yue or me.”

Ao Yue was the Dragon Tribe’s prodigy for this generation. Jiang Shishi and Ao Yue were hailed as the two foremost prodigies of the Demon Region, demonstrating the potential to become an immortal.

This was the highest compliment possible within the Demon Region. Among all the demons who entered the ancient domain, only the two of them had received such an accolade.

“Precisely. That settles it then. With the three of us joining forces, the plan will be foolproof.”

To ensure the plan would be foolproof, the trio first dedicated eight days to slaying thirty demon beasts, amassing the requisite number of demon spirits. This way, even if their primary strategy failed, they would still clear the trial.

This period of hunting demon beasts also served as a break-in period for the three to practice working together, thereby increasing their odds of success when executing the true plan.

~~~

The eight days passed in a blur. For Lu Yang’s trio, the process of slaying demon beasts became increasingly smooth and effortless. Even Advanced Nascent Soul demon beasts could not withstand more than two exchanges against the trio’s combined might.

Lu Yang glanced up at the hourglass. “We slew a few more than planned and overshot our timeframe slightly, but it’s not a big problem. Let’s head to the heavenly stairway entrance now.”

“Alright.” Jiang Shishi felt a thrill of excitement. She had long been ready to put the plan into action.

The three quickened their pace, rushing swiftly toward the heavenly stairway entrance.

However, upon their arrival, they paused in their tracks involuntarily, staring at the scene before them in disbelief.

Lu Yang had devised a “blockade” strategy—relying on their combined combat prowess to prevent anyone else from reaching the heavenly stairway. They had assumed the other prodigies would arrive on the final day, so they only needed to block the entrance a day early.

But now, the entrance was already blocked by others.

The trio had become the ones who would be forced to hand over their hard-earned essence souls obediently!

“Haha! Didn’t expect this, did you? I overheard your plan right from the beginning!” Qin Feng, the young lord of the Jiuying Tribe, laughed uproariously at the trio’s priceless expressions. “When you first entered this first floor and formulated your strategy, I was nearby and heard the entire process!”

Qin Feng’s delight grew as he watched Lu Yang’s visage darken. “Although I don’t know who you are, I must thank you for devising such a plan. A blockade? It truly is an excellent plan. However, in terms of strength, who can match our Demon Alliance within this ancient domain? Even the Dragon and Phoenix tribes are inferior to us.”

The Demon Alliance was a concept proposed by the ancient Dijiang. Before the establishment of the Demon Kingdom, the demon races united under the ancient Dijiang’s leadership were collectively known as the Demon Alliance.

The Dijiang Tribe’s prodigy, personally trained by the ancient Dijiang, did not enter the ancient domain. The Demon Alliance’s leader was the Dijiang Tribe, but with them absent, the remaining races within wished to vie for command authority during this venture into the ancient domain.

Qin Feng had been vexed over searching for a way to secure such command authority. This is a gift delivered right to my doorstep. If I am the one to propose the blockade plan, wouldn’t the command authority of the Demon Alliance belong to me?

Indeed, as he had anticipated, while the Demon Alliance’s prodigies were still debating whether to hunt demon spirits for their essence souls or snatch them from others, Qin Feng presented this strategy. It won unanimous approval, and everyone praised the plan’s brilliance.

Qin Feng naturally and rightly assumed command of the operation this time.

He preened with pride. Behind me stand prodigies from the Baihu Tribe, the Taowu Tribe, and many others—dozens of them in total! No matter how capable Lu Yang’s trio is in combat, they could never defeat all the prodigies of the Demon Alliance!

Lu Yang’s face was ashen, his mind racing to find a solution.

As the situation fell into a stalemate, Jiang Shishi’s followers arrived one after another, equally shocked to find the Demon Alliance blockading the entrance.

Next came Ao Yue and the Nine Sons prodigies. Witnessing this scene, they knitted their brows silently.

Subsequently, it was the lone prodigies from tribes like the Qiongqi Tribe who had yet to align with any group.

The heavenly staircase entrance was already narrow, and now it was thoroughly blocked by the Demon Alliance. Sheer numbers would not be enough to break through the blockade.

Ao Yue gritted his teeth. “How do we know it can’t work if we don’t try?”

He commanded considerable influence among the demon prodigies, able to rally them. He transformed into an azure dragon soaring through the air. The Nine Sons, such as the Baxia, revealed their original forms, ready to join Ao Yue in the assault.

Inspired, the other prodigies also reverted to their original forms—a Jade Rabbit with sleek fur, a hill-sized black Heavenly Dog, a Qiongqi with a tiger’s body and two wings...

“Battle!” Ao Yue’s dragon roar shook the space around them.

He burned his dragon’s essence blood, clutched a dragon pearl in his claw, and morphed into a strip of azure fabric as he shot toward the Demon Alliance.

I alone am sufficient to slay an Advanced Nascent Soul demon beast!

“Battle!”

The prodigies erupted with unprecedented power, coalescing into a single force aimed at overcoming the blockade.

Unfortunately, the Demon Alliance had long anticipated this scenario. Under Qin Feng’s command, they moved with disciplined coordination. It was not a barrier that could be broken by mere fervor and hot-blooded courage from Ao Yue and the others.

The fierce battle raged on for half a day, yet the Demon Alliance stood firm like an iron wall, utterly unbreachable.

Finally, Ao Yue’s side was exhausted and drained, losing the battle.

Qin Feng swaggered over to Ao Yue. “Fellow Daoist Ao Yue, I have no desire to make our relationship too tense. After the Demon Kingdom is established, we still have to exchange cultivation insights and improve together.

“Why don’t we do this? Keep ten essence souls for yourself and hand over the rest to me, and I will grant you passage. How does that sound?”

Ao Yue’s head snapped up, his bloodshot dragon eyes locking onto Qin Feng with such intensity that Qin Feng recoiled in alarm.

But Qin Feng quickly recovered. What’s the use in glaring at me? He’s just furious because of his incompetence.

After a prolonged internal struggle, Ao Yue was compelled by the grim reality and reluctantly surrendered his essence souls. He had twenty of them.

“As expected of Fellow Daoist Ao Yue, you slaughtered so many demon beasts,” Qin Feng said gleefully as he accepted the essence souls.

Seeing Ao Yue submit, the other prodigies also handed over their essence souls, each keeping only ten for themselves. If they only possessed ten, Qin Feng would simply deny them passage.

Gazing at the mountain of essence souls, Qin Feng grinned from ear to ear. He distributed the pile according to pre-decided ratios among the Demon Alliance prodigies. Qin Feng received the largest share, obtaining fifty-three.

Behind the Demon Alliance ranks stood a massive chest emblazoned with the characters for “essence souls.” Qin Feng poured all fifty-three of his essence souls into the chest.

The same emotionless voice echoed once more.

“Qin Feng, fifty-three essence souls. Please proceed to the second level.”

As time was nearly up, the other Demon Alliance prodigies also submitted their essence souls to the ancient domain, thus qualifying to pass the trial and advance.

Next, it was Ao Yue’s group’s turn.

“Ao Yue, ten essence souls. Please proceed to the second level.”

“Dong Shu, ten essence souls. Please proceed to the second level.”

......

Noting there was still a little time left, Qin Feng sauntered over to where Lu Yang’s trio was. He pointedly ignored Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. I have no intention of allowing these two eyesores to enter the second level.

He stopped before Jiang Shishi, whose head was drooping, and smiled. “Shishi, I told you these two lackeys you recruited are useless. See? They can’t even pass the trial now. As long as you agree to become my fiancée, I’ll make the decision—you won’t need to hand over any essence souls, and I’ll still let you pass. What do you say?”

Jiang Shishi abruptly looked up, a smile playing on her lips. “Qin Feng, do you really think you have everything in your hands?”

“What do you mean?!” Qin Feng felt a pang of inexplicable pain at her smile.

Lu Yang let out a lazy chuckle from the side. “Fellow Daoist Qin, your eyesight is concerning. You couldn’t even recognize my clone.”

Meanwhile, the Meng Jingzhou beside him took on Lu Yang’s appearance.

A wooden clone!

Suddenly, a voice sounded from behind Qin Feng. “Fellow Daoist Qin Feng, many thanks for gathering so many essence souls on our behalf.”

Qin Feng whirled around, his eyes threatening to crack from shock and fury, refusing to believe his eyes.

Meng Jingzhou had darted out from inside the chest, holding two massive bundles of essence souls!

“We knew you were listening in back then. You didn’t really think the three of us alone planned to block the exit, right?

“The ‘blockade plan’ was specifically meant for your ears.” freewebnovel.com

The rules had never specified the method to submit the essence souls. Anyone who saw a chest labeled “essence souls” at the heavenly stairway entrance would automatically assume it was the designated deposit point. Along with everyone’s focus on the Demon Alliance, no one would notice anything amiss with the chest.

In truth, this chest had been temporarily constructed by Meng Jingzhou.

Chapter 589: The Unlucky Jiuying Tribe

Qin Feng had smugly believed his concealment was flawless when he eavesdropped on the trio’s entire plan from the shadows. But when it came to the utilization of spiritual consciousness among peers, who could possibly surpass Lu Yang?

After entering the first level, Meng Jingzhou had calculated the distance from the entrance to the heavenly stairway using the map, determining that the fastest possible journey would still take a full day.

The first layer was a circular space. Since the rules stated that essence souls were obtained by slaughtering demon beasts, everyone’s initial reaction would be to fan out from the entrance, gradually exploring the first level, hunting and killing demon beasts. No one would think of checking the situation at the heavenly stairway first.

Upon figuring out the first level’s rules, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou came up with the idea of constructing a chest at the heavenly stairway entrance to collect essence souls.

The only uncertainty in this plan was the unknown strength of the demon beasts. If Nascent Soul demon beasts could unleash power equivalent to the Divine Transfiguration Stage, the demon prodigies wouldn’t even be capable of acquiring ten essence souls. In that case, tricking them at the heavenly stairway exit would be pointless; it would be faster for the trio to simply hunt the demon beasts and obtain the essence souls themselves.

Hence, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou quickly took Jiang Shishi to slay a demon beast and ascertain its strength. After confirming that the demon beasts’ combat power was indeed only at the Nascent Soul Stage, Meng Jingzhou immediately set off for the heavenly stairway entrance, leaving Lu Yang and Jiang Shishi behind.

To avoid raising suspicion, Lu Yang employed the Tree-Planting Mantra and the Animal Form Fist, transforming his wooden clone into Meng Jingzhou’s appearance.

Subsequently, Lu Yang detected Qin Feng hiding nearby. Playing along with the scheme, he outwardly fabricated a “blockade plan” while secretly transmitting auditory messages to inform Jiang Shishi of the true plan.

This was why Jiang Shishi had appeared nervous and emotional. Had it been up to her, she couldn’t have devised a strategy like this in such a short time—she doubted she could have formulated it even if she were given ten days.

Is this the wisdom of human prodigies?

Lu Yang and Jiang Shishi then proceeded to slaughter demon beasts methodically, deliberately arriving at the heavenly stairway slightly later than planned.

This resulted in the scene that had previously unfolded.

“You’ve worked hard, Fellow Daoist Qin Feng. I’ll be accepting these essence souls!” Meng Jingzhou stood on the edge of the chest, laughing heartily. The essence souls were strung together and tied all over his body, making him resemble a zongzi (rice dumpling)[1]—a sight that elicited envy from everyone present.

“Bastard!” Qin Feng erupted in fury, transforming into his original form, the Jiuying, which had one body and nine heads. Each head had the appearance of a giant, jet-black serpent. His eighteen eyes burned red, as if they could drip blood.

He was the one who had suggested the blockade plan to the Demon Alliance prodigies. This was the reason he could naturally and rightly seize the command authority.

Now, the plan has backfired, and I was exploited by the other party, losing all the essence souls. The Demon Alliance prodigies will undoubtedly vent their anger upon me. Even with the backing of the Transcendent Tribulation old ancestor, I could never withstand the wrath of all these races.

“Return the essence souls!” Qin Feng bellowed with ire, all nine serpent heads lunging simultaneously at Meng Jingzhou.

Having anticipated Qin Feng’s foolish move, Meng Jingzhou simply shifted his feet and sidestepped the attack.

Witnessing this, the other Demon Alliance prodigies realized they had been played by Meng Jingzhou. They also revealed their true demon forms and pounced toward him.

We can’t possibly end up without a single essence soul and fail to pass even the first level!

Ao Yue’s palm crackled with lightning as he contemplated whether to join the fray in snatching the essence souls. Their essence souls were also among Meng Jingzhou’s haul.

Right then, Jiang Shishi walked over and stopped Ao Yue. She pointed at the energetic Meng Jingzhou, who was jumping around. “This is my ally. We anticipated the Demon Alliance’s actions and laid this ambush in advance. Rest assured, Junior Brother Ao Yue and all fellow Daoists, our actions target only the Demon Alliance. Once he escapes, he will return ten essence souls to each of you, guaranteeing your entry to the second level.” This was the explanation she had discussed with Lu Yang beforehand.

From the perspective of Ao Yue and the others, they were unaware that Qin Feng had been duped by Lu Yang’s group. They would only assume that Lu Yang’s trio proved superior in wit and skill—predicting Qin Feng’s actions and hiding in the chest to uphold justice. Having lost and regained their essence souls, Ao Yue and the others wouldn’t demand more; ten was sufficient. This way, Lu Yang’s trio would not only earn a favorable reputation but also secure the lion’s share of the essence souls.

Jiang Shishi was grateful that her elder had the foresight to agree to the alliance. Otherwise, I would have been left with a pitiful ten essence souls.

Sometimes, the thought sent chills down her spine. These two human prodigies are too calculating. No wonder Elder always said my cultivation talent is adequate, but my wisdom falls short. So this is what I lack.

“Many thanks, Young Lord Jiang!” The prodigies were filled with gratitude toward Jiang Shishi for her magnanimity.

Ao Yue felt a nagging sense that something was amiss, but now wasn’t the time to dwell on it. The Demon Alliance had bullied us mercilessly moments ago. Isn’t this the perfect chance to retaliate?

“Everyone, let us aid this kind-hearted fellow Daoist in breaking free!”

Ao Yue transformed into his true form, an azure dragon. His dragon pearl released lightning, and along with a roar, he swept his claws through the Demon Alliance’s ranks with unbridled attacks.

Seeing this, the demon prodigies howled and charged headlong into the Demon Alliance’s forces.

Caught between chasing Meng Jingzhou and fending off the relentless assaults from Ao Yue’s group, and further hampered by their distrust of Qin Feng and a breakdown in the chain of command, the Demon Alliance was swiftly routed and fled in panic.

“So, Miss Jiang, teaming up with us two wasn’t a loss, eh?” Lu Yang asked cheerfully. He hadn’t lifted a finger since arriving at the heavenly stairway entrance. Everything had unfolded exactly as he predicted.

Watching Meng Jingzhou jump up and down like a monkey to dodge the attacks was especially satisfying while he rested comfortably from the rear.

“Indeed, it wasn’t a loss.” Jiang Shishi nodded. It’s more than just ‘not a loss’—it is a tremendous windfall. Although the events within the ancient domain can’t be revealed to those outside, the prodigies will know best in their hearts. This single act can elevate my status and image among them significantly.

With the Demon Alliance scattered, they fled in all directions. The rules did not forbid killing and didn’t permit them to reveal the events here; if they died inside, their death would go unavenged.

Meng Jingzhou safely rejoined Lu Yang and Jiang Shishi, panting heavily from exhaustion. One look at Lu Yang’s composed demeanor confirms I was thrown the gruelling task—again.

There’s no other choice. I only have myself to blame for being unable to perform the Tree-Planting Mantra and the Animal Form Fist.

As agreed, Meng Jingzhou distributed ten essence souls to each of the prodigies. The remaining eight hundred essence souls were divided among the trio.

Everyone searched for a while but found no designated submission point. When Ao Yue tentatively stepped onto the heavenly stairway, it absorbed his ten essence souls, and he was teleported to the second level. Only then did everyone understand how to clear the first trial.

One by one, everyone queued up and entered the second floor, leaving only the Demon Alliance prodigies hiding not far away.

After observing that Lu Yang and the others had all ascended, Qin Feng also attempted to proceed to the second level. But since he didn’t possess any essence souls, a barrier materialized before the heavenly stairway, blocking his path.

The final grain of sand in the hourglass fell. The ten days had ended. All the Demon Alliance prodigies were teleported outside the ancient domain.

~~~

“Qin Feng, it’s all your fault!” The Demon Alliance’s prodigies’ eyes instantly reddened. The fortuitous opportunities within the Creation Ancient Domain are bountiful, yet we didn’t even reap the slightest benefit.

“Elder, save me!” Terrified, Qin Feng scrambled to hide behind his tribe’s protector.

Only then did he notice the atmosphere was somewhat off, or rather, palpably heavy. It felt as if the gazes from every race, faint or blatant, were fixed on his Jiuying Tribe, and the attention was far from friendly.

What happened here?

1. Zongzi is often eaten during the Duanwu Festival, also known as the Dragon Boat Festival. More information is provided in the Translator’s Thoughts section below. ☜

Chapter 590: Seed

Unaware of what had transpired in the outside world, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou continued masquerading as demon prodigies and formally stepped into the second level.

The second floor was suffused with floral fragrance, presenting a picturesque scene of flowers in full bloom. It was a seemingly boundless parterre. Within it, a graceful figure knelt, gently smelling the flowers.

Noting everyone’s arrival at the second level, the figure rose, offering a smile and a round of applause in welcome.

“Everyone, welcome to the second floor. I am the spirit of this secret domain. You may address me as Luo Hong.”

A secret domain spirit was an entity that existed only within secret domains created by Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. It was not truly alive but functioned more like a pre-programmed spell. However, this spell had accumulated sufficient experience to mimic the thought process of a living being.

The Creation Ancient Domain was an ancient secret domain. The rules on the first level had been announced in the modern language because the secret domain spirit, Luo Hong, was learning it. In the absence of the secret domain’s master, the secret domain spirit wielded the highest authority within it.

“Greetings, Senior.” Although everyone knew she was essentially a spell, none dared treat Luo Hong as such, bowing to her respectfully.

“It seems this cohort is somewhat polite.” However, such courtesy toward Luo Hong wouldn’t earn them any leniency.

She clapped her hands gently, and a flowerpot and a seed dropped from above each participant.

“The first level tested one’s martial prowess. The second level tests one’s character.

“The trial for this level is simple: grow a flower.

“In your hands is a seed of the Moonshadow Flower. When it blooms, it resembles a peerless beauty dancing under the moonlight—an enchantingly beautiful sight.

“The Moonshadow Flower’s growth cycle is fifteen days. Your task is to have a flower growing within your flowerpot within these fifteen days. Achieve that, and it will be considered a pass. I will not be supervising you all during this period.

“The more luxuriant the flower blooms, the higher your evaluation will be. freewebnovel.com

“Do note that you are forbidden from using any cultivation methods, such as spells or spirit treasures, during this time.

“In addition, you are not allowed to converse with each other. You must grow your flower independently.”

Sensing everyone’s unease, Luo Hong added with a smile. “There’s no need to be overly nervous. Moonshadow Flowers are quite easy to nurture. They will take root and sprout upon contact with soil.”

Lu Yang secretly asked, “Immortal Fairy, have you heard of the Moonshadow Flower?”

“Of course. It’s a pretty flower and very popular. Since you haven’t heard of it, it’s likely because it’s extinct now.”

The rules for the second level sound straightforward, but it’s unfortunate I can’t discuss anything with Old Meng.

Jiang Shishi carefully held her flowerpot. She buried the seed, loosened the soil, watered it, and tended to the seed with meticulous care. Yet, the Moonshadow Flower showed no signs of sprouting.

Her brows furrowed. Jiang Shishi instinctively wanted to consult Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, but she could only abandon the idea upon recalling the rules forbade them from doing so.

She began to replay the rules in her mind, pondering whether she had missed something crucial.

If it were Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, how would he approach this...

~~~

The fifteen days passed swiftly, and the day of inspection arrived.

The demon prodigies and two pure-blooded humans stood in a line, awaiting Luo Hong’s evaluation.

First in line was Su Lian’er of the Nine-Tailed Fox Tribe.

She was dressed in white robes and exceptionally beautiful. Hugging the flowerpot, she appeared pitiable and vulnerable.

The flowerpot was empty.

Luo Hong knitted her brows. “Where is your flower?”

Large tears rolled down Su Lian’er’s cheeks, evoking an urge in others to wipe her tears away. “The flower was growing well, but I have inherited my old ancestor’s legacy, possessing beauty that makes fish sink and geese fall, and eclipses the moon and shames the flowers. The moment the Moonshadow flower bloomed and saw me, it wilted.”

Luo Hong stared at Su Lian’er for a long while before finally letting out a slow breath. “Never mind, I’ll count it as a pass.”

Second in line was Jiang Shishi.

In her flowerpot, the Moonshadow Flower was in full, magnificent bloom.

Luo Hong nodded, signaling Jiang Shishi had passed.

Next was Ao Yue.

His flowerpot was similarly empty.

Luo Hong asked, “Where is your flower?”

Ao Yue cupped his fists and replied with deference, “Senior, I didn’t grow the flower.”

“Give me a reason.”

Hearing this, Ao Yue straightened his back and smiled. “Senior, you stated at the beginning that the second level tests character. In my opinion, the seeds you gave us cannot actually grow Moonshadow Flowers. This trial tests our honesty!”

“...You are eliminated.”

“Why?!” Ao Yue exclaimed anxiously. He was certain he could pass.

Luo Hong sneered. “You have the nerve to ask why? I indeed gave you all seeds that had been thoroughly boiled and couldn’t grow flowers. But who told you this trial tests honesty? Humans are cunning and thick-skinned. Why do demons need honesty? You think you can rely on your honesty to defeat humans?

“This trial tests the ability to lie.

“That little Nine-Tailed Fox lass’ lie was crude, but she still lied, so I let her pass.”

Ao Yue protested. “Then what about Jiang Shishi? How did she grow a Moonshadow Flower?”

Luo Hong sneered again. “Weren’t you listening when I stated the rules? I said, ‘Have a flower growing within your flowerpot.’ When did I ever say you had to plant the seed I gave you all?”

Ao Yue was rendered speechless. Upon closer reflection, it was indeed the case.

It wasn’t just Ao Yue. The demon prodigies behind him, also holding empty pots, hung their heads in shame. They had all assumed Luo Hong’s trial tested honesty.

Jiang Shishi exhaled a sigh of relief. Luckily, I emulated Lu Yang’s thought process, scrutinizing the rules to deduce what Luo Hong truly desired.

The prodigies lining up behind Ao Yue were unsurprisingly eliminated. Luo Hong kept walking until she reached Meng Jingzhou.

She sized him up, his active performance in the first trial having caught her attention. “Where is your flowerpot?”

Meng Jingzhou’s hands were empty—he had no flowerpot, much less a flower.

“Please follow me.” Meng Jingzhou gestured, leading Luo Hong to an area overflowing with vibrant Moonshadow Flowers. The bottom of his flowerpot was completely removed, encircling the most luxuriant Moonshadow Flower cluster like a perimeter wall.

Meng Jingzhou scratched the back of his head with embarrassment, though his grin stretched ear to ear. “Aiya, I’m so sorry! I don’t know what happened with the flower I planted. It grew so much that it burst right through the bottom of the flowerpot. As you can see, it ended up like this.

“Senior, I remember you said that the more luxuriant the flower blooms, the higher the evaluation will be, right?”

Luo Hong, “...”

I did say that, but this is just ridiculous. He clearly figured out that this trial tests one’s lying ability and is now just making things up on the spot.

“Pass.”

The last was Lu Yang. His flowerpot was empty—there was no soil, much less a flower.

“Empty. You have not pa—”

“Wait a moment.” Lu Yang raised a hand to stop her. “The condition for passing is to have a flower growing in the pot within these fifteen days, correct?”

“Correct.”

“Then I have passed.”

“Where is your flower?”

Lu Yang pointed to the vast parterre surrounding them and declared with confidence. “Throughout these fifteen days, I have been continuously planting flowers from this garden into my flowerpot, then moving them out, then planting another batch in, and then moving them out again.

“Therefore, all the flowers in this parterre are considered to have grown from my flowerpot.

“If you don’t believe me, Senior, you can check the root systems of all the flowers here. They will definitely still bear traces of the soil from my flowerpot.”

Luo Hong, “...”

The passing condition didn’t specify that it must be on the fifteenth day, but rather within these fifteen days of the trial.

Even Luo Hong herself hadn’t discovered this loophole in the rules.

“That’s not right. The second trial tests whether you possess the character to lie,” Luo Hong countered, attempting to turn the tables and reclaim her dignity.

“That’s right. Everything I just said was a complete fabrication.”

Chapter 591: Unusual Rewards

Luo Hong, “...”

Lu Yang’s words delivered such a huge blow to Luo Hong that she was momentarily unable to find the words to construct a reply.

She had been a secret domain spirit since she was born. Over the past three hundred thousand years, she had seen every prodigy of the demon race. The current chieftains had all come here to challenge the trials in their youth.

But no prodigy, regardless of their race, had left her as shaken as she was today.

The second level indeed tests one’s ability to lie, but I never imagined someone could fabricate a lie that even managed to deceive me.

Or was what he said actually a lie?

With her current knowledge reserves, she couldn’t determine whether Lu Yang’s words were true or false.

Inside the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was rolling on the floor laughing, clutching her stomach and gasping for air between peals of laughter as tears streamed down her face.

“No, no, I can’t...my stomach hurts from laughing... Hahahahaha...”

She wiped the tears from the corners of her eyes, trying to stifle her laughter, but the moment she took a glimpse at Luo Hong’s stupefied expression, she couldn’t contain herself and burst into laughter again.

Lu Yang looked at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy helplessly. Is it really that funny?

And Senior Luo Hong, you’re stumped by this? Isn’t this exactly what the trial is testing?

I, Lu Yang, always act within the rules, ensuring I never overstep their boundaries.

Since I can already excel perfectly well within the rules, why would I need to cheat?

The rules for this trial were extremely simple, and the loopholes Senior Luo Hong had left behind were also obvious at a glance. For example, the rules didn’t stipulate that the flower must bloom from the provided seed, nor that it must bloom on the fifteenth day, and so forth.

The only uncertainty was whether this trial required us to tell truths or lies. After all, Senior Luo Hong set the rules herself. If she chooses not to abide by them, who could hold her accountable?

Therefore, Lu Yang had prepared for both outcomes, preparing an empty flowerpot for the inspection.

If it tested truthfulness, he would simply state he hadn’t succeeded in growing the flower.

If it tested lying, he would bring out the elaborate explanation he had just given.

Luo Hong inhaled two deep breaths, her fists clenching and unclenching. She practically gritted her teeth as she announced the result.

“You...pass!”

She had no choice but to admit that Lu Yang’s performance on the second floor was the best in history.

Ao Yue and the other demon prodigies stared at Lu Yang in astonishment.

Which race does this guy belong to?

On the first level, he anticipated Qin Feng’s blockade at the heavenly stairway entrance and laid an ambush in advance.

On the second level, he passed using such a bizarre method.

Where did Jiang Shishi find these two geniuses?

Furthermore, based on Ao Yue’s understanding of Jiang Shishi, she should have made the same choice he did. However, the results completely defied his expectations—he was eliminated, while Jiang Shishi passed.

With the second trial concluded, Luo Hong forced herself to stop thinking about Lu Yang and performed her duties. She snapped her fingers, and a massive shower of treasures rained down, piling up into a small hill.

Luo Hong pointed at Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, Jiang Shishi, and Su Lian’er. “You four shall proceed to the third level. The rest are eliminated.

“Considering you all passed the first level, each of you may select one treasure from this pile as your reward. This treasure is for your personal use only. It cannot be transferred, nor can its contents be recited or shared with others.”

Such rules were in place to prevent mighty demon experts from seizing the treasures. After all, even demon experts would covet the treasures here.

“Demon Immortal high above, these are cultivation insights left by our ancient ancestors, which include two phases—the process of shattering the golden core to form the nascent soul and the Nascent Soul Stage itself.” The Jade Rabbit prodigy exclaimed, her rabbit ears twitching in surprise.

Luo Hong had already translated all these cultivation insights.

“Our ancient ancestors’ cultivation insights are here too!” The Qiongqi prodigy also cried out.

The cultivation insights were written with the characters “Jin Shi,” the name of the ancient Qiongqi.

It wasn’t just these two races. The cultivation insights of the ancient ancestors from races eliminated in the first level, such as the Jiuying and the Taowu, were also mixed in the pile like miscellaneous books; it was impossible to find them without careful searching.

Not all these ancient ancestors were half-immortals; many were at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

But ancient Transcendent Tribulation cultivators were different from modern ones. The former could attend lectures given by immortals and listen in on exchanges between half-immortals. Their knowledge and experiences were on a completely different level compared to today’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivators of the demon race. Even among Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, the status of an ancient demon emperor was higher than that of a modern demon emperor in the eyes of demons.

Ao Yue also found the cultivation insights left by his Dragon Ancient Ancestor, and his heart pounded wildly. The Dragon Tribe’s ancient ancestor was renowned as the strongest below the immortals—absolutely powerful.

“What is this? An immortal’s personal notes? Records of Copulation between Jinwu Golden Crows and Jade Rabbits?” The Jade Rabbit prodigy read the title and was so startled that the book nearly dropped.

Lu Yang, “...”

I remember this was research conducted by the Nine-Layers Immortal to study the changes of yin and yang. This Creation Ancient Domain’s collection is really comprehensive to have even gathered this.

Aside from the various ancient texts and copies, there were also natural treasures from ancient times.

Examples were the Longevity Grass that could prolong one’s life by five hundred years, spirit fruits that healed hidden injuries upon consumption, and all sorts of antidotal herbs.

In previous cohorts, there had been demon prodigies whose kin or lover was afflicted with lethal poison from ancient times, their lives hanging by a thread, but modern methods couldn’t detoxify the poison. Hence, they came to the ancient domain to seek long-extinct herbs from the ancient era.

In this cohort, no such situation occurred.

“These things...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned slightly, her legs swinging back and forth as she sat on a tree branch.

“What about them?”

“These things don’t seem like something an ordinary demon could have collected. Many of these cultivation insights are from half-immortals. The average half-immortal wouldn’t have the prestige and face to obtain the cultivation notes from other half-immortals.

“And then there’s this ‘Records of Copulation between Jinwu Golden Crows and Jade Rabbits.’ This is the compilation of the Nine-Layers Immortal’s research results. The copies were only distributed to the four of us; no half-immortals received them.

“Who created this ancient domain?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was perplexed.

Lu Yang’s heart skipped a beat upon hearing this.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy is implying that this ancient domain wasn’t created by a Transcendent Tribulation demon or even a half-immortal, but by one of the Four Ancient Immortals?!

“Never mind. Isn’t there still the third level? Work hard to clear it. Who knows, you might find clues there.”

“What if I still can’t find clues?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy flashed a brilliant smile, revealing eight neatly aligned teeth, and gave a thumbs-up. “Then find a secluded spot and let me interrogate and torture that little lass called Luo Hong!”

Lu Yang prayed he would find a clue on the third level.

~~~

The demon prodigies selected their desired treasures. Ao Yue did not choose his ancient ancestor’s cultivation insights and instead chose a spirit fruit that could dispel hidden injuries.

Ao Yue and the others were teleported out of the ancient domain.

Outside, the atmosphere was tense and heavy. All the demon tribes were staring menacingly at the Jiuying Tribe.

Entering the Creation Ancient Domain was a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity. Yet they didn’t gain a single reward, having been eliminated after believing Qin Feng’s nonsense.

Qin Feng hid behind his tribe’s elder, trembling like a leaf, fearing that he would get skinned alive the moment he showed his face.

Seeing Ao Yue and the rest teleported back, the Phoenix Tribe elder quickly did a head count and heaved a sigh of relief. Jiang Shishi was still inside. Given that Jiang Shishi and Ao Yue were roughly equal in ability, he had assumed she would have been eliminated alongside Ao Yue.

Gan Tian’s tone was placid. “See? I told you joining forces with us wouldn’t be a loss.”

Chapter 592: Meng Jingzhou: This Is Rigged

The Phoenix Tribe elder had also entered the Creation Ancient Domain in his youth. He knew that with Jiang Shishi’s mental state, it would be difficult for her to reach the third level; it was highly likely she would be eliminated.

But since she hasn’t been eliminated, it could only mean her mental state has improved tremendously.

To become a qualified leader, personal strength alone isn’t sufficient; one also needs cunning and thick skin. The best at being thick-skinned is the Qiongqi Tribe Chieftain.

“Who else isn’t out? Jiang Shishi and Su Lian’er?” A demon elder took a headcount and noticed the prodigies from the Phoenix and Nine-Tailed Fox tribes had yet to emerge.

“Wait, there are two others inside as well, following Jiang Shishi,” Qin Feng shouted. Although he did not know Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s race or names, their faces were absolutely unforgettable.

“Oh? Following Jiang Shishi?” The Jiuying Tribe elder narrowed his eyes, realizing an issue. “Elder Jiang Wei, this isn’t right. All of us had an agreement that each tribe could only send one person into the Creation Ancient Domain, yet your Phoenix Tribe sent three?”

He was anxious to redirect the conflict. Besides, based on Qin Feng’s account, the Demon Alliance’s elimination in the first trial was undoubtedly linked to the Phoenix Tribe!

“So what if three entered?” Elder Jiang Wei sneered, utterly unafraid. In terms of foundation, the Phoenix Tribe was the strongest race in the Demon Region. Even the ancient Dijiang didn’t dare to control them for now.

The Dragon Tribe was split into two branches: one in the Demon Region and the other in the East Sea. Thus, their foundation was also divided into two. The branch in the Demon Region could not match the Phoenix Tribe.

Elder Jiang Wei took the initiative to shoulder the matter. I can’t possibly say that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou are humans, and if I’m questioned about their origins, say that they’re from the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Claiming Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou are from the Phoenix Tribe might prevent a fight; we are always overbearing anyway.

But if I were to reveal they are from the Dao-Seeking Sect, even the onlookers would join in the fray.

And if Gan Tian sees her own people getting bullied and calls Yun Zhi over... that would be all the more livelier.

“The Phoenix Tribe is truly overbearing.” The Taowu and Baihu tribes, along with other Demon Alliance member tribes, stepped forward to support the Jiuying Tribe. If they could leverage this opportunity to weaken the Phoenix Tribe severely, they could please the ancient Dijiang.

“The Phoenix Tribe is vast and powerful. Hiding two prodigies and sending them in is of little consequence.” The Dragon Tribe elder stepped out to support the Phoenix Tribe. He had learned that Ao Yue had reached the second level with Jiang Shishi’s help and obtained a spirit fruit that healed hidden injuries. I must repay this favor.

“I think it’s understandable that the Phoenix Tribe made an exception this time.” The Jade Rabbit Tribe elder flung his sleeves as he stepped forth.

“My Heavenly Dog Tribe...”

“My Baxia Tribe...”

More and more demon tribes stepped forward to voice their support for the Phoenix Tribe. Aside from the members of the Demon Alliance, every other demon prodigy present had received assistance from the Phoenix Tribe.

“Seeing” this scene, Gan Tian’s eyelid twitched.

What in the world did those two rascals do inside the secret domain? Why are all these demon tribes standing with the Phoenix Tribe as if they’d been fed some bewitching potion?

When Shifu and the others entered the secret domain, it wasn’t like this at all.

~~~

Luo Hong teleported Lu Yang and the other three to the third level. It was nearly pitch black and contained nothing else.

Luo Hong produced four straw mats and sent them flying to the ground like she was dealing cards. “Don’t be nervous. Please sit. You four have already performed excellently in the first two levels. Even if you don’t pass the third trial, your rewards will still far exceed the others.”

For the first level’s evaluation, Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and Jiang Shishi were tied for first place in history.

For the second level’s evaluation, Lu Yang scored the highest, followed by Meng Jingzhou, then Jiang Shishi, and finally Su Lian’er.

The overall ranking was the same as the second level’s assessment. Lu Yang’s result ranked first in history, and Meng Jingzhou’s result ranked second in history.

Lu Yang appeared the least nervous. He simply sat down as he was told. The other three also took their seats.

“Well? Do you want to bet on who gets the higher evaluation in the third trial?” Meng Jingzhou waggled his eyebrows at Lu Yang, hoping to win back a round.

“That doesn’t seem proper,” Lu Yang replied with a chuckle, looking in no way like he found it “improper.”

Both were competitive individuals who refused to accept defeat. What kind of bet was it if you were guaranteed to win?

Seeing Lu Yang’s smile, Meng Jingzhou knew he had agreed and pressed on. “What’s the prize for the winner?”

“You decide.”

“The loser agrees to do one thing for the winner.”

“Deal!”

Neither of them placed restrictions like “within one’s capabilities” or “within moral bounds.” They knew any request the other party made would naturally fall within those boundaries; it went without saying.

Luo Hong cleared her throat. “As demons, you must never forget history. You should draw experience and lessons from it.

“This third trial tests your mastery of the demon race’s ancient history.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Damn it, the whole thing’s rigged! How do we even compete now?

Unaware of their internal monologues, Luo Hong continued according to the procedure. “After I ask a question, you may seize the chance to answer first. A correct answer awards one point, a wrong answer deducts one point, and no answer yields no points.

“Considering the changes over history, I will pose questions from the perspective of modern demons.

“Now, please listen to the first question: Which race did the Demon Immortal belong to?”

Both Jiang Shishi and Su Lian’er froze.

Which race did the Demon Immortal belong to? Who could possibly know that? Many demon scholars study ancient history, and there are numerous theories about the Demon Immortal’s true form. Should we just hazard a guess?

“The Demon Immortal did not belong to any race. He was the world’s only qilin,” Lu Yang answered lazily. This is purely a giveaway question.

Meng Jingzhou yawned, utterly bored, already thinking about what to eat after returning. freewebnovel.com

“Correct answer. One point awarded.”

Jiang Shishi and Su Lian’er looked at Lu Yang in astonishment. Did he make a wild guess, or did he actually know the Demon Immortal’s true form?

Lu Yang thought to himself, This is just the beginning. If you want to listen to the Qilin Immortal’s scandalous history, I could regale you for three days and three nights without stopping.

Luo Hong was rather surprised. The answer to this question came so fast.

The questions on the third level were random; each trial asked different questions. Moreover, she was only responsible for judging whether the answer was right or wrong, not providing the correct answer.

“Second question: Did the Phoenix Tribe’s ancient ancestor ever force the Demon Immortal to deploy a sword array? If yes, please describe the scene from an objective and impartial perspective.”

Jiang Shishi’s eyes lit up. I may not know other things, but when it comes to the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor, how could I not know?

Su Lian’er looked at Jiang Shishi with jealousy. Why can’t it be a question about the Nine-Tailed Fox Tribe?

Jiang Shishi excitedly raised her hand. “I know this! My Phoenix Tribe’s ancient ancestor once uttered a true sentence that suppressed the Demon Immortal so hard he couldn’t lift his head, forcing him to kneel on the ground with a thud. Under immense pressure, the Demon Immortal activated a sword array in an attempt to resist, but he still failed and was defeated!

“This was the famous ‘One Sentence, Immortal Kneels!’

“Based on my conjecture, this probably happened before the Demon Immortal became an immortal.” Otherwise, it wouldn’t have made sense for the Demon Immortal to lose to the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor.

“Wrong answer. One point deducted.”

“What?!” Jiang Shishi thought she had misheard. This is a story I’d heard directly from our chieftain! It is absolutely true and reliable! How could it be wrong?

With no one else answering, Lu Yang sighed softly. “Senior, I’m not exactly sure which incident you are referring to. The only one I can confirm is the day the Demon Immortal returned home, and the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor stared at him, coldly asking, ‘Which paramour did you visit?’

“Hearing this, the Demon Immortal’s expression changed dramatically. He pulled out his sword array, knelt on it with a thud, and swore to the heavens he wouldn’t dare do it again, vowing that if he ever transgressed again, may he be struck by five lightning bolts.”

“Correct answer. One point awarded.”

Chapter 593: How Did I Become Second Place?

This wasn’t the first time the Qilin Immortal had knelt upon a sword array. The number of instances Lu Yang had heard was already at least a dozen; the actual number was undoubtedly higher. He couldn’t be certain of the specific reason for this particular incident of kneeling on the sword array.

As for the Qilin Immortal swearing to the heavens... with the Heaven Mandate Immortal around, forget being struck by five lightning bolts—you would have been fine even if you were struck by lightning every day.

“What?!”

Jiang Shishi stared at Lu Yang, dumbfounded, then shifted her gaze to Luo Hong’s face. She repeated this three times before finally accepting that Lu Yang’s answer was indeed correct.

But this wasn’t what the chieftain told me, though? How do these two know more about my Phoenix Tribe’s history than our own chieftain?

“Wait, what do you mean by ‘paramour?’ What was the relationship between my ancient ancestor and the Demon Immortal?” Jiang Shishi seemed to have stumbled upon some monumental information within Lu Yang’s answer.

Didn’t historical texts record that our ancient ancestor and the Demon Immortal were rivals? They battled fiercely for a position as an immortal, and in the end, our ancient immortal failed, while the Demon Immortal succeeded.

Why would our ancient ancestor speak to the Demon Immortal with that kind of tone? This doesn’t align with the history I know at all.

Jiang Shishi’s mind was a murky paste. A single question had overturned her entire understanding and her previous knowledge.

Meng Jingzhou glanced at the dazed Jiang Shishi and went back to pondering what to eat after returning.

Su Lian’er also stared at Lu Yang in astonishment. How could anyone know more about the Phoenix Tribe’s history than Jiang Shishi? Just what is the background of this guy called Lu Yang?

Luo Hong paid no mind to their reactions. Whatever their reactions were, it didn’t affect her asking questions; it was all part of the procedure.

“Please listen to the third question. The Dragon Tribe’s ancient ancestor was overwhelmingly powerful, a hurdle all demons had to face on their path to immortal ascension. In the ancient era, there was a demon genius. Although his cultivation talent was concerning, he possessed exceptional talent for researching divine abilities.

“This genius studied assiduously, forgetting sleep and food, and developed a mighty divine ability called ‘Eighteen Dragon-Subduing Palms.’[1] Theoretically, if one could master these eighteen palms, even the Dragon Tribe’s ancient ancestor would be defeated by this alone.

“However, this genius never perfected this mighty ability. What happened?”

The Eighteen Dragon-Subduing Palms was a widely known mighty ability passed down from ancient times in the Demon Region. Its power was unquestionable. All demons were searching for traces of this move, yet their efforts were futile. There were many theories about why this technique was never perfected.

Su Lian’er rushed to answer first. “According to my tribe’s ancient texts, this genius spent his entire life yet failed to perfect this divine ability. I suppose his talent was ultimately limited.”

Luo Hong offered no evaluation. Su Lian’er’s answer couldn’t be considered wrong.

Noticing Luo Hong’s silence, Jiang Shishi provided another answer. “Our ancient texts have similar records. They state that this divine ability was too heaven-defying. This genius encountered a life-and-death tribulation and failed to overcome it despite exhausting all his power. Thus, he perished with his body and Dao destroyed before he could perfect the divine ability.”

Luo Hong shifted her gaze to Meng Jingzhou, signalling he could answer.

Meng Jingzhou looked back at her, signalling her to ask someone else.

Luo Hong shifted her gaze to Lu Yang.

Lu Yang was thin-skinned and felt rather embarrassed from being stared at by Luo Hong. After hesitating for a moment, he divulged an ancient secret. “Regarding this matter, I’ve heard a little. It’s said that the Dragon Tribe’s ancient ancestor wielded the Natural Selection Incipient Dao Fruit. Its effect was that if she endured an attack without dying, it would make her stronger. Thus, if she withstood a complete version of the Eighteen Dragon-Subduing Palms without dying, she would become even more powerful.

“After hearing about this genius’s feats, she visited him, hoping he could perfect the technique to help her grow stronger. The genius was also extremely delighted upon learning this. He wished the Dragon Ancient Ancestor could demonstrate her full power to give him a reference.

“The Dragon Ancient Ancestor unleashed her full power. Winds and clouds shifted, great stars shattered—it was like doomsday. Witnessing this scene, the genius was frightened to death.

“At the time, people called this genius ‘Lord Ye.’ This is the famous tale of ‘Lord Ye’s Love of Dragons.’”[2]

Luo Hong nodded, satisfied with Lu Yang’s answer. “Correct answer. One point awarded.

“As for you two, your answers were not entirely correct. No points awarded or deducted.”

The oblivion trait belonged to complete Dao Fruits; the incipient form lacked this trait. Hence, everyone could remember what Lu Yang said about the Incipient Dao Fruit.

“Next, please listen to the fourth question. The Dragon Ancient Ancestor and the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor engaged in an intense battle when they were half-immortals. The Phoenix Ancient Ancestor died and came back to life in that battle. Please describe this battle in detail.”

Upon hearing this was another question about her Phoenix Tribe’s ancient ancestor, Jiang Shishi’s face lit up with excitement.

I know this battle well! Every movement of the two ancient ancestors emanated immense power. Even the stars in the sky were reduced to dust, the great sun was extinguished, and the universe fell into deathly silence. It was an unprecedented battle of the era! Our Phoenix Tribe’s ancient ancestor was even reborn from the ashes, awakening within the flames.

Both the Dragon and Phoenix tribes took tremendous pride in the formidable power their ancient ancestors displayed in that battle.

She was just about to answer when she remembered Lu Yang’s previous performance. She turned her head toward him. “You answer first.”

Lu Yang’s eye twitched. He actually wasn’t eager to answer this question, lest it ruin the image of the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor in Jiang Shishi’s heart. But since she has already yielded the opportunity to me, I can’t refuse.

Fortunately, the events in the ancient domain can’t be spoken of outside. Otherwise, just these few answers of mine would cause an uproar throughout the entire Demon Region if word got out.

According to the Immortal Fairy, their battle involved setting fire to burn paper, pulling hair, and drawing circles to curse each other.

Directly repeating that verbatim would seem rather disrespectful.

He adopted a solemn expression and spoke in a deep voice, as if he was showing the utmost deference toward the Dragon and Phoenix ancient ancestors. “That battle caused heaven and earth to collapse and space to shatter. The two ancient ancestors unleashed their most powerful methods. Despite hundreds of rounds, neither could gain the upper hand. They used their respective races’ true flames as their primary means of attack. Half-immortal-grade talismans blazed furiously within the true flames, their light piercing the heavens. The might of the talismans shook the past and illuminated the present. The two also used parts of each other’s bodies as mediums to cast unparalleled curses, filling the entire universe with an inauspicious energy.

“The Phoenix Ancient Ancestor was slightly inferior. She died under the curse, but was resurrected within the flames.”

In reality, the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor had used the Play-Dead Technique to feign death, but it was painful getting burned by the Dragon Ancient Ancestor, so she jumped up and howled.

Best not to mention this part.

“Correct answer. One point awarded.”

Jiang Shishi was racked with regret. I could have answered that question too!

“Sixth question: The Nine-Tailed Fox Tribe’s ancient ancestor captivated the world with her charm...”

“Seventh question: ...”

Jiang Shishi and Su Lian’er competed to answer, continuing until the tenth question.

“All ten questions have concluded. Lu Yang scored ten points and passed the third level.”

Out of the ten questions, Su Lian’er answered five incorrectly, scoring minus five points and ranking fourth.

Jiang Shishi answered four questions incorrectly, scoring minus four points and ranking third.

Meng Jingzhou didn’t answer a single question, scoring zero points and ranking second.

“I’ve decided. I’ll eat mung bean cake[3] after we get out.” Meng Jingzhou had finally decided on what to eat.

Returning to his senses, he discovered the competition was over.

“How did I become second place?”

2. This idiom is used when one pretends to be fond of something they actually fear. The story is about a county’s senior official, whom people called “Lord Ye.” He told people he loved dragons, carving a pair of dragons on the stone pillars outside his house, placing a pair of dragons on the roof, and decorating his garden—stones, walls, steps—with dragons. He even named his children after the character for “dragon.” A true dragon learned of his love for dragons and decided to pay Lord Ye a visit to express his gratitude.
