Chapter 594: The Fourth Level

Due to his status as the eldest young master of the Meng Family, Meng Jingzhou was exceedingly well-informed about the modern cultivation world, even more so than Lu Yang.

When it came to ancient history, however, he was completely in the dark. Furthermore, considering the significant discrepancy between the ancient history known by modern cultivators and the actual ancient history, it went without saying.

There was no need for comparison. He suggested that Lu Yang be given a free pass for this level. Just as he had anticipated, Lu Yang answered all ten questions correctly, achieving a full score to pass the level—an unprecedented feat.

But he hadn’t expected his zero points to earn him second place.

Luo Hong cast approving glances at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. “Your results rank first and second in history respectively. Good job.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

What Meng Jingzhou didn’t know was that every prodigy who could reach the third level in every cohort was the best of the best. They were immensely erudite, familiar with events from ancient to modern times. Once the buzzer round began, they would rush to answer the questions out of confidence in their knowledge.

And then they ended up with negative scores.

Losing once could be an accident. Wanting to rectify their scores, they would continue competing to answer the questions. The more they answered, the lower their scores dropped.

By the time the ten questions concluded, it was a contest of who had the most negative points.

Luo Hong pointed at Meng Jingzhou, Jiang Shishi, and Su Lian’er. “You three may receive your rewards.”

With a snap of her fingers, a small mountain of treasures materialized, glittering with golden light. Each item was incredibly valuable, capable of fetching astronomical prices and sparking frenzied scrambles for it.

Unlike the second level, the treasure hill this time was of even higher value, containing even mighty divine abilities long lost to time, such as the Eighteen Dragon-Subduing Palms.

Above each treasure hovered a light indicator. Most were marked with “one,” and a few with “two” or “three.” For example, the Eighteen Dragon-Subduing Palms was marked with a “three.”

“Su Lian’er, your performance on the first level was average. On the second level, you failed to see through what I intended to test; lying is your instinct. Your performance on the third level was also average. You may select one item from here.”

“Many thanks, Senior Luo Hong!” Before entering the Creation Ancient Domain, she had never imagined she could reach this point. It had far exceeded her expectations.

“Jiang Shishi, you obtained two hundred and eighty essence souls on the first level, setting a historical record—an extremely outstanding performance. On the second level, you saw through what I intended to test. Your performance on the third floor was average. You may select three items from here.”

“Many thanks, Senior Luo Hong.”

“Let me remind you, you can choose most treasures freely, but some items are so valuable that selecting one is equivalent to selecting two or three.”

The Eighteen Dragon-Subduing Palms was marked with “three.” Choosing it would be equivalent to selecting three items. The complete version of the Eighteen Dragon-Subduing Palms could defeat the Dragon Ancient Ancestor and was a top-tier, mighty divine ability. Even an incomplete version would allow one to dominate their cultivation realm once mastered.

Luo Hong then turned to Meng Jingzhou and summarized, “You obtained two hundred and eighty essence souls on the first level, jointly setting a historical record with Jiang Shishi—an extremely outstanding performance. On the second level, you not only saw through the trial’s content but also planted numerous flowers in the flowerpot. On the third level, you achieved the second-best result in history. You may select five items from here.”

Being able to select five items indicated that Meng Jingzhou’s overall result could rank second in the entire history of the Creation Ancient Domain. If Lu Yang’s results hadn’t preceded his, he could have ranked first.

Su Lian’er chose a defensive ancient talisman, capable of blocking a strike from a Fusion cultivator at full strength.

Jiang Shishi chose a Phoenix Visualization Drawing. The phoenix in the painting was vividly lifelike, its wings spread as it soared, seemingly ready to fly out of the canvas at any moment.

This painting was the work of a half-immortal. It had the effects of calming the spirit, enabling a focused mind, and reconstructing bloodlines, accelerating the process of bloodline awakening. It was filled with boundless mysterious wonders.

It was marked with a “three.”

Meng Jingzhou found himself in a dilemma while selecting. Most of these items were of little use to him. If he wanted them, he could find them in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Hmm? What cultivation technique is this? Such a strange name. Primal Chaos, One Qi, Two Origins, Four Divisions, Six Directions, Eight Corners, Nine Lands, Ten Heavens, Only I Reign Supreme Immortal Art?

“Such a long name?” Don’t understand.”

Meng Jingzhou flipped through the manual. The text within had been translated. The cultivation manual was marked with a “five,” making it the most valuable among all the treasures.

“So expensive, yet it’s only half a manual?” He grumbled. The cultivation manual only detailed the cultivation process from the Qi Training Stage to the Nascent Soul Stage; it was only the first half.

“Numbers Immortal Art?!”

Upon hearing the name, Lu Yang’s eyes widened sharply. That thing exists here? This is the Nine-Layers Immortal’s cultivation technique!

“You’ve heard of it?” Meng Jingzhou asked.

Lu Yang nodded. This is absolutely an amazing treasure. “Don’t exchange for it yet. Let me ask first.”

He turned and entered his mental space. “Immortal Fairy, do you know the contents of the Numbers Immortal Art?” If the Immortal Fairy can recite it from memory, there’ll be no need to acquire it.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy revealed a look of disdain. “Is it not enough that I remember the name of the Nine-Layers Immortal’s cultivation technique? Why would I bother remembering the contents?”

“Then what about that half a cultivation manual in Old Meng’s hands...”

“Just exchange for it. This cultivation technique is pretty good. The Nine-Layers Immortal boasted about it in front of me, saying that different people would gain different insights from it, and that it aids in comprehending one’s own divine abilities and understanding others. There were other benefits too, but I can’t recall them.”

Having received an affirmative answer, Lu Yang exited his mental space and nodded firmly, uttering a single word. “Exchange.”

Without hesitation, Meng Jingzhou exchanged for this half a manual of an immortal art.

Luo Hong waved her hand. “You three may leave.”

Before they could even say anything to Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou and the other two were teleported out of the ancient domain.

Only Lu Yang and Luo Hong were left in this vast space.

“Senior Luo Hong, you...”

Luo Hong circled Lu Yang with keen interest, clicking her tongue in amazement. “I have seen a few lucky ones who guessed one question correctly. But someone like you, who answered all ten correctly? That has never happened before. I always believed no one would ever be able to answer all ten questions correctly.” freewebnovel.com

Luo Hong snapped her fingers. The third level instantly brightened, revealing a city bustling with horses and carriages, people coming and going, and great demons walking among them. Demons and humans coexisted harmoniously, presenting a scene of a prosperous golden age.

“Don’t be surprised. This is the illusory domain I usually live in. It has been three hundred thousand years. I couldn’t possibly have spent every day planting flowers and mingling with demons. Where you need to go is the fourth level.”

“The fourth level?”

In the model of the ancient domain shown upon entering the ancient domain, there was no space for a fourth level.

Luo Hong simply smiled, gesturing for Lu Yang to look up at the sky.

A beam of light appeared in the sky, transforming into a golden stepladder that connected the third level to the fourth. The living beings within the city stopped in their tracks, gazing up at the sky. They pointed at the golden heavenly stepladder with a mixture of fear and curiosity.

“The one who created me told me that if anyone could clear the secret domain, they were to be sent to the fourth level. The fourth level is beyond my jurisdiction. I do not know what lies there.”

“Who created you, Senior?”

“I will tell you after you return from the fourth level,” Luo Hong said with a wide smile.

It was obvious to Lu Yang now. Unless I reach the fourth level, Senior Luo Hong won’t divulge a single word.

But that’s not a problem. I’d intended to go to the fourth level anyway.

“Then I shall take my leave for now, Senior.” Lu Yang cupped his fists.

“Go on, go on. I shall await your return.”

Lu Yang stepped onto the golden heavenly stepladder. The moment his foot made contact, a warm current flowed through his whole body, infusing him with strength.

Subsequently, Lu Yang disappeared into the fourth level. The golden stepladder crumbled, transforming into a shower of golden rain that scattered across the city.

~~~

The fourth level was completely different in style from the first three levels. It resembled a lady’s boudoir. Attention to detail was evident in every corner, hinting that the room’s owner must have been a meticulous person.

“This room looks familiar,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked. Since there was no one else around, she emerged from the mental space, her attire still brimming with a wild nature.

Chapter 595: Jiang Lianyi

Before coming to the ancient domain, Lu Yang had never imagined his training experience here would involve so many matters. Considering the Creation Ancient Domain’s renown in the Demon Region, he and Meng Jingzhou had discussed that since they were already here, it would be a waste not to go. Thus, they entered the ancient domain under Gan Tian’s lead.

Unexpectedly, they had encountered comprehension insights left by ancient great demons and even stumbled upon the Nine-Layers Immortal’s cultivation technique.

The fourth level of the Creation Ancient Domain was unknown to any prodigy who had entered the ancient domain in the past three hundred thousand years. It was a place even the secret domain spirit, Luo Hong, was unqualified to set foot in.

Now, it welcomed its first visitor.

It was deathly silent here. The hollow echo of footsteps reverberated, as if someone was following behind.

Lu Yang carefully observed the fourth level. The room was decorated with an understated yet profound essence. The owner is presumably a senior of exceedingly refined bearing.

Every single ornament in the room exuded age and extraordinariness. Lu Yang could only identify the origins of a small portion.

A tone table carved from top-grade spirit stone marrow, jade chairs fused from the essence of the sun and the essence of the moon, liuli-glazed floor tiles refined from special star cores, a Kunlun bronze mirror, Dao Enlightenment teacups, Ever-Bright Immortal Lamps...

These were things Lu Yang had only ever seen within his own mental space; the Everlasting Immortal Fairy occasionally changed the style of the mental space.

When Lu Yang heard the Everlasting Immortal Fairy introducing them previously, his eyes had twitched. The value of these items was beyond his imagination. Now, seeing them materialize before his eyes was an entirely different feeling.

Lu Yang noticed an emerald-green jade flute hanging on the wall. It was slender and elegant, its details exquisite. The design of a hundred birds was vividly lifelike, giving a sense of lightness and purity.

At the far end of the room lay a bed shrouded in a curtain of light gauze. One could only make out the figure of a female cultivator lying upon it.

“Immortal Fairy, have you remembered whose room this is?” Lu Yang asked softly, worried about disturbing the room’s owner.

“It’s Jiang Lianyi.”

Jiang Lianyi was a prodigy of the ancient Phoenix Tribe, the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor, wife of the Qilin Immortal, and one of the Ten Ancient Beauties.

Lu Yang’s hand, which was about to part the gauze curtain, paused momentarily as he thought to himself, As I thought. He drew aside the curtain and saw a peerlessly beautiful woman lying on the bed, clad in bright crimson robes like a flame.

It was none other than the legendary Jiang Lianyi.

Her breath was gone, her vitality dissipated. Her lips were pale, and her eyes were tightly shut. Wearing a serene expression, she had her hands crossed over her chest.

“Has she passed away?” Lu Yang’s voice quivered, his face full of disbelief. He knew the methods archaic cultivators used to slumber. No matter how deep their slumber was, one could still sense a faint aura from them, completely different from Jiang Lianyi’s condition.

How could a great legendary figure like Jiang Lianyi possibly have died?

But at the thought of the Epoch Immortal’s corpse buried beneath the Five-Elements Sect and the old Qiongqi within the black coffin in the Qiongqi Tomb, Lu Yang had no choice but to accept this fact.

The affairs of antiquity are shrouded in mystery; anything is possible. The only thing I can do is accept it. freewebnovel.com

He wondered if the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could accept it. She shared a close bond with Jiang Lianyi. Despite the Immortal Fairy’s usual cheerful demeanor, facing the departure of a friend must weigh heavily on her heart.

If Jiang Lianyi is dead, then what about the Dragon Ancient Ancestor, Ao Ling? And what about the Qilin Immortal? Their circumstances probably aren’t much better. It’s even possible that all three had perished.

“She’s not dead. This is the Play-Dead Technique.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy glanced at Lu Yang, whose expression was complicated as he struggled to accept the news of Jiang Lianyi’s demise. Why are you cursing her for no reason?

Lu Yang fell silent for a moment. “...Play-Dead Technique?”

Immortal Fairy, why couldn’t you have said that earlier? I grieved for nothing.

“Did you forget? I taught her the Play-Dead Technique. Back then, she wasn’t skilled and got burned until she howled in pain...”

“Alright, enough, stop talking.” Lu Yang hurriedly cut off the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s reminiscing. Talking about this in front of the person in question doesn’t seem very appropriate.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy placed her hands on her hips, looking quite proud. “My Play-Dead Technique is far more reliable than petty methods like being frozen by ice. The principle of being frozen by ice is to slow down time, reducing the rate of lifespan loss. But the lifespan will still drain away eventually. Some unlucky fellow might oversleep and sleep until death.

“For example, the ancient Dijiang had seventy to eighty thousand years of lifespan before sealing himself. Upon waking this time, he probably only has twenty to thirty thousand years left.

“In contrast, once the Play-Dead Technique is cast, it is equivalent to death. There’s no need to worry about lifespan depletion at all.”

In a state of death, how could there be any exhaustion of lifespan?

“Step aside. I’ll revive her,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy instructed Lu Yang.

Lu Yang moved aside as he was told. Such matters are beyond the capabilities of a Golden Core old ancestor.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy extended her index finger. Dao charm flowed at her fingertip, and endless Great Dao talismans emerged, gathering above her head. They collided silently, the impacts producing resplendent light that forced Lu Yang to close his eyes.

The massive tide of talismans poured down, converging madly upon her fingertip. Her index finger gently touched Jiang Lianyi’s brow, sending out ring after ring of invisible ripples. It felt like a wind had passed, causing the gauze curtains around the bed to billow and making the stone table, jade chairs, and bronze mirror tremble slightly.

Swept by the ripples, Lu Yang sensed the dual charm and taste of death and life, yet upon closer inspection, there was nothing. It was truly bizarre.

Jiang Lianyi’s complexion turned from pallid to rosy. In the blink of an eye, it became as flushed as a living person’s. Her long eyelashes fluttered as if she was about to wake up.

“Mmm~~” Jiang Lianyi let out a lazy hum, graceful and indolent, exactly like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy when she just woke up.

As Jiang Lianyi returned from death, the entire fourth level came to life. The stone table, jade chairs, and bronze mirror swayed rhythmically as if they were dancing, while the jade flute on the wall emitted a lively melody... It was as if they were cheering and celebrating their master’s awakening.

Jiang Lianyi sat up on the bed, her head muddled. She felt like she had slept for a very, very long time, so long it had to be measured in units of ten thousand years. Her memories were somewhat blurred, and she continuously sorted through them in her mind.

Gazing around her surroundings, she momentarily forgot why she had slept here and why she had woken up now. Right as she turned her head, a face even prettier than hers drew near.

“Lianyi, you’re awake?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clambered onto the bedside and leaned close to Jiang Lianyi, giving her quite a fright. Seeing Jiang Lianyi awake, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s lips curved upwards in a brilliant smile, her eyes sparkling with delight.

“Who are you?” Jiang Lianyi stared blankly at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. I, an almighty half-immortal, detected nothing when this person approached me.

“You don’t recognize me anymore? I’m Huang Doudou—the Everlasting Immortal Fairy Huang Doudou,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy introduced herself earnestly.

Jiang Lianyi was a cautious person, yet she found herself utterly unable to raise her guard toward this girl who had suddenly appeared.

Two distinct trails of tears streamed down Jiang Lianyi’s cheeks uncontrollably. She continuously wiped at them with her wrist, but the tears fell in large drops and were unstoppable.

Even though she was crying, an indescribable joy welled up in her heart.

“Strange, why am I crying?”

Chapter 596: Trust

When Jiang Lianyi asked, “Who are you?” Lu Yang’s heart wrenched painfully.

It seems the mastermind behind the scenes had completely erased the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence. It wasn’t just replacing her name in books—it was altering memories, wiping out all traces of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy from everyone’s minds. Even someone as powerful as Jiang Lianyi was not spared.

Jiang Lianyi was a peerless half-immortal qualified to contend for a position as an immortal. If even she couldn’t escape it, one can imagine the case for other cultivators and mortals.

No wonder nobody had uttered the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s name to resurrect her after her death.

“Everlasting Immortal Fairy Huang Doudou?”

Jiang Lianyi stopped her tears. She found the name utterly unfamiliar, with not the slightest impression left in her mind; confusion clouded her eyes.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s smile gradually faded. Although she had mentally prepared for it, truly learning that Jiang Lianyi had forgotten her still brought disappointment and sorrow. “That’s right, I am the Everlasting Immortal Fairy Huang Doudou! Alongside the Qilin Immortal, Nine-Layers Immortal, Heaven-Mandate Immortal, and Epoch Immortal, we were known as the Five Ancient Immortals. I was the last to become an immortal among us five!”

Jiang Lianyi countered, “The last to become an immortal was my husband; he was the fourth to ascend. There were only four immortals in ancient times. How could there be a fifth?”

“Then what about Little Ling’s and your culinary skills? I taught you two how to cook!”

Little Ling was the Dragon Ancient Ancestor, Ao Ling.

Jiang Lianyi replied, “We were self-made geniuses. No one taught us.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “And the Play-Dead Technique! The technique you just performed was something I taught you and Little Ling!”

Jiang Lianyi elaborated, “The Play-Dead Technique was something Little Ling and I obtained while exploring a secret domain. It was an ancient ruin, so old its origins couldn’t be verified. After we left, the secret domain collapsed into ruins.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pressed on. “When you two married the Qilin Immortal, I gave you all an immortal fruit! On the fruit was written ‘For the Most Beautiful Demon!’”

Jiang Lianyi denied it. “I don’t remember such a thing at our wedding. When we married, the three immortals—Nine-Layers, Heaven Mandate, and Epoch—came to congratulate us and gave us immortal fruits. But none of the immortal fruits had ‘For the Most Beautiful Demon’ written on them.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was undeterred. “We often ate meals together! And your cave abode, your bedroom—I’ve visited them all!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy listed events after events, describing them vividly, but she only received Jiang Lianyi’s silence in return.

Jiang Lianyi remained silent for a long time.

“I’m sorry. I have no recollection of everything you’ve said.”

Jiang Lianyi was no longer groggy like she was when she just woke up. Having quickly sorted through all her memories, she even clearly remembered the events right before she entered her slumber.

At the time, my hubby’s behavior was very strange. He stubbornly insisted I use the Play-Dead Technique to enter a death state, without even explaining why. Out of trust, I performed the technique. Upon waking up, I saw an unfamiliar woman and a Golden Core cultivator.

She was certain her memories were clear and complete with no loopholes. They were logically consistent from beginning to end and were not the slightest bit related to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes glistened, tears stubbornly swirling within them, refusing to fall.

When Jiang Lianyi saw her like this, her heart ached terribly for reasons she couldn’t grasp.

“Immortal Fairy...” Lu Yang wanted to console the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, but when he tried to pat her shoulder, his hand passed right through; the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was in a soul state.

Just as Jiang Lianyi was about to say something comforting, she felt something in front of her chest. She instinctively reached for it and touched a stone.

“Recording stone?” Jiang Lianyi grew even more baffled. I don’t remember having this stone before my slumber. Did my hubby slip it in?

She channeled spirit energy into the recording stone. Magnificent yet complex patterns appeared on its surface. The phantom image of a man with coral horns on his head materialized. The man bore an elegant demeanor and was clad in black robes embroidered with the design of myriad beasts.

“Qilin Immortal?”

“Husband?”

This male phantom image was none other than the Qilin Immortal.

Lu Yang also recognized the Qilin Immortal. Come to think about it, this is the second time I’m seeing the Qilin Immortal—the first time was a historical projection, and now it is a phantom image.

“Lianyi, you must have many questions in your heart. You will meet someone. Please do not panic. This person is trustworthy, even more so than me or Heaven Mandate and the others!

“You will find this person very unfamiliar, with no memory of her origins. Please think about it. If this person has no connection to you at all, how could she have undone your Play-Dead Technique?”

Jiang Lianyi froze. That’s right. The ancient ruin had vanished. Only Little Ling and I know the Play-Dead Technique. My husband, Heaven Mandate, Nine-Layers, and Epoch didn’t learn it, and neither did they need to.

How does this woman who calls herself the Everlasting Immortal Fairy know the Play-Dead Technique?

The Qilin immortal phantom image continued, “Someone has altered your memories, but I don’t know this person’s identity yet. You don’t need to know the details of this matter; do not get involved. This is a battle at the immortal level. The only thing you need to know is that the person who awakened you is trustworthy!”

Then, the Qilin Immortal phantom image turned to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, revealing a smile and applauding to congratulate her. “Everlasting, you’ve finally been revived! I just don’t know how far in the future your era is from mine. I am very sorry we never managed to resurrect you. The enemy’s methods exceeded our expectations. Not only half-immortals, but even we were affected. We could only remember you as ‘Everlasting,’ but we were unable to utter your true name.

“We tried calling your name in sequence, but every time we called one name, we would forget the previous name we’d called, trapping us in an endless loop. What gave us slight solace was that we confirmed you would be resurrected in the future based on conversations through the time passageway.

“Lianyi’s feelings for you run deeper than her feelings for me. I didn’t wish for her to be limited by lifespan and pass away without seeing you again. That’s why I arranged this meeting between you. Even if she has forgotten you, I’m sure she’ll still be overjoyed upon seeing you revived.

“To let you find Lianyi, I created this secret domain and hid Lianyi on the fourth level. This secret domain should be considered an ancient secret domain by future generations of cultivators—or simply called an ancient domain. That doesn’t matter. In any case, this secret domain holds immense value for future cultivators and will be very famous. You’re someone who likes to join in the excitement, so you’re bound to come here. Besides, setting up this secret domain will also allow me to provide some fortuitous opportunities for our demon race. freewebnovel.com

“Through the time channel conversations, we learned that you are in a soul state and that there is a little Golden Core cultivator beside you. You’ve likely been residing in his mental space all this time. This secret domain can attract both you and him.

“The first level’s trial tests basic martial prowess. With you around, the little Golden Core cultivator shouldn’t have any problem passing.

“The second level’s trial is more complicated. With your sharp intuition, you can make the correct choices. This trial shouldn’t be difficult for you either.

“The third level intends to distinguish you from the little demon geniuses. Only you can answer the questions on this level.

“By the way, I am currently fighting it out with your killer through various means. I’m not sure where I’ll be when you resurrect, so I won’t leave a location for you and spare you the unnecessary trouble. If you are revived, the world is only so big—we will eventually meet.

“Well then, until we meet again. Goodbye.”

Chapter 597: Meeting for the First Time

As the Qilin Immortal’s phantom image vanished, the patterns on the recording stone faded. It remained unresponsive no matter how much spirit energy was channeled into it. The recording stone had become useless.

The whole place was draped in silence.

Jiang Lianyi opened her arms and gently embraced the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, patting her back softly. “Don’t cry. I believe you. Can you tell me what I was like in your memories?”

Lu Yang’s inability to touch the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was due to the insufficient cultivation of his soul. In Jiang Lianyi’s case, it was effortless.

“Mmm!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded vigorously, forcing her tears back.

Jiang Lianyi got out of bed and invited the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Lu Yang to sit at the stone table, where she began brewing tea.

The curled golden tea leaves unfurled in the cup. Countless laws evolved in the cup before finally dissolving.

This was for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

If Lu Yang were to take a sip, he feared he would be melted on the spot by the laws of the tea leaves.

Jiang Lianyi personally poured tea for Lu Yang. He hurriedly stood up to thank her, feeling overwhelmed by the honor.

Lu Yang drank a different type of tea. He didn’t know its name, but it was certainly good tea. The tea’s fragrance lingered at the tip of his nose, and his cultivation technique automatically began circulating.

“You and I first got to know each other because of a misunderstanding...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recounted in detail the story of how she and Jiang Lianyi met and became friends, clearly describing the specifics of teaching her culinary skills and the Play-Dead Technique.

“Back then, you and Ao Ling cried and begged to become my disciples, but I didn’t agree. Not long after, you two faced the Qilin Immortal in battle. Unable to overcome his Survival of the Fittest Incipient Dao Fruit, you lost the qualification for immortal ascension.”

She continued narrating Jiang Lianyi’s wedding with the Qilin Immortal, their life after marriage, and her attending gatherings of the Five Immortals and conversing joyfully...

Jiang Lianyi remained absorbed in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s vivid portrayals, unable to free herself for a long time.

“Finally, I lost consciousness. When I woke up again, I met Lu Yang.” By the end, even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy herself laughed.

“Why are you crying?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy noticed Jiang Lianyi sitting there in a daze with vacant eyes, allowing tears to stream down her cheeks.

“Ah? Ah.” Only after the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s reminder did Jiang Lianyi seem to have woken from a dream. Snapping back to her senses, she wiped her tears while apologizing, forcing a smile. “I’m sorry for letting you see me make a fool of myself. I don’t know why, but the tears just won’t stop.”

Is it because the Everlasting Immortal Fairy is pitiful, waking to find her old friends suddenly gone and the world having completely forgotten her? Or is it because she is so pitiable, yet completely unaware and still living without a care?

Or is there some other reason?

Jiang Lianyi didn’t know.

She wiped her tears dry and inhaled two deep breaths to calm herself, regaining her dignified and graceful demeanor. “The Jiang Lianyi in your memories is very similar to me. The details you describe also don’t seem fabricated. But I really don’t remember these events you spoke of. Without personal experience, I can’t truly empathize.

“A voice deep in my heart keeps telling me to believe you, saying I must must must trust you. My husband said the same. I choose to believe you. Unfortunately, I have no impression of those experiences. I am not the Phoenix Tribe’s prodigy from your memories, nor can I pretend to be.

“So...”

Jiang Lianyi stood up and extended her hand with a smile.

“Can we get to know each other again? I’m Jiang Lianyi.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stood up and shook her hand, also smiling.

“I’m Huang Doudou.”

The two shook hands, smiling at each other as if they were meeting for the first time, yet also as if they had known each other for a long time.

Jiang Lianyi then walked over to Lu Yang, startling him. He didn’t know what this ancient ancestor intended to do.

Jiang Lianyi said solemnly, “Thank you for resurrecting Everlasting-jiejie. On behalf of Little Ling and my husband, I thank you!” She bowed deeply, frightening Lu Yang so much that he hastily stood up and told her he couldn’t accept it, wanting to help her up.

But Jiang Lianyi was an almighty half-immortal. How could Lu Yang possibly budge her? Despite exerting all his strength, he couldn’t even make the hem of her clothes flutter. He could only watch helplessly, his calves trembling as Jiang Lianyi bowed.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked, “Can you share what happened before you performed the Play-Dead Technique?”

“Of course.”

The three sat down, and Jiang Lianyi began recalling the past.

“At the time, I was cultivating when suddenly a wave of dizziness hit me. It felt like I had forgotten something very important, leaving a hollow sensation in my heart. But upon closer recollection, I couldn’t remember what exactly I had forgotten.

“My husband was guarding my cultivation when his expression changed drastically. His visage distorted with extreme fury, and his pupils blazed with rage. I had never seen him that angry before.

“Revealing his Qilin true form, my husband fully released his oppressive pressure. The entire galaxy shook. I was closest and felt it most deeply, and even I couldn’t withstand it. This oppressive pressure was so powerful that it made my heart palpitate.

“My husband flew out of the cave abode, heading north. He crossed countless galaxies and probably stopped in the region of the North Star. Only then did I notice that it wasn’t just my husband—Heaven Mandate, Nine-Layers, and Epoch also displayed the same wrath as my husband, if not greater.

“The four immortals acted simultaneously. Their auras could be sensed throughout the entire universe. That kind of burning rage could make even my heart quiver. It seemed capable of incinerating everything.

“Although the four of them often sparred and exchanged moves, and there were times when real fire was ignited, none of their fights had been like this one.

“I also have no idea who their opponent was. I only remember the battle lasted seven days and seven nights straight without a decisive outcome. The level of that battle was too high, beyond my scope of understanding. Please forgive me for being unable to describe it in detail.

“I don’t know if the opponent vanished or for some other reason, but in the end, the four of them used the power of their Dao Fruits to refine all the stars in the sky into six continents, forming a cube that sealed all living beings, including themselves.

“My husband returned severely wounded. He told me the situation was perplexing and instructed me to immediately perform the Play-Dead Technique and leave the rest to him. Seeing my husband’s grave visage, I didn’t doubt him. I used the Play-Dead Technique and fell into a death-like slumber.

“When I woke up again, I met you two.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded. “In other words, this secret domain wasn’t created by you but the Qilin Immortal?”

Jiang Lianyi replied, “At the very least, I have no impression of this secret domain. I don’t know anything about a first or second level.”

“What do you plan to do next? Do you want to leave this place with us?”

“Before that, may I ask how long I have been asleep?”

“Roughly three hundred thousand years. Your Phoenix Tribe is now the number one major tribe in the Demon Region, and they revere you as their ancient ancestor. There are many legends about you in the outside world.”

“I actually slept for that long?” Jiang Lianyi was shocked. I thought it wouldn’t have been more than a hundred thousand years. After so long, how has the cultivation world changed?

“Then let’s go out and take a look.” Jiang Lianyi developed a strong interest in the outside world. “By the way, there’s one more thing I was embarrassed to mention earlier.” She thought about it and felt that bottling it inside her heart felt uncomfortable.

“Feel free to speak.”

“Can you wear something more formal?” Jiang Lianyi sized up the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. This style of dressing is too coarse.

“No.”

“Oh.”

Chapter 598: Seven-Star Sword Set

“City Lord, these are the official documents submitted from below.” A subordinate carried a stack of official documents and placed them on the city lord’s desk, dividing them into two piles.

The city lord was a female cultivator with a rare appearance. No one dared to question this city lord, nor did they dare to comment on her looks. To serve as city lord in a city with a majority of male cultivators spoke volumes about her methods and cultivation level.

“It’s been three days already. Why hasn’t he come back down yet?” Luo Hong sat in the main hall of the City Lord Estate on the third level. She had given herself the identity of city lord.

After handling the city’s affairs, she looked up at the sky as usual, toward the location of the fourth level.

Suddenly, a gap appeared in the sky. Three figures emerged from the gap and appeared in the main hall of the City Lord Estate in a flash.

“Senior Luo Hong, we meet again,” Lu Yang greeted with a smile.

Luo Hong, “...”

I remember you went up alone. Why are there three people now?

Moreover, Luo Hong felt the two individuals behind Lu Yang were unfathomable, possessing terrifying strength. As the spirit of the secret domain, Luo Hong could mobilize all its power. This place was filled with treasures, yet not a single demon prodigy who had grown into a mighty expert had dared to force their way in, a testament to how fearsome Luo Hong was.

Even so, she still felt she was no match for the two figures behind Lu Yang.

In fact, she even felt a sense of reverence and fear toward the female cultivator in red.

“Luo Hong pays respects to the Mistress!” Luo Hong immediately knelt and kowtowed to Jiang Lianyi.

“Wait a moment. Who are you?” Jiang Lianyi shifted a step to the side, unwilling to accept someone kneeling to her for no reason.

“I am the spirit of this secret domain, created by Master.”

“Who is your master?”

“Shi He. Master told me to call him ‘Qilin Immortal.’” Shi He was the Qilin Immortal’s name.

Luo Hong continued, “My master created this secret domain. He said if anyone answered all the questions on the third level correctly, they should be allowed to enter the fourth level, where the Mistress stays. Once the Mistress appears, everything in the secret domain, including me, belongs to her.”

A complex immortal seal appeared on Luo Hong’s brow. She offered the seal with both hands and deferentially presented it to Jiang Lianyi.

“It is indeed the mark left by my husband.” Jiang Lianyi accepted the seal. This was the secret domain’s seal. Possessing it granted control over everything in the secret domain.

In an instant, Jiang Lianyi could sense the structure of the secret domain. With a single thought, she could make Luo Hong do anything, and the secret domain’s treasury could be opened at will.

Jiang Lianyi casually swiped her hand across the air, slicing open a spatial rift with countless treasures piled up like a mountain. Even great demons would go green with envy at these treasures, but they were nothing special in Jiang Lianyi’s eyes. freewebnovel.com

“Do you need these?” Jiang Lianyi turned to ask Lu Yang. If he wanted them, she could give him all these treasures.

Lu Yang was somewhat conflicted. It’s true that these treasures are valuable, but I’m not short on money, nor do I need spirit stones. As for magical treasures, probably none are more valuable than the Qingfeng Sword. There are also cultivation insights and techniques, but with the scripture library and Big Senior Sister around, I have no need to study the experiences left by mighty demon experts.

“I heard some demon prodigies obtained an immortal grass here that allows one to leap a major cultivation realm after consumption, and with no side effects at that?”

Jiang Lianyi reached out, traversing space. She plucked a spirit grass with seven leaves and specks of starlight from the second level. “You’re referring to the Seven-Star Moon-Chasing Grass. Its growth conditions are extremely strict. It can indeed elevate one’s cultivation by a major realm. For example, if you are at the Advanced Golden Core Stage, you can rise to the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage. But calling it an immortal grass is overestimating it. After consuming it, one can no longer break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.”

“Forget it then.” Lu Yang believed cultivation should progress steadily in incremental steps; there was no need to rush.

Jiang Lianyi replanted the Seven-Star Moon-Chasing Grass.

“Can I pick a few swords? To form a sword array,” Lu Yang suddenly said.

“Sure.”

With a hook of Jiang Lianyi’s finger, seven precious swords of different styles floated out from the treasure pile, emitting a cold gleam. “These seven swords are all yours.”

All the swords in the Creation Ancient Domain were growth-type magical treasures. The names of the swords were engraved on their hilts: Tianshu (Dubhe), Tianxuan (Merak), Tianji (Phecda)...

Luo Hong was most familiar with these treasures and introduced them. “These names correspond to the Big Dipper (Seven Stars) in ancient times. This set of swords is called the Seven-Star Sword Set.”

Above each sword hovered the number “two.”

“Good stuff.” Lu Yang was a sword cultivator after all. Obtaining seven different precious words made him grin from ear to ear.

“How do I make it acknowledge a master? By dripping blood on it?”

Luo Hong replied solemnly, “It’s not that simple. These seven swords all have a spiritual nature. To subdue them, one must nurture them with their body, heart, and blood. It’s a lengthy process, taking anywhere from a month to a year.”

The Seven-Star Sword Set emitted continuous sword cries, confirming Luo Hong’s words.

Sword cultivators were proud, and their precious swords also had their own pride. Not just anyone could use them freely. From the moment a sword was born, three usage rules were established: none but peerless sword cultivators; none but peerless geniuses; none but those who moved them with sincerity.

Although the Seven-Star Swords hadn’t reached the point of developing intelligence, they possessed spirit.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stepped forward and vigorously tapped whichever sword was humming the loudest. Once the Seven-Star Sword Set fell silent, she pointed at Lu Yang and stated, “You’ll follow him from now on! Understand?”

The Seven-Star Swords emitted humming sounds, trembling like leaves.

One shouldn’t mistake her actions for casual taps—they were attacks directly targeting their spiritual nature. If the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wished, mere taps could erase their spiritual nature.

The swords floated over to Lu Yang, nuzzling against him with intimate attitudes.

Lu Yang hurriedly moved away. A fluffy little rabbit nuzzling me is fine, but seven swords? Are you trying to slice me to death?

Lu Yang ran ahead, the Seven-Star Sword Set relentlessly chasing him behind. Finally, Lu Yang stored them away using his identity jade tablet, and only then did they settle down.

Jiang Lianyi said to Luo Hong, “Continue your previous duties in the secret domain. Everything remains as before.”

“Yes!”

“Also, do not reveal anything about my or Everlasting-jiejie’s matters.”

“As you command!”

When they were descending from the fourth level, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had told Jiang Lianyi not to speak of her existence outside, lest they alert the enemy.

Jiang Lianyi said, “Let’s go. It’s a good chance to see what the cultivation world is like now.”

Three hundred thousand years have passed. I’m afraid old friends are gone; even if things are the same, the people are no longer the same.

“Speaking of old friends, there is one recently,” Lu Yang remarked, stroking his chin. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had already returned to his mental space.

“Who?”

“The ancient Dijiang. He has been slumbering from ancient times until now. After waking, he planned to unify the Demon Region and establish a demon kingdom. I reckon we’ll be just in time for his kingdom-founding ceremony after we get out of here.”

Jiang Lianyi was dazed for a moment before realizing who Lu Yang meant by the ancient Dijiang. This is really a case of how things are the same, but the people are no longer the same. “He can establish a demon kingdom? Has he grown capable?”

“There’s one more matter I’d like to seek your opinion on,” Lu Yang said.

“You are the one who resurrected Everlasting-jiejie. There’s no need to be so formal with me. Speak your mind.”

“Have you heard of the Heavenly Court?”

Chapter 599: Drawing Enmity

At the Creation Ancient Domain’s exit, the two opposing sides faced each other, prepared for confrontation.

“Chieftain Jiang, let me advise you—surrendering now is the wisest move. Your Phoenix Tribe has gone too far,” the Jiuying Tribe Chieftain threatened icily, his gaze resembling a venomous viper. “Not only did your Phoenix Tribe send three people in this time, but two of them also received rewards on the third level, and one person still hasn’t emerged!” freewebnovel.com

The demon elders present had all entered the Creation Ancient Domain Before and knew it was divided into three levels. Only by passing the first level could one obtain the most basic reward.

The Demon Alliance prodigies hadn’t even passed the first level and were eliminated.

Ao Yue and the others were defeated at the second level, receiving only the most basic reward.

Meng Jingzhou, Jiang Shishi, and Su Lian’er received the rewards from the third level.

If that was all, it would have been fine. Every generation had demon prodigies who obtained rewards on the third level.

The problem was that someone hadn’t left the secret domain! This was an unprecedented situation!

The Creation Ancient Domain was mysterious and profound. The third-level rewards were bountiful enough to make even Fusion cultivators’ eyes go green with envy. If someone stayed longer in the secret domain, what kind of rewards would they acquire?!

The Jiuying Tribe was suspected of being the financial backer of the Diabolic Sound Heavenly Maiden. The Jiuying Tribe’s young lord had also sabotaged the Demon Alliance prodigies in the ancient domain. Therefore, the Jiuying Tribe was resented by various major demon tribes, and they urgently needed to divert the other demons’ attention.

And the Phoenix Tribe was the perfect target!

To this end, the Jiuying Tribe even summoned their chieftain to exert pressure.

“If your Phoenix Tribe is willing to pledge allegiance to the Demon Kingdom, we can let bygones be bygones and forget this matter!” The Jiuying Tribe Chieftain’s gaze was gloomy, revealing the true purpose of this trip.

The Phoenix Tribe was already within the scope of tribes the Demon Alliance intended to suppress and rope in. Unfortunately, the Phoenix Tribe’s foundation ran too deep, so the ancient Dijiang didn’t dare to act rashly.

This is the perfect opportunity to rely on the Demon Alliance to exert pressure on the Phoenix Tribe and rope them in!

This would be a great meritorious achievement!

“Let bygones be bygones? What an arrogant tone!” The Phoenix Tribe Chieftain sneered several times. The Jiuying Tribe’s intentions are glaringly obvious.

The Phoenix Tribe Chieftain was called Jiang Xi, a graceful and beautiful woman draped in phoenix robes. She had a noble and extraordinary demeanor, bearing some resemblance to Jiang Shishi.

Phoenixes were a matriarchal race, with female powerhouses being the majority. By tradition, the chieftain was always a woman.

“Your tribe’s geniuses’ skills were inferior, yet you blame my Phoenix Tribe?”

Without Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s assistance in the first trial and the inspiration from their actions, how could Jiang Shishi have passed the second level and obtained the Phoenix Visualization Drawing?

This was a supreme treasure left by the ancient ancestor. Jiang Shishi was already exceptionally talented. With the aid of this visualization treasure, her reaching the Transcendent Tribulation Stage was set in stone.

For this reason alone, their Phoenix Tribe was determined to protect Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou!

The original conflict was the Jiuying Tribe elder uniting with the Demon Alliance to exert pressure on the Phoenix Tribe. The Phoenix Tribe had the Dragon Tribe as an ally and multiple races who had received Lu Yang’s assistance in the secret domain, so they didn’t fear the Demon Alliance.

Seeing this, the Jiuying Tribe called over their chieftain.

Not to be outdone, the Phoenix Tribe also called over their chieftain.

As things unfolded, the chieftains of the various major races had all arrived, each lending their presence to support their own races.

“What’s going on with Little Junior Brother? It’s been three days, and he still hasn’t come out?” Gan Tian quietly asked Meng Jingzhou. If something were to happen to Little Junior Brother in the secret domain, I’d feel guilty for life.

Meng Jingzhou revealed a helpless smile. “Senior Sister, putting aside the secret domain’s rule of not divulging what happens inside, whereby I can’t say anything, even if I could say anything, I genuinely have no idea what that grandson Lu Yang is doing in there.

“You need not worry about him, Senior Sister. Based on my understanding of him, he should be safe inside the secret domain. He might even be more comfortable than we are out here.”

Meng Jingzhou knew best what trump cards Lu Yang had. Internally, he has an ancient immortal protecting him, and externally, he has the Animal Form Fist to summon Big Senior Sister. With both internal and external safeguards, what could possibly go wrong?

“Refusing a toast only to be forced to drink a forfeit—you were given the easy way out, yet you insist on choosing the hard way out!” The Jiuying Tribe Chieftain’s visage distorted with viciousness.

Most of the demon tribes have already joined the Demon Kingdom. The ancient Dijiang’s unification of the Demon Region is already a foregone conclusion. The Dragon and Phoenix tribes can’t see the situation clearly and dare to resist stubbornly. I had kindly advised them to submit to the Demon kingdom early, and this is how I was treated!

They truly don’t know how the character for “death” is written!

“Haha, it’s so lively here?”

A hearty laugh echoed from the sky. Factions from outside the Demon Region had arrived!

“Isn’t this the Nine-Headed Snake? I trapped you in a secret domain for five years, remember? It’s been over a thousand years since we last met, right?

“You, from the Taowu Tribe, what was your name again? Still remember me? I’d even beat you up before!”

Finding the voice familiar, Meng Jingzhou looked up. It was his shifu.

Third Elder sat on a cloud, cheerfully recounting the embarrassing stories of the Jiuying Tribe Chieftain and other demons.

First Elder, Fourth Elder, Fifth Elder, and Seventh Elder were also present. Over half of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s elders had arrived at the Creation Ancient Domain.

“Finally here.” Gan Tian heaved a sigh of relief. Seeing the situation escalating, she had contacted Yun Zhi to consult her on what should be done.

Yun Zhi’s reply was simple: I’ll send people to divert attention.

Coincidentally, the Demon Kingdom’s founding was imminent. Major factions from the cultivation world were sending representatives, and the Dao-Seeking Sect was no exception. Thus, Yun Zhi had the elders attending the founding ceremony assist Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“They’re from the Dao-Seeking Sect!” Upon seeing these familiar faces, the Jiuying Tribe Chieftain was furious, his face contorted. With a bang, he transformed into his Jiuying true form—a body composed of nine heaven-devouring pythons.

The events of a thousand years ago were still fresh in his memory. If not for these fellows, how could I have been trapped in a secret domain for five long years?! I nearly held up my cultivation!

The Taowu Tribe Chieftain was equally enraged. A thousand years ago, I was full of spirit and ambition, a genius celebrated by the entire Taowu Tribe. At the height of my fame, these fellows from the Dao-Seeking Sect privately challenged me to a one-on-one fight.

If they had used underhanded methods to win, that would have been fine. Yet it was a fair fight that time. My skills were inferior, and I lost to the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Old Three in a contest of physical strength and power!

He viewed this as a great humiliation and hadn’t told anyone. This incident made me despondent for a long time. Now that the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Old Three has dredged this up and disclosed it to the public, how could I leave this lying down?!

It wasn’t just these two races. Even the usually good-tempered Jade Rabbit Tribe showed hostility upon seeing the Dao-Seeking Sect’s elders.

“It’s the Dao-Seeking Sect! Everyone, attack together!”

With the Dao-Seeking Sect airing their embarrassing stories one by one, the demons temporarily forgot about decorum and the Demon Alliance. They just wanted to swarm the Dao-Seeking Sect and capture them!

The great demons revealed their true forms one after another. For a moment, it was a scene of demons running wild, with demon energy soaring to the heavens.

Seeing their objective achieved, First Elder quickly gathered everyone and fled.

“Stop right there if you dare!” The Jiuying Tribe Chieftain chased after them desperately.

But how could First Elder listen to his nonsense? He rode the clouds and mist, escaping at top speed!

The bustling Creation Ancient Domain instantly became empty, leaving only Gan Tian and Meng Jingzhou staring at each other.

Even the Phoenix Tribe had given chase. Although they held no deep grudge against the Dao-Seeking Sect, not chasing them would make it seem like they didn’t fit in.

The corners of Meng Jingzhou’s mouth twitched. Fortunately, I had kept a low profile in the Demon Region and hadn’t exposed my identity as a Dao-Seeking Sect disciple. If I had, it would have been disastrous!

“Haha, I’m out!”

The exit of the Creation Ancient Domain opened. Lu Yang hopped out, expecting a welcome from the crowd.

“Where’s everyone?”

Chapter 600: Where is the Ancient Dijiang? I’ll Go Settle Accounts with Him

This differed drastically from Lu Yang’s expectations.

I had set a record in the ancient domain and reached the fourth level. Logically speaking, many demons should be waiting at the exit to corner me, demanding the rewards I obtained in the ancient domain.

Especially the Jiuying Tribe. I targeted Qin Feng so much inside the ancient domain. Shouldn’t the Jiuying Tribe be the main force attacking me outside?

First, Qin Feng would challenge me one-on-one, citing that the strong should be revered. Then, after Qin Feng’s defeat, the Jiuying Tribe elder would intervene, bullying the weak with his power.

At that point, the Phoenix Tribe would step forward to support me, blocking the Jiuying Tribe elder’s attack.

Considering the Jiuying Tribe’s ability to fan the flames, the Demon Alliance would side with them, saying things like “Your virtue doesn’t match your position—a junior like you has no right to obtain important treasures in the ancient domain,” “Hand them over quickly, and we might spare your life,” or “How dare you bully the members of our Demon Alliance? You will die today!”

The Phoenix Tribe would be no match for the Demon Alliance, and I would fall into crisis.

At this point, Senior Jiang Lianyi would make her entrance, backing me up. With a glare from her phoenix eyes, she would release her half-immortal oppressive pressure and declare, “Let’s see who dares touch him!” Then, she would go on a rampage and intimidate everyone.

How satisfying that would be!

But why are only Old Meng and Third Senior Sister at the exit?

Seeing that the situation outside was different from Lu Yang’s plan, Jiang Lianyi didn’t wait for his signal and stepped out of the ancient domain. She wore a dazzling, crimson long dress. With her tall stature and aloof expression, she instilled reverence and awe in people’s hearts.

Meng Jingzhou was stunned. Why is there an extra person? Why hadn’t I seen this person in the secret domain?

Gan Tian’s reaction was even stronger, her voice quivering. “Y-you are the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor?” freewebnovel.com

The Phoenix Tribe had portraits of their old ancestor inside their tribe, and Gan Tian had seen them before. The person Little Junior Brother brought out looks exactly like she has stepped out of the ancient paintings—they look exactly the same! No, she’s even more lifelike than the image in the paintings.

Gan Tian was passionate about archaeology. With a living ancient person appearing before her, especially the renowned Phoenix Ancient Ancestor surrounded by countless legends, how could she not be excited?

Soon after, Gan Tian calmed down. Wait, no matter how lucky Little Junior Brother is, he couldn’t possibly have found the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor. This must be an incarnation or clone left by the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor.

“I am Jiang Lianyi.” The citizens on the third level spoke in the modern tongue, and Jiang Lianyi had learned it with a sweep of her spiritual consciousness.

Hearing Jiang Lianyi’s self-introduction, Gan Tian’s heart missed a beat. It really is the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor from the legends?!

Meng Jingzhou stared at Jiang Lianyi and Lu Yang as if he had seen a ghost, his face full of disbelief. What’s going on with you, kid? How did a trip to the ancient domain result in you summoning the Phoenix Tribe’s old ancestor?

Gan Tian was emotional as she asked, “Legends say you had perished. Have you undergone nirvana rebirth and returned?”

Jiang Lianyi, “...”

The story of nirvana rebirth has been passed down until now? Would answering that I used the Play-Dead Technique to feign death until now tarnish my image?

She replied placidly, “Do not spread this matter. Only you three know of my resurrection.”

The three nodded repeatedly.

“By the way, where are the Phoenix Tribe and the other races?”

Lu Yang thought, Since I’ve also awakened the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor, along with my connection to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, there shouldn’t be a problem with me becoming the Phoenix Tribe’s second ancestor, right?

Gan Tian recounted everything that had transpired from when Lu Yang entered the ancient domain to when he emerged from it.

Jiang Lianyi furrowed her brow slightly, somewhat displeased. “Such audacity from Zhu Tian! To think he tried to use his Incipient Dao Fruit to control my Phoenix Tribe! Does he think I’m not around?”

Zhu Tian was the name of the ancient Dijiang. Dijiang were fully red, and they used “Zhu” as their surname.

As a fellow possessor of the Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit, Jiang Lianyi knew what it meant to have a master-servant mark planted by such an Incipient Dao Fruit. It represented absolute control of the strong over the weak; even life and death were the difference of a mere thought.

In ancient times, she hadn’t even done such a thing. She never expected that Zhu Tian would have grown ambitious and emboldened in an era without immortals, plotting to not only unify the demon race but also prepare to control the Phoenix Tribe. If the Phoenix Tribe’s foundation and heritage weren’t as deep, they would likely have been controlled long ago.

“Where is Zhu Tian? I’ll go find him!” She had a fiery temperament to begin with. Zhu Tian is practically riding on the Phoenix Tribe’s head! Does he really think I’m dead?!

Startled, Lu Yang secretly asked in his mental space, “Immortal Fairy, didn’t you say those who awaken from slumber have greatly diminished strength and require a long time to recover? Senior Jiang just woke up. Can she defeat the ancient Dijiang?”

“You must be joking. Don’t mix my Play-Dead Technique with those miscellaneous methods! Once my Play-Dead Technique is cast, one’s vitality is completely locked within the body. Lianyi’s strength now is the same as in the ancient era—she’s at her peak condition!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy placed her hands on her hips, extremely proud of her Play-Dead Technique.

Ascertaining that Jiang Lianyi’s strength hadn’t dwindled, Lu Yang became even more respectful and hurriedly advised, “Senior, please don’t be overly angry over this matter and harm your body. Senior Zhu Tian’s whereabouts are elusive, but the kingdom-founding ceremony is about to be held. As the ruler, Senior Zhu Tian will definitely attend. We can find him there.”

“That also works.”

Lu Yang kindly suggested, “There’s one more thing. This attire of yours is too ostentatious. I’m afraid someone would recognize you even before you attend the ceremony. If Senior Zhu Tian learns of your arrival, he might hide. Would you like to consider a simple disguise?”

Setting Jiang Lianyi’s identity aside, just her appearance—ranked among the top three of the Ten Ancient Beauties—would attract countless gazes wherever she went, making her the center of attention. On top of that, the Phoenix Tribe had portraits of Jiang Lianyi. It would be strange if chaos didn’t break out.

Jiang Lianyi thought it made sense. She took out a black cloak from her storage ring and draped it over herself with practiced ease, seeming to have done this action numerous times.

“Hmm? Why did I do that subconsciously?” Jiang Lianyi froze, somewhat baffled. Given my personality, I never act secretively. I shouldn’t have worn cloaks often. This doesn’t make sense.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was not at all surprised and transmitted an auditory message to Jiang Lianyi. “I often took you and Little Ling to auctions, where we pretended to be harmless, playing the pig to eat the tiger. Back then, all three of us wore cloaks.”

Gan Tian took out her beast hide, invited Jiang Lianyi to sit on it, and set off for the Dijiang Tribe with the other three.

On the beast hide, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was feeling bored when she suddenly remembered something. “Isn’t there something off about the way you and Lianyi address each other?

“Lianyi calls me jiejie.

“Lu Yang, you call her senior.

“Lianyi calls you Lu Yang.”

“What’s the problem with that?” Lu Yang didn’t see an issue. What else should I call her? Lianyi-jiejie?

“No no, the seniority is messed up. Although I didn’t formally accept Lianyi as a disciple, we had a master-disciple relationship in practice. Lu Yang, as the second-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage and my disciple, your status should be higher than Lianyi’s based on sect affiliation.”

“So...?”

“So, you are Lianyi’s Big Senior Brother!”

Jiang Lianyi nodded. “I’ll listen to Everlasting-jiejie. What about you, Big Senior Brother?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, please don’t speak nonsense. I’m afraid the Qilin Immortal might suddenly appear behind me.

And Senior Lianyi, please don’t mess around. My fate profile is shallow; I can’t bear such a form of address.

Chapter 601: New Member of the Heavenly Court Creed

Gan Tian piloted the beast hide for five days before finally arriving at the site of the Demon Kingdom’s founding ceremony.

Originally, this area was a continuous mountain range. Through the efforts of the Demon Alliance, it had been transformed into a plain. A lofty imperial city had risen from the ground, standing firm on the plain.

A city molded from metal was especially striking in the savage and untamed Demon Region. Great peaks towered, surrounded by mountains. The magnificent metal city standing within the encirclement of these peaks was particularly eye-catching. It was fully pitch-black, oppressive, and suffocating, exuding an air of intimidation.

With the kingdom-founding ceremony approaching, all factions with Fusion cultivators had been invited. Most of these forces had arrived at the metal city early. Along with the Demon Alliance members stationed here, the metal city was bustling with activity.

Great Xia, the East Sea, the Demon Kingdom, and various rogue cultivators had gathered here. Factions from across the cultivation world had come to witness this event.

After organizing the Dao-Seeking Sect’s anniversary celebration, Lu Yang had become familiar with all the major sects in Great Xia. However, many unfamiliar major factions had arrived again this time.

After all, the Demon Region had been chaotic for three hundred thousand years. With the sudden announcement of founding a nation, everyone wanted to bear witness to this historic moment.

The founder was even more extraordinary. It was the ancient Dijiang, a half-immortal who had lived from antiquity to the present! Anyone who had studied ancient history knew of his fearsome reputation!

“Demon City?”

Suspended above the city gate were two large characters—Demon City.

Upon seeing these two characters, a hazy and boundless energy surged forth, allowing one to inhale the aged, dusty smell of history.

“Little Lu, Little Meng, over here, over here.” As Lu Yang’s group landed at the city gate, they heard First Elder’s auditory message.

“Look to your left.”

The two turned their heads and saw First Elder and Third Elder squatting by the roadside.

First Elder and Third Elder were quite conspicuous. The demons passing by glared at them fiercely, but bound by the rules of the Demon City, they couldn’t attack. They could only enter the city indignantly.

With the kingdom-founding ceremony just around the corner, starting a fight near the Demon City would be a slap to the Dijiang Tribe. Even those with grudges against the Dao-Seeking Sect didn’t dare to seek revenge or cause trouble at this time.

For this reason, First Elder and Third Elder dared to show their true faces.

The Demon City had four gates. Fourth Elder, Fifth Elder, and Seventh Elder were guarding the other three. Upon learning that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were at the east gate, the three elders convened here.

“Elders, you managed to escape?” Meng Jingzhou remembered that the demons chasing the five elders were so angry that they almost burned their essence blood. They could still escape under such circumstances?

First Elder stroked his beard and laughed heartily. “Naturally, it’s because the five of us have made ample preparations that we dared to come to the Demon Region. If they want to catch up to us, they should cultivate to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage first!”

“It’s been a long while, elders,” Gan Tian greeted politely.

“Gan Tian, it’s been about a hundred years since we last met. It seems you’ve gained a lot in the Demon Region. Your cultivation is probably the highest among your peers, already at the Apex Void Refinement Stage. You’ll soon catch up to Little Dai.” First Elder chuckled. This lass Gan Tian is diligent and inquisitive, often making our hearts blossom with joy during her time at the Dao-Seeking Sect—the complete opposite of the infuriating Ye Zijin.

Both are disciples of the Taciturn Daoist Priest, so why is the difference so big?

“Apex Void Refinement Stage?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were astonished. They had always assumed Gan Tian was at the Fusion Stage. Isn’t it said that cultivation at the Void Refinement Stage fluctuates greatly? Why isn’t it reflected in Third Senior Sister?

“Of course, it’s the Apex Void Refinement Stage,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said lazily. “Didn’t you notice this little lass never acted personally but used magical treasures instead?”

With her reminder, those memories suddenly struck Lu Yang. Throughout our journey, Third Senior Sister had either used the guqin, beast hide, or Invisibility Talismans. I’ve never seen her using spells or similar methods.

“This little lass seizes the opportunity when her cultivation fluctuates to the Fusion Stage, whereby she’ll inject spirit power into her magical treasures, storing them in advance. When her cultivation drops, she can still use the magical treasures normally.”

Lu Yang remembered the time he and Meng Jingzhou participated in the sect’s entrance examinations. Old Meng had brought several magical treasures stored with spirit energy in advance, all brought from home.

“When you reach the Void Refinement Stage, you can try this method to protect yourself,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy told him.

Even so, Lu Yang thought Gan Tian was quite bold. Cultivators at the Void Refinement Stage typically choose to go into seclusion, live in isolation, become mortal, take the imperial examinations to become officials, or even sit in jail—in short, whatever is safest.

Who’s like Third Senior Sister, bouncing around actively in the dangerous Demon Region, with spare energy to take the two of us into tombs for archaeology?

Lu Yang had learned some things about the Void Refinement Stage. He heard the Taciturn Daoist Priest frequently spent his weak phase in jail. Among the elders, a few stayed in the sect obediently. As for the senior disciples, many chose to pose as mortals, living and eating with them, only revealing their cultivation to show off in times of danger. The methods varied.

“Immortal Fairy, how did you spend your Void Refinement Stage?” Lu Yang was curious. Given her personality, it’s hard to imagine her going into seclusion or living in isolation. In the chaotic ancient era, sitting in jail or pretending to be a mortal probably wouldn’t have worked.

“Simple. I created clones. My cultivation fluctuated, and so did my clone’s cultivation. From a probability standpoint, my clones and I couldn’t all simultaneously be at a low point; at least one would be at a higher cultivation.”

Lu Yang contemplated it thoroughly. “What if you and your clones all hit a low point at the same time?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy found Lu Yang’s question stupid and answered matter-of-factly. “Create more clones, of course.”

“...Makes sense.”

“And this is...” First Elder had long noticed the figure in a black cloak behind Lu Yang. They had been catching up, so First Elder hadn’t had time to ask about the figure’s origin.

A cold and crisp voice came from under the black cloak, answering without the slightest hesitation, “Lu Yang is my Big Senior...”

Having quick eyes and a sharp tongue, Lu Yang hurriedly said, “This is a new member of our Heavenly Court Creed.”

The concept of the Heavenly Court had been fabricated by the Five Ancient Immortals to deceive later generations. Jiang Lianyi had naturally heard of this term. Furthermore, with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy serving as the ruler of the Heavenly Court, Jiang Lianyi readily agreed when Lu Yang invited her to join the Heavenly Court Creed.

As for the matter of addressing him as “senior brother,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy insisted that Lu Yang was an inner disciple while Jiang Lianyi was an unofficial disciple, thereby making Lu Yang her senior brother; Jiang Lianyi insisted on calling Lu Yang her senior brother; Lu Yang insisted that Jiang Lianyi was considered his senior.

It could only be said that each of them had their own insistence and perseverance.

“A new member?” Seventh Elder was delighted. He trusted Lu Yang’s judgement. Anyone he brings into the Heavenly Court Creed is definitely trustworthy. He paced with his hands behind his back, speaking like an old sage. “This old man joined the Heavenly Court Creed earlier than you and is counted as your senior. If you encounter anything you don’t understand, feel free to ask this old man. The same goes for cultivation matters. This old man has quite some insights into this regard.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Gan Tian, “...”

“Alright.”
